### `[THE LARGEST CURATED ZSH COMPLETION CORPUS IN EXISTENCE // 28,491 FILES]`

> *"Every CLI you've heard of, completed. Plus several you haven't."*

> _"The shell is the street. The completions are the chrome."_

### [`strykelang`](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/strykelang) &middot; [`zshrs`](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zshrs) · [`MenkeTechnologiesMeta`](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/MenkeTechnologiesMeta) · [`zpwr`](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zpwr) · [`zshrs`](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zshrs) · [`zsh-cargo-completion`](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zsh-cargo-completion) · [`zsh-expand`](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zsh-expand)

## [0x00] // WHAT IS THIS

A **massive** zsh completions plugin — over 28k command completions wired into compsys. Most were auto-generated by Python scripts that jacked into `--help` output, man pages, and web research, ripping completion data straight from the source. But then all completions have been cleaned, verified and updated with latest command options. Many have been handwritten as well.  Architecture-prefixed completions live in the `architecture_src` directory. A large ZUnit suite (see **// STATS** and **// TESTING**) validates structure, syntax, and coverage.

### // HARVESTED ECOSYSTEMS

Tool names for the completion corpus were harvested from:

- **Nix / nixpkgs** — every `pkgs.<attr>` shipping a binary
- **Homebrew** — every formula in `homebrew/core` (and the `cask` bottles that install CLIs)
- **Debian / Ubuntu APT** — every `bin/*` from `apt-cache pkgnames`, `/usr/share/man/man1`, `/usr/share/man/man8`, `/usr/share/man/man5`, `/usr/share/man/man6`, etc.
- **Fedora** — every binary from Fedora package repos
- **macOS system binaries** — `/usr/bin`, `/usr/sbin`, `/usr/libexec`, etc.
- **Kali Linux** — every binary shipped in the Kali package set
- **Alpine Linux** — `apk` package set
- **FreeBSD** — ports binaries and man pages
- **Various other Linux distros**
- **GitHub Releases** + **GitHub tree / code search** (multiple harvest rounds)
- **npm / npx / web research** — `create-*` scaffolders, scoped `@org/*` CLIs, and other Node tools verified against the npm registry (`npm view` bin/readme), live `npx … --help` output, package dist/tarballs, and upstream readmes (multi-round manual harvest; trivial or interactive-only scaffolders skipped)
- **Local zinit plugin checkouts** — completions vendored from installed plugins
- **crates.io**
- **Exotic language ecosystems** — Hackage (Haskell: `hakyll`, `shake`, `taffybar`), OPAM (OCaml: `odig`, `irmin`, `js_of_ocaml`, `learn-ocaml`, `alcotest`), Hex.pm (Elixir: `phx_new`, `ex_doc`, `dialyxir`, `igniter`, `mneme`), CPAN (Perl: `perlimports`, `perlnavigator`), CRAN (R: `radian`, `littler`), and AUR helpers (`aurman`, `pakku`) — verified against each project's cmdliner/argparse/OptionParser/Mix.Task switches, GetOptions definitions, or Cmd modules at the upstream source URL embedded in every completion file
- **Termux:API + Termux:tools** (Android) — all 57 `termux-*` commands from `termux-api-package/scripts/` (toast, vibrate, notification, sms-send, location, sensor, camera-photo, tts-speak, dialog, share, …) plus 13 `termux-*` commands from `termux-tools/scripts/` (backup, change-repo, info, open-url, reload-settings, restore, setup-storage, wake-lock, …) — flags parsed directly from each upstream `show_usage()` echo block and `getopts` spec, generated by `scripts/` automation
- **More exotic stragglers** — `nph` (Nim source formatter), `vab` (V Android Builder), `leo` (Aleo/Provable zero-knowledge language CLI), `cellranger` (10x Genomics single-cell sequencing pipeline) — flags from upstream README/usage docs / clap derive sources / 10x Cloud command-line argument reference
- **WebAssembly compiler toolchain** (Binaryen + WABT) — `wasm-as`, `wasm-dis`, `wasm-merge`, `wasm-shell`, `wasm-split`, `wasm-reduce`, `wasm-metadce`, `wasm-ctor-eval`, `wasm-fuzz-types`, `wasm-emscripten-finalize` (Binaryen, from `src/tools/*.cpp` + shared `ToolOptions` + 21-feature `feature.def`) and `wat-desugar` (WABT, from `src/tools/wat-desugar.cc`)
- **Bioinformatics** — `mash` (genome distance, marbl/Mash), `kraken2` + `kraken2-build` (taxonomic classification, DerrickWood), `centrifuge` + `centrifuge-build` + `centrifuge-inspect` (DaehwanKimLab), `trim_galore` (Rust rewrite — FelixKrueger), `macs2` (ChIP-seq peak caller — macs3-project/MACS, 138 flags across 12 subcommands), `deeptools` (NGS viz suite launcher) — verified against `GetOptions`, clap `cli.rs`, and argparse `add_argument` blocks
- **ML/AI tooling** — `llamafile` (Mozilla-Ocho, forwards llama.cpp common args), `vllm` (vllm-project, `entrypoints/cli/`), `wandb` (Click-based CLI), `mlflow` (Click-based CLI), `clearml` (multi-binary dispatch covering `clearml`, `clearml-session`, `clearml-serving`)
- **Astronomy, robotics, and misc** — `topcat` (Starlink/Bristol tabular data analyzer, SUN/253), `stilts` (TOPCAT's command-line companion, 50 tasks from SUN/256), `webots` (Cyberbotics robot simulator), `gazebo` + `gzserver` + `gzclient` (Gazebo Classic — new `gz` Ignition CLI deliberately not included; different architecture), `wllvm` + `wllvm++` + `extract-bc` (whole-program LLVM, travitch), `sox-ng` (modern SoX fork using `_ng` suffixed binaries), `pwn` (pwntools CTF/exploit-dev CLI, 20 subcommands from `pwnlib/commandline/main.py`)
- **Web3 / Blockchain** — `forc` (Sway/Fuel language, with plugin passthroughs to forc-fmt/forc-doc/forc-debug/forc-lsp/forc-publish/forc-tx), `btcwallet` (btcsuite Bitcoin wallet from `config.go` go-flags struct), `bcoin` + `bcoin-cli` + `bcoin-wallet` + `bwallet` + `bwallet-cli` (bcoin-org Bitcoin node + CLI), `movefmt` (Move language formatter, getopts-based), `move-prover` + `mvp` (Move formal prover, clap-derive from aptos-core)
- **TeX/LaTeX niche** — `latex2html` (113 Getopt::Long options), `mk4ht` (TeX4ht macro driver — 86 `<variant><dialect>` subcommands), `ltx2x` (LaTeX-to-XML/RTF/text), `latex-make` (CTAN make targets). `bibtexextract` deliberately skipped — no canonical tool exists by that name in CTAN or GitHub.
- **APL / Lisp / Smalltalk REPLs** — `gnu-apl` + `apl` (45 verified options from `UserPreferences.cc`), `klong` (kg.c usage), `kona` + `k` (kc.c args getopt), `ecl` (Embeddable Common-Lisp 30 options from cmdline.lsp), `pharo` (Pharo VM parameters from `parameters.c` + Smalltalk option handler)
- **Audio / EDA / Modern JS / Cargo** — `sonic-pi` + `sonic-pi-cli` (Widdershin/sonic-pi-cli `stop` subcommand only), `librepcb` + `librepcb-cli` (24 export options across open-project/library/symbol/package/step), `tjs` (txiki.js JS runtime: run/eval/serve/test/bundle/compile/app), `llrt` (AWS Low-Latency Runtime: compile/test), `cargo-dylint` (trailofbits Dylint clap structs), `cargo-features` (ToBinio cargo-features-manager `prune` subcommand)
- **Software-Defined Radio** — `rtl_433` (merbanan/rtl_433 — 38 options from src/rtl_433.c usage()), `hackrf-info` + `hackrf_info` (greatscottgadgets/hackrf — takes no flags upstream), `hackrf_sweep` (16 options + FFTW wisdom), `hackrf_clock` (HackRF Pro CLKIN/CLKOUT signal selection), `urh` + `urh_cli` (jopohl/urh Universal Radio Hacker — 37 cli flags for RX/TX/modulation/encoding), `sdrangel` + `sdrangelsrv` + `sdrangelbench` (f4exb/sdrangel MainParser flags), `sdrpp` (AlexandreRouma/SDRPlusPlus core/src/command_args.cpp defineAll())
- **Esoteric languages + live coding + niche cloud** — `lci` (justinmeza LOLCODE interpreter; main.c longopt table), `awib` (matslina Brainfuck compiler — no CLI flags, target via `@TARGET` directive in source), `foxdot` + `FoxDot` (Qirky/FoxDot Python live coding env for SuperCollider), `chicken` (Chicken Scheme compiler — 70+ flags from upstream wiki "Using the compiler" manual), `lakefs` (treeverse/lakeFS Git-for-data server — cobra subcommands run/setup/migrate/superuser/lua/gc/kv/flare, with nested migrate {version,up,goto,task} and kv {get,scan,dump,load})
- **Model Context Protocol server family** — All 7 active reference servers from `modelcontextprotocol/servers` (`mcp-server-everything` with stdio/sse/streamableHttp transports, `mcp-server-fetch` with `--user-agent`/`--ignore-robots-txt`/`--proxy-url`, `mcp-server-filesystem` with variadic allowed-directory paths, `mcp-server-git` with click `-r/--repository`/`-v/--verbose`, `mcp-server-memory`, `mcp-server-sequential-thinking`, `mcp-server-time` with `--local-timezone`) plus 11 archived servers from `modelcontextprotocol/servers-archived` still installable via `npx` (`mcp-server-{aws-kb-retrieval,brave-search,everart,gdrive,github,gitlab,google-maps,postgres,puppeteer,redis,slack}` — all are env-driven; only postgres/redis take a positional connection URL, only gdrive takes an optional `auth` token)
- **OCR + Modern AI/ML platforms** — `surya` family (`surya_ocr`, `surya_layout`, `surya_detect`, `surya_table`, `surya_latex_ocr`, `surya_gui`, `texify_gui` from datalab-to/surya), `marker` family (`marker`, `marker_single`, `marker_chunk_convert`, `marker_server`, `marker_gui`, `marker_extract` from datalab-to/marker), `nougat` + `nougat_api` (Meta Nougat scientific PDF OCR), `modal-client` (Modal serverless platform — 21 top-level + 53 nested subcommands), `marimo-cli` (Marimo reactive notebooks — 13 top-level subcommands), `cog-cli` (Replicate Cog ML packaging — 12 top-level subcommands), `e2b-cli` (E2B sandbox developer CLI — `auth`/`template`/`sandbox` groups with nested commands)
- **Linux / Bluetooth / AppImage / OIDC** — `appimage` + `*.AppImage` (meta-completion for AppImage runtime args from type2-runtime `runtime.c`), `appimaged` (probonopd/go-appimage daemon — `wrap`/`update`/`run`/`start` subcommands), `gattool` + `gatttool` (BlueZ legacy BLE attribute-protocol tool from bluez/attrib/gatttool.c), `iwspy` (wireless-tools spy list — positional-only grammar), `oidc-login` + `kubectl-oidc_login` (int128/kubelogin OIDC kubectl plugin — 23 flags across get-token/setup/clean)
- **ARM Cortex embedded toolchain** (`architecture_src/`) — all 20 `arm-none-eabi-*` cross-compiler + binutils binaries (`c++`, `g++`, `gcc`, `gcc-ar`, `gcc-nm`, `gcc-ranlib`, `addr2line`, `ar`, `as`, `c++filt`, `cpp`, `elfedit`, `ld`, `nm`, `objcopy`, `objdump`, `ranlib`, `readelf`, `size`, `strip`), mirrored from the existing `aarch64-linux-gnu-*` template family. `arm-none-eabi-gdb` was already covered by `more_src/_gdb-multiarch`'s multi-stem compdef.
- **VR/AR + IoT** — `monado-service` + `monado-cli` (Monado OpenXR runtime, test/probe subcommands; gitlab.freedesktop.org/monado), `openxr-explorer` + `openxrexplorer` (maluoi/openxr-explorer), `wivrn-server` + `wivrn-dashboard` (WiVRn streaming server — CLI11-based 9 flags), `mqtt-cli` + `mqtt` (HiveMQ MQTT CLI — 8 top-level subcommands + ~90 per-subcommand options from MqttCLICommand.java), `hass-cli` upgraded (Home Assistant CLI — full state-machine across 16 plugins)
- **Modern dev tools** — `mpy-cross` (MicroPython cross-compiler from mpy-cross/main.c), `cling` + `cling-jupyter` (C++ interactive interpreter — ClingOptions.td + clang passthroughs), `protoc-gen-ts` (TypeScript protoc plugin — stdin/stdout, no CLI; documented real OPTIONS keys in comment), `granted-cli` (common-fate Granted — urfave/cli 13 top-level subcommands), `aws-sso-cli` (synfinatic/aws-sso-cli — Kong-based 14 top-level subcommands)
- **3D printing + GIS** — `prusaslicer` + `prusa-slicer` (PrusaSlicer 42 CLI actions/transforms from PrintConfig.cpp; upgrade — old file was config-options-level), `cura-engine` + `CuraEngine` (Ultimaker CuraEngine slice/connect/help subcommands), `octoprint` (Click-based 11 top-level subcommands incl. serve/daemon/safemode/systeminfo/analysis/client/config/dev/plugins/timelapse/user), `qgis_process` (QGIS headless processing from qgsprocess.cpp), `grass8` + `grass` (GRASS GIS 8.x — `--tmp-project`/`--tmp-location`/`--tmp-mapset`/`--timeout`/`--config`), `grass7` (GRASS 7.x — `-wxpython`/`-wx`/`--wxpython`/`--wx`)
- **F# / .NET + Robotics** — `fake-cli` (FAKE F# Make build automation — Cli.fs docopt block), `paket-bootstrapper` + `paket.bootstrapper` (Paket bootstrapper from BootstrapperHelper.cs HelpText), `fsdocs` (F# docs generator — 4 verbs build/watch/init/convert, 37 flags across Option attributes), `fsx` + `fsxc` (F# script runner from nblockchain/fsx Fsxc.fs ParseArgsInternal), `rqt` (ROS Qt GUI framework — qt_gui_core/qt_gui/main.py argparse, 22 flags)
- **Cloud niche + Audio + Nix** — `upcloud-cli` + `upctl` (UpCloudLtd 21 top-level cobra subcommands + 104 nested), `exoscale-cli` (exoscale/cli 14 top-level subcommands, `_exo` already covers the actual binary), `fluidsynth` (FluidSynth real-time SoundFont synthesizer — 29 flags from src/fluidsynth.c long_options), `nix-direnv` + `nix-direnv-reload` (direnv stdlib extension — minimal CLI: only the generated `nix-direnv-reload` shim with no arguments). `hcloud-cli` deliberately skipped (Debian package name; binary is `hcloud`, already covered).
- **AI image/video upscaling (NCNN+Vulkan)** — `realsr-ncnn-vulkan` (Real-ESRGAN/Real-SR), `waifu2x-ncnn-vulkan`, `video2x` (k4yt3x — 42 flat flags via boost::program_options, not subcommands as spec assumed), `anime4kcpp` + `ac_cli` (Anime4KCPP — CLI rewrote to CLI11, has video subcommand)
- **Streaming + speech + media indexer** — `jacktrip` (Stanford CCRMA network audio — 59 flags from Settings.cpp longopts), `livekit-cli` + `lk` (LiveKit Cloud — 15 top-level cobra subcommands, ~50 nested), `livekit-egress` (LiveKit egress service), `rhvoice-test` + `rhvoice-service` + `RHVoice-test` + `RHVoice-service` (RHVoice speech synthesis), `moonlight-qt` + `Moonlight` (Moonlight Qt game-streaming client — 4 subcommands stream/list/pair/quit), `moonlight-embedded` + `moonlight` (Moonlight embedded — single-dash long options, 7 positional actions), `prowlarr` + `Prowlarr` (indexer aggregator — both `-flag` and `/flag` forms), `pavucontrol-qt` (Qt pavucontrol — QCommandLineOption block)
- **Hardware control + boot managers + Wi-Fi forensics + Wayland terminal IPC** — `ratbagctl` (libratbag gaming-mouse config — 8 top-level + nested actions), `poop` (Andrew Kelley's Performance Of Our Programs benchmark — 4 flags from src/main.zig), `zfsbootmenu` + `generate-zbm` (ZBM Boot Menu — 16 flags from bin/generate-zbm Perl Getopt::Long), `refind-install` + 4 sibling refind-* binaries (rEFInd EFI boot manager — refind-install/mkrlconf/mkdefault/mvrefind/mkfont per-binary dispatch), `hcxdumptool` + 8 sibling `hcx*tools` (Wi-Fi pcap/PMKID/handshake tools from ZerBea/hcxtools — `hcxpcapngtool` 31 flags / `hcxhashtool` 50 flags / etc.), `footclient` (foot Wayland terminal IPC client — 19 flags; agent fixed spec which incorrectly listed `foot-msg`)
- **Crypto wallet + PGP + QUIC stacks + game engine** — `trezorctl` (Trezor click-based CLI — 22 top-level subcommands + 10 globals), `sequoia-keystore` (Sequoia-PGP keystore daemon — clap derive, 7 flags), `ngtcp2-client` + `ngtcp2-server` (ngtcp2 reference QUIC implementation — 56/44 flags), `quicinterop` + `quicattack` (Microsoft msquic test tools — 12/8 flags), `quiche-client` + `quiche-server` (Cloudflare quiche QUIC — 39/30 flags from apps/src/args.rs ClientArgs/ServerArgs), `defold` (Defold game engine launcher — 67 flags + 5 subcommands build/bundle/clean/distclean/resolve from Bob.java; agent corrected spec which listed non-existent compile/run/update subcommands)
- **Bioinformatics + Astronomy (deep)** — `freebayes` (Bayesian variant caller — 79 long flags from src/Parameters.cpp long_options[]), `igv` (Integrative Genomics Viewer Java launcher), `sextractor` + `sex` + `source-extractor` (74 PARAM overrides from src/preflist.h), `scamp` (98 PARAM overrides), `swarp` + `SWarp` (64 PARAM overrides), `solve-field` (Astrometry.net solver wrapper — 92 long flags from solver/solve-field.c + augment-xylist.c), `astrometry-engine` (the actual Astrometry.net engine — 13 flags from solver/engine-main.c; agent corrected spec flags `-i/--input`/`-d/--inputs-dir`/`-s/--single`/`-r/--ranges` which don't exist upstream — real names are `--inputs-from`/`--base-dir`/`--solved`)
- **Hare language + OpenFOAM + DB + DNS** — `harec` (Hare compiler from sr.ht ~sircmpwn/harec — getopt string `"a:D:hM:m:N:o:Tt:v"`), `haredoc` (Hare doc extractor from ~sircmpwn/hare), `openfoam` + `openfoam-docker` + `openfoam-docker-arm` (OpenFOAM container wrapper — 26 flags), `pimpleFoam` (foamRun PIMPLE solver — argList common opts + `-solver`), `foamCleanCase` (OpenFOAM case-cleanup — 2 flags from bin/foamCleanCase usage()), `foamListTimes` (14 flags from foamListTimes.C addBoolOption + timeSelector::addOptions), `mssql-conf` (Microsoft SQL Server config — 8 subcommands setup/set/unset/traceflag/set-collation/set-edition/setup-ad-keytab/validate-ad-config + 36 settings), `aerospike-cli` (reugn/aerospike-cli SQL JDBC CLI — closest real binary by that exact name), `knot-dig` (Knot DNS dig alias — 139 entries: 16 `-` opts + ~123 `+[no]…` plus-options from kdig_params.c)
- **NCBI BLAST+ database utilities** — `blastdbcmd` (32 flags from c++/src/app/blastdb/blastdbcmd.cpp), `update_blastdb` + `update_blastdb.pl` (14 flags from update_blastdb.pl Getopt::Long table), `blastdb_aliastool` (24 flags incl. real `-oid_masks`/`-seqid_*` block), `blastdbcheck` (17 flags; spec's `-isam`/`-no_legacy`/`-binary_size` don't exist). Agent downloaded the NCBI BLAST+ 2.17.0 source tarball for verification.
- **HMMER 3.x utilities** — `hmmstat` (only `-h` upstream — spec's `--cpu`/`--mpi` aren't in ESL_OPTIONS), `hmmfetch` (5 flags incl. real `-O`), `hmmsim` (39 flags — full ESL_OPTIONS including `--mpi`/`--Eft`-family), `hmmemit` (15 flags incl. real `-C`/`-L`/`--local`/`--unilocal`/`--glocal`/`--uniglocal`/`--minl`/`--minu`), `hmmpgmd` (11 flags — spec's `--cs`/`--ws` don't exist, real is `--ccncts`/`--wcncts`), `hmmer` (no actual upstream binary — file written as documented placeholder for user-defined wrappers).
- **Voice / speech recognition + Arch build tools** — `whisper-cli` (whisper.cpp 66 flags from examples/cli/cli.cpp; legacy `main` upstream-deprecated, prints redirect warning to whisper-cli), `wyoming-piper` (rhasspy/wyoming-piper 20 flags incl. `--noise-w-scale`/`--noise-w` alias), `wyoming-faster-whisper` (21 flags). `wyoming-cli` deliberately skipped (rhasspy/wyoming is a protocol library with no console_scripts). `mkarchroot` (9 flags from src/mkarchroot.in getopts `'hUC:M:c:f:s'`; spec's `-N` doesn't exist), `makechrootpkg` (15 flags from src/makechrootpkg.in getopts; spec misclassified `-C` and bind flags — real semantics from upstream).

Notable per-binary highlights: **s6-dns-hosts-compile** (2 flags; compile `/etc/hosts` into a packed cdb for fast s6-dns client lookup). **s6-dnsq** + **s6-dnsqr** (4 flags each; low-level direct DNS query, `-1`/`-2` stdout/stderr packet-dump mutex + `-t MS` + `-D LEVEL` debug; positionals are qtype (autocomplete A/AAAA/MX/NS/CNAME/PTR/SOA/SRV/TXT/ANY) + query name + (s6-dnsq only) nameserver IPs). **s6-dnssrv** (3 flags + 3 positionals; SRV-record lookup with `service`/`protocol`/`name` triplet — service autocomplete enum: http/https/ftp/ssh/smtp/imap/imaps/pop3/pop3s/ldap/ldaps/xmpp/xmpp-server/xmpp-client/sip/sips/kerberos/ntp/dns; protocol autocomplete: tcp/udp/tls). **s6-randomip** (3 flags; generate random valid IPv4/IPv6 addresses without DNS query — `-4`/`-6` family mutex + `-n N`). **File `_mdevd` (2-stem `#compdef mdevd mdevd-coldplug`)** extracted from [`skarnet/mdevd/src/mdevd/mdevd.c`](https://github.com/skarnet/mdevd/blob/master/src/mdevd/mdevd.c) + [`mdevd-coldplug.c`](https://github.com/skarnet/mdevd/blob/master/src/mdevd/mdevd-coldplug.c) USAGE strings + `subgetopt_r` specs (`nNv:D:I:o:O:b:f:s:d:F:C` and `v:s:O:b:`) + case-arm decoding for the 2-way `-n`/`-N` dry-run mutex (`dryrun = 1` print-only-no-act xor `dryrun = 2` verbose-dry-run-print-every-event-and-match). udev replacement implementing the busybox mdev configuration syntax but running as a long-lived netlink-listener daemon (vs mdev which is invoked per-event by the kernel), making it suitable as the device-management daemon under s6 supervision. **mdevd** (12 flags inc. `-v VERB`, `-D NOTIFD`, `-I INTAKE`, `-o OUTPUTFD`, `-O NLGROUPS` bitmask, `-b KBUFSZ`, `-f CONFFILE`, **2-way mutex `-n`/`-N`** dry-run, `-s SLASHSYS`, `-d SLASHDEV`, `-F FWBASE`, `-C` coldplug-then-exit). **mdevd-coldplug** (4 flags; one-shot coldplug helper walking `/sys/devices` to force netlink uevents for every node currently present — sends events to the running mdevd via netlink group; useful at boot for devices that were already present before mdevd started). **File `_utmps-utmpd` (3-stem `#compdef utmps-utmpd utmps-write utmps-wtmpd`)** extracted from [`skarnet/utmps/src/utmps/utmps-{utmpd,write,wtmpd}.c`](https://github.com/skarnet/utmps/tree/master/src/utmps) USAGE strings (utmps-utmpd: `int main(void)` no args — pure daemon; utmps-wtmpd: optional positional wtmp-file override; utmps-write: full subgetopt `uwU:W:t:T:h:i:l:p:`) + case-arm decoding showing `utmps-write -u`/`-w` are **independent bit flags** (`what |= 1` / `what |= 2`) **NOT mutex** — both can be combined to write the same record into both utmp AND wtmp simultaneously (this is the typical login-style use case). utmps replaces glibc's system-wide utmpx-mutex-locked file approach with a UCSPI socket protocol talking to dedicated long-running daemons, eliminating the historical setuid binaries + race-condition class. **utmps-write** has 10 flags + 3 positionals (entry id + type + tty line); type field autocomplete: EMPTY/RUN_LVL/BOOT_TIME/NEW_TIME/OLD_TIME/INIT_PROCESS/LOGIN_PROCESS/USER_PROCESS/DEAD_PROCESS/ACCOUNTING. **Hunt-skip log this round**: skarnet/s6-networking (UCSPI-TCP/IP server family — needs systematic audit since older rounds covered some), skarnet/execline (shell-replacement language ~40 chain-loadable binaries — many names like `backtick`/`foreground`/`if`/`ifelse`/`importas`/`redirfd`/`pipeline`/`elglob`/`loopwhilex`/`tryexec`/`withstdinas` clash with shell builtins or other Unix commands; per-binary dup audit + clash-vs-coverage judgment-call required). The `skadns` subdir of s6-dns (libs6dns + skadns library helpers — header files + non-public-binary linker source, not user-facing CLIs). **Blacklist additions (19)**: 2 entries in `m*` range + 14 in `s6-d*`/`s6-r*` range + 3 in `u*` range. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 132nd consecutive clean round.
- **Skarnet s6-portable-utils R126 — 41-stem multi-binary harvest** (`#compdef s6-basename s6-cat s6-chmod s6-chown s6-cut s6-dirname s6-dumpenv s6-echo s6-env s6-expr s6-false s6-format-filter s6-grep s6-head s6-hiercopy s6-linkname s6-ln s6-ls s6-maximumtime s6-mkdir s6-nice s6-nuke s6-pause s6-printenv s6-quote s6-quote-filter s6-rename s6-rmrf s6-seq s6-sleep s6-sort s6-sync s6-tai64ndiff s6-tail s6-touch s6-true s6-uniquename s6-unquote s6-unquote-filter s6-update-symlinks seekablepipe`) (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep; per-binary audit identified `s6-clock` + `s6-mkfifo` as the 2 already-covered binaries in this repo, deliberately omitted from the new `#compdef` line). Surface extracted source-direct from upstream [`skarnet/s6-portable-utils/src/s6-portable-utils/*.c`](https://github.com/skarnet/s6-portable-utils/tree/master/src/s6-portable-utils) USAGE strings + `subgetopt_r` option-string specs + case-arm decoding for the mutex flag groups via `gh api`. Single multi-stem file `_s6-basename` is the alphabetically-first stem (`s6-basename` < `seekablepipe` because `6` (0x36) < `e` (0x65)). **Coverage**: 41-stem multi-binary harvest of the portable coreutils-style utility binaries that ship with the s6 family — sister tools to the existing larger s6 ecosystem (R117-R125). The portable utils are deliberately not POSIX-compatible drop-in replacements; they trade compat for correctness, smaller code, and consistent behavior across platforms (Linux/BSD/Solaris/macOS). Reusable helper `_s6_digit_lines` shared between `s6-head` and `s6-tail` for the 9-way `-1..-9` digit-shortcut line-count mutex. **Notable per-binary surfaces**: **s6-chown** (`Uu:g:` 3 flags; `-u UID` xor `-U` env-mode (`-U` decoded from source body: reads `$UID` + `$GID` env vars via `getenv("UID")` + `getenv("GID")` + `uid0_scan`/`gid0_scan`)). **s6-cut** (`nsb:c:f:d:` 6 flags; **3-way mutex `-b`/`-c`/`-f`** byte/char/field selection + `-d DELIM` + `-n` no-mb-split + `-s` suppress-no-delim). **s6-dumpenv** (`nNm:` 3 flags; **2-way mutex `-n`/`-N`** empty-value rejection xor allowance + `-m MODE` octal). **s6-grep** (`EFicnqv` 7 flags; **2-way mutex `-E`/`-F`** extended-regex xor fixed-string + `-icnqv` standard grep flags). **s6-head** + **s6-tail** (subgetopt `S123456789n:c:` / `123456789n:c:`; **digit-shortcut 9-way mutex** `-1..-9` shared via helper + line/char count flags). **s6-ln** (`nsfLP` 5 flags; **2-way mutex `-L`/`-P`** follow-symlinks xor no-follow + `-n` treat-dest-as-file + `-s` symlink + `-f` force). **s6-ls** (`0aAx:` 4 flags; **2-way mutex `-a`/`-A`** show-dot+dotdot xor exclude-dot+dotdot (case-arm decoded: `all = 1` xor `all = 2`) + `-0` NUL-separate + `-x PATTERN` repeatable exclude). **s6-maximumtime** (`0abikqtx12` 10 flags; **10-way signal-selection mutex** `-0` (no signal) / `-a` (SIGALRM) / `-b` (SIGABRT) / `-i` (SIGINT) / `-k` (SIGKILL) / `-q` (SIGQUIT) / `-t` (SIGTERM, default) / `-x` (SIGXCPU) / `-1` (SIGUSR1) / `-2` (SIGUSR2) — each decoded from `tosend = SIG... ; break ;` case arm). **s6-nice** (`Iin:` 3 flags; **2-way mutex `-I`/`-i`** strict-error xor ignore-setpriority-failures + `-n INCR`). **s6-nuke** (`htk` 3 flags; **3-way signal mutex** `-h` SIGHUP / `-t` SIGTERM (default) / `-k` SIGKILL — broadcast to every process except self + pid 1). **s6-pause** (`thaqbip:` 7 flags; signal-list **builders** — not mutex — each of `-t`/`-h`/`-a`/`-q`/`-b`/`-i` appends one signal to the wake-list via case-arm `sigs[nsig++] = SIG...; break ;` + `-p SIG,SIG,...` for additional names/numbers). **s6-printenv** (`nd:0` 3 flags; **2-way mutex `-0`/`-d`** NUL-delim xor custom-delim + `-n` no-newline). **s6-sort** (`bcfru0` 6 flags; standard sort-style flags). **s6-unquote-filter** (`qQvwd:` 5 flags; **4-way mutex `-q`/`-Q`/`-v`/`-w`** invalid-byte handling: silent-drop / silent-drop-warn-stderr / verbose-passthrough / warn-and-continue). **No-flag binaries** (`int main(void)`): s6-cat / s6-false / s6-sync / s6-true; **no-flag with argv**: s6-tai64ndiff (reads s6-log timestamps from argv files or stdin) + s6-rmrf + s6-touch + s6-update-symlinks (positional-only). **Hunt-skip log this round**: 2 binaries from this repo were already in older coverage and deliberately omitted: `s6-clock` (CLOCK_REALTIME printer) and `s6-mkfifo` (mkfifo(2) wrapper — already covered in `more_src/_s6-mkfifo`); skarnet/s6-networking + skarnet/s6-dns + skarnet/execline + skarnet/utmps + skarnet/mdevd remain deferred from R124/R125. **Blacklist additions (41)**: 41 entries in `s*` range — by far the largest single-round blacklist add in s6-family coverage to date. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 131st consecutive clean round.
- **Skarnet s6-linux-utils R125 — fstab2s6rc/rngseed/s6-chroot/s6-freeramdisk/s6-hostname/s6-logwatch/s6-mount/s6-pivotchroot/s6-ps/s6-swapoff/s6-swapon/s6-umount (12-stem multi-binary)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surface extracted source-direct from upstream [`skarnet/s6-linux-utils/src/s6-linux-utils/*.c`](https://github.com/skarnet/s6-linux-utils/tree/master/src/s6-linux-utils) USAGE strings + `subgetopt_r` option-string specs + skalibs `GOL_main` `gol_bool` + `gol_arg` tables + case-arm decoding for the mutex flag groups (`rngseed`: -r/-R credentialed-vs-uncredentialed entropy reads, -n/-N blocking-vs-nonblocking, -w/-W credentialed-vs-uncredentialed entropy writes — decoded from `flags.read=1/flags.rcred=1|0`, `flags.block=0|1`, `flags.write=1/flags.wcred=1|0` case-arm assignments; `fstab2s6rc`: 3 paired-bit-clear-vs-set mutex groups `-A`/`-a` noauto, `-U`/`-u` uuid, `-E`/`-e` essential — extracted from `gol_bool` `.clear`/`.set` field pairings) via `gh api`. Single multi-stem file `_fstab2s6rc` is `#compdef fstab2s6rc rngseed s6-chroot s6-freeramdisk s6-hostname s6-logwatch s6-mount s6-pivotchroot s6-ps s6-swapoff s6-swapon s6-umount` (filename uses alphabetically-first stem `fstab2s6rc` since `f` < `r` < `s`). **Coverage**: 12-stem multi-binary harvest of the Linux-specific system-administration utilities that compose with the s6 init+supervision stack (R117-R124). Sister to R124's `_s6-linux-init` (pid 1 + shutdown) and to the existing s6-svc/s6-supervise infrastructure. **Per-binary surface**: **fstab2s6rc** (GOL_main; 10 flags + 1 positional): generate an s6-rc compiled-db source tree from /etc/fstab entries (one s6-rc service per mountpoint); 3-pair mutexes inc. `-A`/`-a` noauto-handling, `-U`/`-u` UUID-emission, `-E`/`-e` essential-marking + `-F FSTAB` / `-m MODE` octal-perms / `-B BUNDLE` group-bundle / `-d BASEDEP` dependency. **rngseed** (subgetopt `d:v:rRnNwW`; 8 flags): maintain the kernel CSPRNG seed across reboots via RNDADDENTROPY ioctl; `-d SEEDDIR` (default /var/lib/rngseed), `-v VERB`, **3 mutex pairs** `-r`/`-R` (read with/without credit), `-n`/`-N` (non-block/block), `-w`/`-W` (write with/without credit). **s6-chroot** (chroot(8) minimalist; 2 positionals: dir + prog). **s6-freeramdisk** (1 positional: /dev/ram*; calls BLKFLSBUF). **s6-hostname** (1 optional positional: get or set kernel hostname). **s6-logwatch** (subgetopt `m:`; 1 flag + 1 positional): tail an s6-log directory; `-m CHARS` max per-entry char cap (NOT a pattern — verified via case-arm `if (!uint0_scan(l.arg, &maxlen))`). **s6-mount** (subgetopt `nz:arwt:o:`; 7 flags + 2 positionals): mount(8) replacement supporting both `-a -z fstab` mount-all form AND `-t type -o options device mountpoint` single-mount form; `-n` no-op (kept for util-linux compat — confirmed via `case 'n' : break ;`), `-z FSTAB` alternative fstab, `-a` mount-all, **2-way mutex** `-r`/`-w` ro xor rw, `-t TYPE` (autocomplete enum: ext4/ext3/ext2/btrfs/xfs/zfs/f2fs/vfat/tmpfs/proc/sysfs/devtmpfs/cgroup/cgroup2/overlay), `-o OPTS` repeatable. **s6-pivotchroot** (3 positionals; Linux pivot_root(2) + chroot atomic swap used by s6-linux-init during initramfs handoff). **s6-ps** (subgetopt `Hlw:W:o:`; 5 flags): ps(1) replacement reading /proc directly; `-H` tree mode, **2-way mutex** `-l` long xor `-o FIELDS` custom field list (autocomplete enum of ~25 supported fields: pid/ppid/pgid/sid/uid/gid/user/group/tty/tpgid/stat/command/args/nice/pri/rtprio/policy/cputime/utime/stime/start_time/vsize/rss/start/ttime), `-w SPACING` column spacing, `-W WCHANFILE` (default /proc/kallsyms). **s6-swapoff** / **s6-swapon** / **s6-umount** (each: `-a` mount-all-from-fstab + 1 optional positional). **Hunt-skip log this round**: skarnet/s6-portable-utils (43 portable-utility binaries — `s6-basename`/`s6-cat`/`s6-chmod`/`s6-chown`/`s6-clock`/`s6-cut`/`s6-dirname`/`s6-dumpenv`/`s6-echo`/`s6-env`/`s6-expr`/`s6-false`/`s6-format-filter`/`s6-grep`/`s6-head`/`s6-hiercopy`/`s6-linkname`/`s6-ln`/`s6-ls`/`s6-maximumtime`/`s6-mkdir`/`s6-mkfifo`/`s6-nice`/`s6-nuke`/`s6-pause`/`s6-printenv`/`s6-quote-filter`/`s6-quote`/`s6-rename`/`s6-rmrf`/`s6-seq`/`s6-sleep`/`s6-sort`/`s6-sync`/`s6-tai64ndiff`/`s6-tail`/`s6-touch`/`s6-true`/`s6-uniquename`/`s6-unquote-filter`/`s6-unquote`/`s6-update-symlinks`/`seekablepipe` — these need a separate per-binary dup audit since several names overlap with coreutils-style commands like `s6-cat`/`s6-grep`/`s6-head`/`s6-tail`/`s6-sort` that may have been previously batched; deferred for R126+ systematic audit), skarnet/s6-networking + skarnet/s6-dns (TCP/IP UCSPI server family + DNS resolver utilities — partial coverage in older rounds; needs systematic audit), skarnet/execline (shell-replacement language ~40 chain-loadable binaries — many names clash with shell builtins), skarnet/utmps (utmp/wtmp replacement family), skarnet/mdevd (udev replacement). **Blacklist additions (12)**: 1 entry in `f*` (fstab2s6rc) + 1 in `r*` (rngseed) + 10 in `s6-*` range. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 130th consecutive clean round.

Covers the 9 s6-linux-init binaries not previously included (s6-linux-init-maker — the boot-image generator — was already covered). **s6-linux-init** (12 flags; stage-1 pid 1 binary that brings up the early boot environment then chain-loads stage-2): GOL_main long-options — `-v VERB`/`--verbosity`, `-c BASEDIR`/`--basedir`, `-p PATH`/`--initial-path`, `-s DIR`/`--envdumpdir`, `-m UMASK`/`--umask`, `-d FSTYPE`/`--slashdev`, `-D NAME`/`--default-runlevel` (default "default"), **2-way mutex `-n`/`--no-unmount-slashrun` xor `-N`/`--hands-off-slashrun`**, `-C`/`--container`, `-B`/`--no-logger`, `-W FD`/`--readiness-fd`. **s6-linux-init-telinit** (1 positional): switch to a different runlevel. **s6-linux-init-echo** (2 flags + variadic): `-n` no-trailing-newline + `-s SEP` field separator; minimal echo replacement for early-boot scripts. **s6-linux-init-logouthookd** / **s6-linux-init-nuke** / **s6-linux-init-umountall** (no CLI flags): logout-cleanup daemon / SIGKILL-everything-except-pid-1 / unmount-everything-except-devtmpfs/proc/sysfs (hardcoded MAXLINES=99). **s6-linux-init-hpr** (9 flags; low-level halt/poweroff/reboot called by shutdown after grace): **3-way mutex `-h`/`-p`/`-r`** primary action (case arms: what=1/2/3) + `-f` skip `/run/initctl` + **2-way mutex `-d`/`-w`** wtmp-mode (no-record xor only-record-no-actual) + `-W` no-wall + `-n` no-sync + `-i` confirm-hostname. **s6-linux-init-shutdown** (12 flags + 2 positionals; util-linux-compatible shutdown(8) replacement): **5-way mutex `-h`/`-p`/`-r`/`-k`/`-c`** primary (case arms what=1/2/3/4/cancel) + **2-way mutex `-H`/`-P`** secondary after-halt action (subwhat=1/2) + **2-way mutex `-f`/`-F`** fsck-skip xor fsck-force (both case-arm no-ops kept for util-linux backwards-compat — confirmed by source comments `/* talk to the hand */` `/* no, the other hand */`) + `-a` honor `/etc/shutdown.allow` + `-i` confirm-hostname + `-t SEC` grace-period; positionals are time-spec + optional broadcast message. **s6-linux-init-shutdownd** (5 flags; long-running daemon that orchestrates the shutdown sequence): `-d FD` notification-fd + `-c BASEDIR` + `-g MS` grace ms + `-C` container + `-B` no-logger. **Hunt-skip log this round**: skarnet/s6-linux-utils (separate misc-utility repo — distinct from s6-linux-init; needs its own R125+ round), skarnet/s6-portable-utils (cross-platform companion to s6-linux-utils; another candidate R125+ round), skarnet/s6-networking (UCSPI-TCP/IP server family — partially covered in older rounds; needs systematic audit), skarnet/s6-dns (DNS resolver utility family — fresh candidate for R126+), skarnet/execline (shell-replacement language with ~40 chain-loadable binaries — many names like `backtick`/`foreground`/`if`/`ifelse` clash with shell builtins, evaluate per-binary), skarnet/utmps (utmp/wtmp replacement family), skarnet/mdevd (udev replacement). **Blacklist additions (13)**: 4 entries in the `s6-rc*` range + 9 entries in the `s6-linux-init*` range. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 129th consecutive clean round.

and from [`src/supervision/s6-permafailon.c`](https://github.com/skarnet/s6/blob/master/src/supervision/s6-permafailon.c) USAGE string (no subgetopt; pure positional). **Coverage**: 3 files covering 12 binaries — completes the `src/supervision` directory minus the 6 binaries already covered (s6-supervise/s6-svc/s6-svstat/s6-svok/s6-svscan/s6-svscanctl per pre-R123 audit). **File `_s6-svdt` (8-stem `#compdef s6-svdt s6-svdt-clear s6-svlink s6-svlisten s6-svlisten1 s6-svperms s6-svunlink s6-svwait`)** — supervision-tree manipulation clients: **s6-svdt** (3 flags + 1 positional; dump down-time entries / death tally for a service; `-S` flat numeric xor `-s` sub-summary mutex + `-n MAXENTRIES`), **s6-svdt-clear** (no flags + 1 positional; reset down-time history), **s6-svlink** (5 flags + 3 positionals; atomically link a servicedir into a scandir; `-d`/`-D` down-block-mode mutex, `-f` force, `-P` protect-on-rescan, `-t MS`), **s6-svlisten** (`#flags + variadic`; multi-service state-wait + chain-load prog; 6-way state mutex + `-a`/`-o` ALL/ANY conjunction mutex + `-t MS`; positionals are servicedirs terminated by `""` then prog-and-args), **s6-svlisten1** (single-service variant of svlisten; 6-way state mutex + `-t MS`), **s6-svperms** (10 flags + variadic; get/set permission triple on servicedirs that controls who can use s6-svc/s6-svwait; `-v` verbose, **5-way mutex** `-u`/`-g GROUP`/`-G GROUP`/`-o`/`-O GROUP` perms-target, **2-way mutex** `-e`/`-E GROUP` event-subscription gid filter), **s6-svunlink** (2 flags + 2 positionals; inverse of svlink; `-X` skip bring-down, `-t MS`), **s6-svwait** (same surface as svlisten but does NOT chain-load any prog; just waits then exits — used for one-shot state-wait checks in scripts). Reusable helper `_s6_sv_state_flags` shared by svlisten/svlisten1/svwait. **File `_s6-notify-fd-from-socket` (3-stem `#compdef s6-notify-fd-from-socket s6-notify-socket-from-fd s6-notifyoncheck`)** — service-readiness notification adapters bridging between the s6 "write to notification-fd" readiness protocol and the systemd-style `sd_notify(3)` UNIX-socket protocol: **s6-notify-fd-from-socket** (forward adapter; receive sd_notify-style `READY=1` datagram then signal readiness on s6 notification-fd; 5 flags inc. `-f`/`--no-doublefork` xor `--doublefork` mutex, `-3 FD`/`--notification-fd FD`, `-t MS`/`--timeout MS`), **s6-notify-socket-from-fd** (inverse adapter; receive s6 readiness signal then emit sd_notify datagram; 7 flags inc. `-k`/`--keep-environment` to retain `NOTIFY_SOCKET` env var, `-d FD`/`--notification-fd FD`, `-t MS`/`--timeout MS`), **s6-notifyoncheck** (wrap a long-running service with a periodic external check; 8 flags inc. `-d`/`--doublefork`, `-3 FD`/`--notification-fd FD`, `-s MS`/`--initial-sleep MS`, `-T MS`/`--global-timeout MS`, `-t MS`/`--local-timeout MS`, `-w MS`/`--waiting-time MS`, `-n N`/`--tries N`, `-c PROG`/`--check-program PROG` (execline-only — gated by `#ifdef S6_USE_EXECLINE` in source)). **File `_s6-permafailon` (1-stem)** — service-death-rate auto-disabler designed to be placed in a servicedir's finish script. No CLI flags + 4 positionals: `seconds` (rolling-window size in seconds), `deathcount` (threshold), `statuslist` (comma-separated list of fatal exit statuses), prog-and-args. If the service has died `deathcount` times within `seconds` with any of the `statuslist` exit statuses, triggers a permafailure by chain-loading prog (typically `s6-svc -O .` to disable). **Hunt-skip log this round**: s6-background-watch.c (header file, not a separate binary — confirmed by re-reading the conn-tools/supervision file listing). **Blacklist additions (12)**: 12 entries distributed across `s6-n*` (3), `s6-p*` (1), and `s6-sv*` (8) ranges. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 128th consecutive clean round.
- **Skarnet s6 conn-tools tail R122 — s6-sudo/s6-sudoc/s6-sudod (3-stem) + s6-accessrules-cdb-from-fs/s6-accessrules-fs-from-cdb (2-stem) + s6-connlimit (1-stem) + s6-ioconnect (1-stem) — 4 files / 7 binaries** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surface extracted source-direct from upstream skarnet/s6 [`src/conn-tools/s6-sudo{,c,d}.c`](https://github.com/skarnet/s6/tree/master/src/conn-tools) + [`s6-accessrules-{cdb-from-fs,fs-from-cdb}.c`](https://github.com/skarnet/s6/tree/master/src/conn-tools) + [`s6-connlimit.c`](https://github.com/skarnet/s6/blob/master/src/conn-tools/s6-connlimit.c) + [`s6-ioconnect.c`](https://github.com/skarnet/s6/blob/master/src/conn-tools/s6-ioconnect.c) USAGE strings + `subgetopt_r` option-string specs + case-arm decoding for non-obvious flag groups via `gh api`. **Coverage**: 4 files covering 7 binaries — finishes off the entire `src/conn-tools` directory of upstream s6 (the rest of which was already covered in R117/R120/R121). Carryforward from R121 hunt-skip log. **File `_s6-sudo` (3-stem `#compdef s6-sudo s6-sudoc s6-sudod`)** — Skarnet's UCSPI-sudo privilege-escalation framework: **s6-sudo** (client; 8 flags + variadic positionals): 3-way mutex verbosity `-q`/`-Q`/`-v`, `-p BINDPATH` local socket bind path, `-l LOCALNAME` PROTO_LOCAL override, `-e` do NOT transmit environment to remote prog, `-t MS` connection setup timeout, `-T MS` total run timeout; positionals are s6-sudod socket path + remote prog-and-args. **s6-sudoc** (UCSPI-client half; 3 flags + variadic): `-e`, `-t MS` connection (`timeoutconn`), `-T MS` total run; positional is remote prog-and-args. Typically invoked indirectly via s6-sudo. **s6-sudod** (server-side prog runner; 5 flags + variadic): `-0` null-redirect stdin / `-1` null-redirect stdout / `-2` null-redirect stderr as independent bitwise toggles, `-d` null-redirect all four proxied fds at once (equivalent to `-0 -1 -2` + control-fd), `-t MS` client inactivity timeout; positional is prog-and-args. **File `_s6-accessrules-cdb-from-fs` (2-stem `#compdef s6-accessrules-cdb-from-fs s6-accessrules-fs-from-cdb`)** — bidirectional converter between filesystem-tree access-rules db (one file per rule, easy to edit) and packed CDB file (single atomic file, fast to query at server-runtime; what production s6 servers query via the `-x RULESFILE` flag from R120/R121): **s6-accessrules-cdb-from-fs** (1 flag + 2 positionals): `-m MODE` / `--mode MODE` octal permissions on output CDB (extracted from `subgetopt_long` table `{ .so = 'm', .lo = "mode", .i = GOLA_MODE }`); positionals are output CDB file + input rules directory tree. **s6-accessrules-fs-from-cdb** (no flags + 2 positionals): output rules directory + input CDB file. **File `_s6-connlimit` (1-stem)** — environment-driven connection-count guard: chain-loads prog if under limit; reads `$PROTO`, then queries `$PROTOCONNNUM` and `$PROTOMAX` from the UCSPI server environment to decide whether the current peer has exceeded its concurrent connection allowance. No CLI options (pure env + argv[1..] chain-loader). **File `_s6-ioconnect` (1-stem)** — bidirectional I/O splicer that shuttles bytes between (stdin → `-w fdw`) and (`-r fdr` → stdout) until either side closes; typically used inside a UCSPI pipeline. 3 flags: `-t MS` inactivity timeout, `-r FD` source fd (default 6), `-w FD` sink fd (default 7). The deprecated `-0`/`-1`/`-6`/`-7` flags discovered in the `012t:r:w:67` subgetopt string are case-arm no-ops kept only for backward compatibility (auto-detected at runtime per upstream source comments `/* these options are deprecated */` `/* only there for compatibility */` `/* flagsocket is autodetected now */`); NOT offered for completion. **Hunt-skip log this round**: s6-svc/s6-svstat/s6-svok/s6-svscan/s6-svscanctl/s6-svlisten/s6-svlisten1/s6-svperms/s6-svlink/s6-svunlink/s6-svwait/s6-svdt/s6-svdt-clear/s6-supervise/s6-notifyoncheck/s6-notify-fd-from-socket/s6-notify-socket-from-fd/s6-permafailon (entire `src/supervision` directory — 18 binaries — partially already in older completions, but at least s6-svc/s6-svstat/s6-svok/s6-svscan were noted "already partially covered" in R117 hunt-skip; needs systematic R123+ audit of which are actually covered vs missing). **Blacklist additions (7)**: 7 entries distributed across `s6-a*`, `s6-c*`, `s6-i*`, `s6-s*` ranges. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 127th consecutive clean round.
- **Skarnet s6 ipcserver framework R121 — s6-ipcclient/s6-ipcserver/s6-ipcserver-access/s6-ipcserver-socketbinder/s6-ipcserverd (5-stem multi-binary)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Single multi-stem file `_s6-ipcclient` is `#compdef s6-ipcclient s6-ipcserver s6-ipcserver-access s6-ipcserver-socketbinder s6-ipcserverd`. **Coverage**: 5-stem multi-binary harvest covering the s6 UCSPI UNIX-domain socket client+server framework — Skarnet's clean-room reimplementation of Dan Bernstein's UCSPI-UNIX protocol with the supervised-process improvements that motivate the rest of s6. Carryforward from R118/R119/R120 hunt-skip log. **Per-binary surface**: **s6-ipcclient** (connect to a UNIX-domain socket and chain-load prog with the connection wrapped as UCSPI protocol fds — typically fd 6/7) — 5 flags + 2 positionals: **3-way mutex verbosity** `-q` xor `-Q` xor `-v` (quiet xor very-quiet xor verbose), `-p BINDPATH` local socket path to bind from, `-l LOCALNAME` PROTO_LOCAL env override; positionals are server socket path + prog-and-args. **s6-ipcserver** (all-in-one UNIX-domain UCSPI server superdaemon: binds, listens, accepts, and spawns prog per connection — composes the work of s6-ipcserver-socketbinder + s6-ipcserverd in a single binary) — 16 flags + 2 positionals: **3-way mutex verbosity** `-q`/`-Q`/`-v`, **2-way mutex `-d`/`-D` SO_REUSEADDR** (default-set xor unset), **2-way mutex `-P`/`-p` peer-credentials lookup** (P=no-lookup xor p=lookup-default), `-1` readiness, `-c MAXCONN` total connections (default 40), `-C LOCALMAXCONN` per-peer-uid connections (default 40), `-b BACKLOG` listen backlog, `-a PERMS` octal socket perms (default 0700), `-u UID` / `-g GID` / `-G GID,GID,...` privilege drop, `-U` ucspi env mode; positionals are socket path + prog-and-args. **s6-ipcserver-access** (access-control filter: invoked under s6-ipcserver, consults an access-rules db, denies or allows the peer, then chain-loads prog if allowed) — 6 flags + variadic positional: `-v VERB` verbosity, **2-way mutex `-e`/`-E` default-allow xor default-deny-default**, `-l LOCALNAME` PROTO_LOCAL override, **2-way mutex `-i RULESDIR` xor `-x RULESFILE`** access-rules backing store; positional is prog-and-args. **s6-ipcserver-socketbinder** (socket-binding half of the s6-ipcserver pipeline: binds path, optionally listens, then chain-loads prog with the bound socket on fd 0) — 6 flags + 2 positionals: **2-way mutex `-d`/`-D` SO_REUSEADDR**, **2-way mutex `-M`/`-m` SOCK_STREAM-default xor SOCK_DGRAM**, `-B` bind-only-no-listen, `-b BACKLOG`, `-a PERMS`; positionals are socket path + prog-and-args. **s6-ipcserverd** (accept-loop half of the s6-ipcserver pipeline: expects a bound listen() socket on fd 0, typically piped in from s6-ipcserver-socketbinder, and spawns prog per connection) — 5 flags + variadic positional: `-v VERB`, `-1` readiness, **2-way mutex `-P`/`-p` peer-credentials lookup**, `-c MAXCONN`, `-C LOCALMAXCONN`; positional is prog-and-args. **Hunt-skip log this round**: s6-sudo/s6-sudoc/s6-sudod (s6 UCSPI-sudo family in src/conn-tools — discovered via gh api; 3-stem multi-binary candidate for R122+), s6-accessrules-cdb-from-fs/s6-accessrules-fs-from-cdb (s6 access-rules conversion utilities — sister tools to the `-i RULESDIR`/`-x RULESFILE` flags in s6-ipcserver-access; 2-stem candidate for R122+), s6-connlimit/s6-ioconnect (s6 connection rate-limiting and bidirectional pipe utilities — deferred for a misc R123+ round). **Blacklist additions (5)**: 5 entries in the `s6-ipc*` range. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 126th consecutive clean round.
- **Skarnet s6 fdholder server R120 — s6-fdholder-daemon/s6-fdholder-delete/s6-fdholder-getdump/s6-fdholder-setdump/s6-fdholder-transferdump/s6-fdholderd (6-stem multi-binary)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surface extracted source-direct from upstream skarnet/s6 [`src/fdholder/s6-fdholder-{daemon,delete,getdump,setdump,transferdump}.c`](https://github.com/skarnet/s6/tree/master/src/fdholder) + [`src/fdholder/s6-fdholderd.c`](https://github.com/skarnet/s6/tree/master/src/fdholder/s6-fdholderd.c) USAGE strings + `subgetopt_r` option-string specs via `gh api`. Single multi-stem file `_s6-fdholder-daemon` is `#compdef s6-fdholder-daemon s6-fdholder-delete s6-fdholder-getdump s6-fdholder-setdump s6-fdholder-transferdump s6-fdholderd`. **Coverage**: 6-stem multi-binary harvest covering the s6 file-descriptor holder server-side binaries plus the atomic dump-management family — sister tools to R117's `_s6-fdholder-list` (client-side: s6-fdholder-list/store/retrieve). The fd-holder server pattern lets unrelated processes exchange live OS file descriptors (sockets, pipes, ttys) across an s6 supervised process tree via UNIX-domain socket protocol. **Per-binary surface**: **s6-fdholder-daemon** (long-lived listener variant — opens its own listening socket and runs the s6-fdholderd protocol engine) — 14 flags + 1 positional: shared `-v VERBOSITY` / `-1` (notify-readiness on fd-1) / `-c MAXCONN` (default 16) / `-n MAXFDS` (default 1000) / `-i RULESDIR` xor `-x RULESFILE` (mutex access-rules) / `-t MS` (per-client timeout) / `-T MS` (lameduck shutdown timeout); plus daemon-specific `-d` xor `-D` (daemonize-default xor stay-foreground mutex) / `-b BACKLOG` (listen backlog) / `-u UID` / `-g GID` / `-G GID,GID,...` (supplementary gids) / `-U` (ucspi mode); positional is socket path. **s6-fdholderd** (UCSPI-mode kernel of the fdholder server — designed to be invoked under `s6-ipcserver` / `s6-ipcserverd` with a connected client already on the protocol fds) — 8 flags + no positionals: the shared server-flag subset only (no listen-socket / daemonize / drop-privs flags, since those concerns are delegated to the wrapping ucspi server). **s6-fdholder-delete** (delete a held fd from the server by id) — 1 flag + 2 positionals: `-t MS` operation timeout; positionals are socket + descriptor id. **s6-fdholder-getdump** (atomically retrieve ALL held fds + ids from a running fdholder server, then chain-load prog with those fds/ids in environment — used by s6-rc to snapshot live socket state for restart-as-same-server) — 1 flag + variadic positionals: `-t MS` timeout; positionals are socket + prog-and-args. **s6-fdholder-setdump** (atomically load a dump of fds+ids from stdin into a fresh fdholder server — paired with the prior `getdump`) — 1 flag + 1 positional: `-t MS` timeout; positional is socket. **s6-fdholder-transferdump** (atomically migrate all held fds from one fdholder server `socketfrom` to another `socketto`; combines getdump + setdump in a single hot-handoff) — 1 flag + 2 positionals: `-t TIMEOUTFROM:TIMEOUTTO` (compound colon-separated timeout pair, one per endpoint); positionals are source + destination socket paths. Reusable helper array `_s6_fdh_server_flags` shared between s6-fdholder-daemon and s6-fdholderd (8 common server-config flags). **Hunt-skip log this round**: s6-ipcserver/s6-ipcserver-access/s6-ipcserver-socketbinder/s6-ipcserverd/s6-tcpserver4d/s6-tcpserver6d (R118/R119 carryforward; s6-networking server family), s6-ioconnect/s6-format-filter/s6-permafailon/s6-permafailon01 (R118/R119 carryforward), s6-accessrules-cdb-from-fs/s6-accessrules-fs-from-cdb (s6 access-rules conversion utilities — discovered via `gh api repos/skarnet/s6/contents/src/conn-tools`; deferred for a dedicated round). **Blacklist additions (6)**: 6 entries in the `s6-fd*` range. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 125th consecutive clean round.
- **Skarnet s6 ftrig family R119 — s6-ftrig-listen/s6-ftrig-listen1/s6-ftrig-notify/s6-ftrig-wait/s6-ftrigrd (5-stem multi-binary)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surface extracted source-direct from upstream skarnet/s6 [`src/pipe-tools/s6-ftrig-{listen,listen1,notify,wait}.c`](https://github.com/skarnet/s6/tree/master/src/pipe-tools) USAGE strings and [`src/libs6/s6-ftrigrd.c`](https://github.com/skarnet/s6/tree/master/src/libs6) `main()` signature via `gh api repos/skarnet/s6/contents`. Single multi-stem file `_s6-ftrig-listen` is `#compdef s6-ftrig-listen s6-ftrig-listen1 s6-ftrig-notify s6-ftrig-wait s6-ftrigrd`. **Coverage**: 5-stem multi-binary harvest covering the s6 fifodir event-trigger CLI family — the consumer half of the fifodir IPC primitive whose producer half (`s6-mkfifodir` / `s6-cleanfifodir`) was covered in R118's `_s6-envdir`. **Per-binary surface**: **s6-ftrig-listen** (chain-load prog after matching events on multiple (fifodir, regexp) pairs) — 3 flags + variadic positionals: **2-way mutex match-mode** `-a` conjunction (default; all pairs must match) xor `-o` disjunction (any single pair matches), `-t MS` timeout in milliseconds; positionals are alternating fifodir/regexp pairs terminated by empty string `""` followed by prog-and-args. **s6-ftrig-listen1** (single-pair variant of s6-ftrig-listen) — 1 flag + 3 positionals: `-t MS` timeout; positionals are fifodir + event regexp + prog-and-args (does chain-load prog after match). **s6-ftrig-notify** (emit each character of message as a separate event into fifodir; null character 0x00 cannot be transmitted) — no flags + 2 positionals: fifodir + event message string. **s6-ftrig-wait** (single-pair wait variant of s6-ftrig-listen1; does NOT chain-load any program after match) — 1 flag + 2 positionals: `-t MS` timeout; positionals are fifodir + event regexp. **s6-ftrigrd** (internal s6 fifodir-trigger server daemon spawned by libs6 `ftrigr_start`/`ftrigr_startf`; not directly invoked by users) — no CLI arguments (`main(void)` signature in source); reads requests via the skalibs SASS server protocol on stdin/stdout. **Hunt-skip log this round**: s6-fdholder-daemon/s6-fdholder-delete/s6-fdholder-getdump/s6-fdholder-setdump/s6-fdholder-transferdump/s6-fdholderd (R117 ext — 6 additional s6-fdholder server-side and dump-management binaries discovered via `gh api repos/skarnet/s6/contents/src/fdholder`; deferred for a dedicated R120+ round), s6-ipcserver/s6-ipcserver-access/s6-ipcserver-socketbinder/s6-ipcserverd/s6-tcpserver4d/s6-tcpserver6d (R118 deferral; s6-networking server family), s6-ioconnect/s6-format-filter/s6-permafailon/s6-permafailon01 (R118 deferral; more s6 utility binaries). **Blacklist additions (5)**: 5 entries in the `s6-f*` range between `s6-envuidgid` and `s6-mkfifodir`. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 124th consecutive clean round.
- **Skarnet s6 utilities R118 — s6-envdir/s6-setlock/s6-fghack/s6-mkfifodir/s6-cleanfifodir (5-stem multi-binary)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surface transcribed directly from upstream skarnet.org documentation at [skarnet.org/software/s6/s6-{envdir,setlock,fghack,mkfifodir,cleanfifodir}.html](https://skarnet.org/software/s6/) via WebFetch. Single multi-stem file `_s6-envdir` is `#compdef s6-envdir s6-setlock s6-fghack s6-mkfifodir s6-cleanfifodir`. **Coverage**: 5-stem multi-binary harvest covering core s6 chain-loaded process-management utilities. Sister tools to R117's s6-fdholder family. **Per-binary surface**: **s6-envdir** (set environment variables from a directory of files then chain-exec prog) — 5 flags + 2 positionals: `-i`/`-I` strict-mode toggle (strict=default exits 111 if dir missing; loose=chain-exec unchanged), `-n` preserve trailing whitespace, `-f` verbatim file content as value, `-L` remove 4096-byte per-file read limit, `-c NULLIS` replace nulls with first char of NULLIS string; positionals are env directory + prog-and-args. **s6-setlock** (acquire advisory lock then chain-exec prog) — 6 flags + 2 positionals: **3-way mutex lock-acquisition mode** `-n` nonblocking xor `-N` blocking (default) xor `-t MS` timed; **2-way mutex lock-type** `-r` shared xor `-w` exclusive (default); `-d FD` expose lock on file descriptor; positionals are lock file + prog-and-args. **s6-fghack** (open many file descriptors all writing to a single pipe then spawn prog as child — detects process backgrounding in supervised services where missing this hack causes spurious service-down reports) — no flags; just positional prog-and-args. **s6-mkfifodir** (create a fifodir — directory containing a control FIFO used by the s6-ftrig family for event notification) — 2 flags + 1 positional: `-f` force/reset permissions on existing fifodir, `-g GID` restrict listenability to GID group members; positional is fifodir path. **s6-cleanfifodir** (garbage-collect dead listeners from a fifodir) — no CLI options; positional fifodir path (must be owned by the current user). **Hunt-skip log this round**: s6-ftrigr-list/s6-ftrigrd/s6-ftrig-listen/s6-ftrig-notify/s6-ftrig-wait (s6-ftrig event-notification family — uses fifodirs created by s6-mkfifodir; deferred for separate ftrig-focused round), s6-ipcserver/s6-ipcserver-access/s6-ipcserver-socketbinder/s6-ipcserverd/s6-tcpserver4d/s6-tcpserver6d (s6-networking server family — deferred), s6-ioconnect/s6-format-filter/s6-permafailon/s6-permafailon01 (more utility binaries — deferred for completeness round). **Blacklist additions (5)**: alphabetically distributed across the s6-c*/s6-e*/s6-f*/s6-m*/s6-s* ranges. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 123rd consecutive clean round.
- **Skarnet s6 fdholder R117 — s6-fdholder-list/store/retrieve (3-stem multi-binary; s6 fd-holder client tools)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surface transcribed directly from upstream Skarnet documentation at [skarnet.org/software/s6/s6-fdholder-{list,store,retrieve}.html](https://skarnet.org/software/s6/) via WebFetch. Single multi-stem file `_s6-fdholder-list` is `#compdef s6-fdholder-list s6-fdholder-store s6-fdholder-retrieve`. **Coverage**: 3-stem multi-binary harvest covering the s6 file-descriptor holder client utilities. Each communicates with an `s6-fdholderd` daemon via UNIX socket — useful for passing live file descriptors (sockets, pipes) across unrelated processes in s6-init / s6-rc supervised process trees. Sister tools to the already-covered s6-svc / s6-svstat / s6-svok / s6-svscan service manager family. **Per-binary surface**: **s6-fdholder-store** (store a file descriptor in the fd-holder daemon under a given id) — 3 flags + 2 positionals: `-d FD` descriptor number to store (default 0), `-T MS` descriptor expiration time, `-t MS` operation timeout; positionals are socket path + descriptor identifier. **s6-fdholder-list** (list all descriptors currently held) — 1 flag + 1 positional: `-t MS` operation timeout (safeguard against wrong socket); positional is fdholder socket path. **s6-fdholder-retrieve** (retrieve a held file descriptor and execute a program with it connected to stdin) — 2 flags + 3 positionals: `-D` delete the descriptor from server storage after retrieval (requires both read and write permissions for the identifier), `-t MS` operation timeout; positionals are socket path + descriptor identifier + program-and-arguments to execute. **Hunt-skip log this round**: fttimer/ftrandom/ftmemchk (R113 ft2demos remaining deferrals — Debian dyn.manpages 404 chain persists; no GitHub mirror of `freetype-demos` source easily accessible via gh api; deferred indefinitely until savannah.nongnu.org mirror is identified), execline binaries (backtick/foreground/if/ifelse/importas/redirfd/pipeline/elglob/loopwhilex/tryexec/withstdinas — Skarnet's shell-replacement family; many names clash with shell builtins or other commands, so completion adds limited value; deferred), s6-rc/runit-init/utmps (s6-rc service-manager + runit-init + utmps — separate research), runsv/runsvchdir/runsvdir/sv (runit family already partially covered). **Blacklist additions (3)**: 3 between `s6-envuidgid` (23338) and `s6-linux-init-maker` (23342) for `s6-fdholder-list`/`s6-fdholder-retrieve`/`s6-fdholder-store`. - **Mozilla WOFF1 R116 — sfnt2woff + woff2sfnt (2-stem multi-binary; original Mozilla WOFF1 zlib variants)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Single multi-stem file `_sfnt2woff` is `#compdef sfnt2woff woff2sfnt`. **Coverage**: 2-stem multi-binary harvest covering the original (non-zopfli) WOFF1 bidirectional converters. **Sister files in this round's WOFF/SFNT family**: `_sfnt2woff-zopfli` from 2026-05-17 covers the bramstein zopfli-recompression variants `sfnt2woff-zopfli` + `woff2sfnt-zopfli`; `_ttf2woff2` from 2026-05-21 covers Google's WOFF2 compressors `ttf2woff2` + `woff2_compress`; `_woff2_decompress` from 2026-05-21 covers Google's WOFF2 decoder. Combined, the **WOFF conversion ecosystem coverage is now 6 binaries across 4 multi-stem files**. **Per-binary surface**: **sfnt2woff** (SFNT → WOFF1 zlib-based compressor) — 4 flags shared with the zopfli variant: `-v MAJOR.MINOR` font version, `-m metadata.xml` (not validated), `-p private.dat` private data block; positional input `*.otf/*.ttf` font. **woff2sfnt** (WOFF1 → SFNT decompressor or single-block extractor) — 3 mutually-exclusive extract modes (only one of `-v`/`-m`/`-p` may be used at a time, source-verified): `-v` write font version to stdout, `-m` write WOFF metadata block to stdout, `-p` write private data block to stdout; positional input `*.woff` file. **Hunt-skip log this round**: 4 of 6 originally-targeted WOFF utilities turned out to be **already covered** with case-sensitivity-aware existing coverage — woff2_compress (covered as part of `_ttf2woff2` multi-stem), woff2_decompress (covered as `_woff2_decompress`), sfnt2woff-zopfli (covered as part of `_sfnt2woff-zopfli` multi-stem), woff2sfnt-zopfli (covered as part of `_sfnt2woff-zopfli` multi-stem); this round adds the only truly fresh 2 (the **original non-zopfli Mozilla** variants). Reaffirms the **scan-by-exact-binary-name discipline** from earlier rounds (snarkos/near-cli-rs/czkawka_cli/featureCounts/etc.). cu2qu/opentype-feature-freezer/ufo2ft/ufoLib2 (libraries or small surfaces; deferred), fttimer/ftrandom/ftpatchk (R113 ft2demos remaining deferrals; still pending). **Blacklist additions (2)**: 1 between `sfltool` (23955) and `sfnt2woff-zopfli` (23957) for `sfnt2woff`; 1 between `woff2_info` (28718) and `woff2sfnt-zopfli` (28720) for `woff2sfnt`. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 121st consecutive clean round.
- **Source Foundry UFO tools R115 — ufodiff + ufolint (2-stem multi-binary; UFO source diff + linter)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surface transcribed directly from upstream READMEs at [github.com/source-foundry/ufodiff](https://github.com/source-foundry/ufodiff) and [github.com/source-foundry/ufolint](https://github.com/source-foundry/ufolint) via WebFetch. Single multi-stem file `_ufodiff` is `#compdef ufodiff ufolint`. **Coverage**: 2-stem multi-binary harvest covering Source Foundry's UFO (Unified Font Object) source-management CLIs — sister tools to the R111 fontmake and R114 fontbakery harvests. **Per-binary surface**: **ufodiff** (UFO source file diff for typeface git workflows; supports UFO versions 2 and 3) — state-machine with **5 subcommands**: `delta` (plain text with `[A]` added / `[D]` deleted / `[M]` modified indicators), `deltajson` (JSON output), `deltamd` (GitHub-flavored Markdown), `diff` (ANSI-colored text diff), `diffnc` (uncolored text diff for non-terminal output). Common syntax pattern: `ufodiff <sub> [all] [commits:N | branch:NAME] [optional UFO filter]` — the **scope-selector positional** uses a colon-separated mini-DSL (`commits:5` for last-5 commits, `branch:master` for branch comparison, `all` for all commits). Plus optional UFO file filter as 2nd positional. **ufolint** (UFO source linter for CI — exits 0 on pass, 1 on any failure) — single-binary CLI with no subcommands; positional `*.ufo` directory paths. Performs static analysis covering: **UFO version compatibility**, **mandatory files and directories**, **file path naming conventions**, **XML file validity**, **plist formatting and values**, **GLIF file format compliance**, **PNG image specifications** (UFO v3+), **library import compatibility**. **Hunt-skip log this round**: cu2qu/cu2qu-cli (cubic-to-quadratic curve converter — likely small surface or library-level), opentype-feature-freezer (small utility), ufo2ft (library not a CLI), ufoLib2/ufolib2 (libraries), woff2_compress/woff2_decompress (separate WOFF2 conversion utilities; deferred), sfnt2woff/woff2sfnt (WOFF1 conversion utilities; deferred), fttimer/ftrandom/ftpatchk (R113 ft2demos remaining deferrals — also still pending). **Blacklist additions (2)**: 2 between `uflow-bpfcc` (27251) and `ufraw` (27254) for `ufodiff`/`ufolint`. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 120th consecutive clean round.
- **fontbakery R114 — fontbakery (1 stem; fontTools font-QA tool)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surface transcribed directly from upstream `Lib/fontbakery/cli.py` at [github.com/fonttools/fontbakery](https://github.com/fonttools/fontbakery) via `gh api` inspection of every `argument_parser.add_argument` call plus the `CLI_PROFILES` list. Single-stem file `_fontbakery` is `#compdef fontbakery`. **Coverage**: fontbakery is the fontTools font QA tool that runs check suites against font binaries with multiple foundry-specific profiles. State-machine with **12 top-level subcommands**: `check-profile` (most flexible — runs an explicit profile module name) plus 11 foundry-specific shortcuts `check_<profile>` where the profile is one of an **11-value enum**: adobefonts/fontbureau/fontval (Microsoft FontVal wrapper)/fontwerk/googlefonts (most-used)/iso15008 (in-vehicle display)/microsoft/notofonts (Google Noto)/opentype (vendor-agnostic spec)/typenetwork/universal (foundry-agnostic). All `check_*` subcommands inherit the same **29-flag shared `_check_flags` helper**: `--configuration FILE` TOML/JSON config, repeatable `*-c/--checkid` whitelist, repeatable `*-x/--exclude-checkid` blacklist, `-v/--verbose` (shortcut for `-l PASS`), repeatable `*-l/--loglevel` with **8-value status enum** (DEBUG/INFO/WARN/PASS/SKIP/FAIL/ERROR/FATAL), `-m/--loglevel-messages`, `--succinct`, `-F/--full-lists`, `-S/--show-sections`, `-g/--gather-by` 4-value enum (font/family/glyph/iso15008_section), `-o/--order` 4-value enum (same), `-q/--quiet`, `-n/--no-progress`, `-C/--no-colors`, **theme toggle** `--dark-theme` xor `--light-theme`, `--timeout SEC`, `--skip-network` (offline mode), **4 report-format outputs** `--json FILE`/`--badges DIR`/`--ghmarkdown FILE`/`--html FILE`, `-J/--jobs N` (0=auto), `-j/--auto-jobs` (shortcut for `--jobs=0`), `-e/--error-code-on` exit-code-on-status. Top-level flags: `--list-subcommands`, `-L/--list-checks`. **Hunt-skip log this round**: ufodiff/ufolint/ufolib2 (separate UFO inspection/validation utilities; ufoLib2 is the Python library not a CLI), cu2qu/cu2qu-cli (cubic-to-quadratic curve converter — likely small surface or library-level), opentype-feature-freezer (small utility), fonttools-cli (fontTools umbrella project's CLI dispatcher — actual binaries are `ttx`/`pyftsubset`/`pyftmerge`/`pyftinspect`; ttx already covered, others deferred), sfnt2woff/woff2sfnt and woff2_compress/woff2_decompress (WOFF conversion utilities — separate vendor tools; deferred), ufo2ft (library not a CLI), fttimer/ftrandom/ftpatchk (R113 ft2demos remaining deferrals). **Blacklist additions (1)**: 1 between `font_cache` (8400) and `fontforge` (8402) for `fontbakery`. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 119th consecutive clean round.
- **FreeType ft2demos extras R113 — ftdump/ftstring/ftdiff/ftlint/ftmulti (5-stem; ft2demos completion)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Single multi-stem file `_ftdump` is `#compdef ftdump ftstring ftdiff ftlint ftmulti`. **Coverage**: 5-stem multi-binary harvest **resolving the R112 ft2demos extras deferral**. Combined with R112's 4-stem `_ftview`, the FreeType ft2demos coverage is now **9 stems across 2 multi-stem files** (`_ftview` ftview/ftvalid/ftbench/ftgrid + `_ftdump` ftdump/ftstring/ftdiff/ftlint/ftmulti). **Per-binary surface**: **ftdump** (simple font dumper — print font file information relevant to FreeType) — 6 flags: `-c/-C` charmap coverage, `-n` SFNT name tables, `-p` TrueType programs, `-t` SFNT table list, `-u` emit UTF-8, `-v` version. **ftstring** (interactive string renderer) — 6 flags: `-d WxH[xD]` window dimensions (default 640x480x24), `-r` dpi (default 72), `-e` encoding 4-value enum (unic/symb/ADOB/ADBC), `-m` custom text, `-k` keystroke emulation (`q` = batch mode), `-v` version; positional point size + font file. **ftdiff** (display text in 3 columns with different hinting modes per column — useful for comparing hinting strategies) — 6 flags: `-w` window width default 640px, `-h` window height default 480px, `-r` dpi default 72, `-s` character size default 16pt, `-f UTF8_TEXT_FILE` custom content, `-v` version. **ftlint** (lint a font — check for FreeType loading issues across glyphs) — 5 flags: `-f HEX` FT_LOAD_XXX load flags (default 0), `-r` 5-value render-mode enum (0=normal/1=light/2=mono/3=LCD-horizontal/4=LCD-vertical), `-i I-J` glyph index range (default all), `-q` quiet mode, `-v` version; positional ppem + font file. **ftmulti** (interactive viewer for variation fonts — Multiple Masters / GX / OpenType variations) — 7 flags: `-w/-h` window dimensions, `-e` encoding 4-value enum, `-r` dpi, `-f` first glyph index, **`-d "axis1 axis2 ..."`** variation-font axis design coordinates (distinguishing this binary as the GX/MM-specific viewer vs ftgrid which has the same axis flag with implied `-n`), `-v` version. **Hunt-skip log this round**: ftchkwd (man page redirect chain via dyn.manpages.debian.org returns 404; deferred), ftmemchk (memory-check internal tool, deferred), fttimer (small timer demo, deferred), ftpatchk (patcher check, deferred), ftrandom (random font subset tester, deferred), ftvalid_internal (internal validator, not user-facing). **Blacklist additions (5)**: 2 between `ftdi_eeprom` (8657) and `ftdv` (8660) for `ftdiff`/`ftdump`; 2 between `ftgrid` (8663) and `ftp` (8666) for `ftlint`/`ftmulti`; 1 between `ftpd` (8668) and `ftvalid` (8670) for `ftstring`. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 118th consecutive clean round.
- **FreeType ft2demos R112 — ftview/ftvalid/ftbench/ftgrid (4-stem multi-binary; FreeType demo CLIs)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surface transcribed directly from upstream FreeType ft2demos man pages at [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/freetype2-demos/](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/freetype2-demos/) via WebFetch of `ft{view,valid,bench,grid}.1.en.html`. Single multi-stem file `_ftview` is `#compdef ftview ftvalid ftbench ftgrid`. **Coverage**: 4-stem multi-binary harvest of FreeType demo CLIs. **Resolves R111 deferral**. **Per-binary surface**: **ftview** (interactive glyph viewer over all glyphs of a font) — 9 flags: `-d WxH[xD]` window dimensions (default 640x480x24), `-r` dpi (default 72), `-f` first index, `-e` encoding 4-value enum (unic/symb/ADOB/ADBC), `-m` render text, `-l` startup rendering mode 0-6, `-L` LCD filter weights, `-p` preload, `-k` emulate keystrokes; positional point size + font file. **ftvalid** (OpenType layout table validator) — 6 flags: `-f` font index, `-t` 3-value validator enum (ot/gx/ckern), `-T` SFNT table tags (colon-separated) or ckern dialect (ms/apple), `-l` list layout tables, `-V` 3-value strictness enum (0=default/1=tight/2=paranoid), `-v` version. **ftbench** (benchmark common FreeType operations) — 12 flags incl. repeatable `*-b` test selector with **12-value enum** (a=load-glyphs/b=advance-widths/c=render-glyphs/d=get-glyphs/e=char-indices/f=iterate-CMap/g=open-face/h=embolden/i=stroke/j=bboxes/k=cboxes/l=open+load), `-c` max iterations (0=time-limited), `-t` time-limit sec (default 2), `-f` load flags hex, `-s` face size ppem (default 10), `-i I-J` glyph index range, `-r` 5-value render-mode enum (0=normal/1=light/2=mono/3=LCD-horizontal/4=LCD-vertical), `-H` CFF hinting engine, `-I` TrueType interpreter version, `-m` max cache size KiB (default 1024), `-p` preload, `-C` compare with cached. **ftgrid** (inspect glyphs on a grid; variable-font axis aware) — 8 flags: `-d WxH[xD]`, `-r` dpi, `-f` first index, `-e` encoding 4-value enum, **variable-font specific** `-a "axis1 axis2 ..."` axis coordinates (implies `-n`), `-n` don't display named instances of variation fonts, `-k` emulate keystrokes, `-v` version. **Hunt-skip log this round**: ftdump/ftstring/ftmemchk/ftlint/fttimer/ftdiff/ftchkwd/ftmulti (additional ft2demos binaries — these tools exist in the ft2demos package but were not in my candidate list this round; queued for separate ft2demos-completion round to capture the full set), font-info/ttf-tools (deferred — fontTools-bundled scripts), gulim2bdf/otf2bdf/mkfontscale (small font conversion utilities, deferred). **Blacklist additions (4)**: 1 between `ft2nfdump` (8655) and `ftdi_eeprom` (8656) for `ftbench`; 1 between `ftest` (8660) and `ftp` (8661) for `ftgrid`; 2 between `ftpd` (8664) and `fuck` (8666) for `ftvalid`/`ftview`. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 117th consecutive clean round.

output is first positional, input files are repeatable positionals). **parquet-schema** (print schema + metadata) — `-v/--verbose` for full metadata, positional file. **parquet-fromcsv** (CSV → Parquet — 15 flags incl. `-s/--schema FILE`, `-i/--input-file`, `-o/--output-file`, `-f/--input-format` 2-value enum (csv/tsv), `-b/--batch-size`, `--has-header`, `-d/--delimiter`, `-r/--record-terminator` 2-value enum (lf/crlf), `-e/--escape-char`, `-q/--quote-char`, `-D/--double-quote`, `-C/--csv-compression`, `-c/--parquet-compression` default snappy, `-w/--writer-version` 2-value enum, `-m/--max-row-group-size`. **parquet-rowcount** (return row count for ≥1 files; positional files). **parquet-layout** (print physical layout — row groups, column chunks, pages). **parquet-index** (print page index for a specific column — 2 positionals: file + column name). **parquet-show-bloom-filter** (read bloom-filter data; 3 positionals: file + column + values). **Hunt-skip log this round**: chdb-cli (ClickHouse-style fork of CHDB; deferred — separate research), arrow-cli (no `apache/arrow-cli` repo; the Arrow project does not ship a single CLI binary by that name), arrow-flight-sql (RPC layer, not a CLI), q-cli/qsv (deferred), parq/parquet-go (alternative parquet implementations in Python and Go; share fastq-dump's spot/filter/output flags via the shared build setup) — 8 flags incl. `-A/--accession`, `-O/--outdir`, `-Z/--stdout`, `-N/-X` spot range, `--gzip/--bzip2`. **srapath** (resolve NCBI repository paths/URLs for SRA accessions) — 14 flags verified via `srapath.c` defines: `-a/--protocol` 5-value enum (http/https/fasp/gs/s3), `-c/--cache`, `--perm` permissions/cart, `-d/--project N`, `-e/--vers`, `-f/--function` 4-value enum (names/resolve/search/srapath), `--location`, `--ngc`, `-P/--path` path-style only, `-p/--param`, `-r/--raw`, `-j/--json`, `-t/--timeout SEC`, `-u/--url URL`. **sra-pileup** (samtools-style pileup directly from an SRA accession) — 12 flags: `-r/--aligned-region chr:from-to`, `-o/--outfile`, `-t/--table` 3-value enum (p/s/e for primary/secondary/evidence), `-q/--minmapq`, `-Q/--minbasequal`, `-d/--duplicates`, `--noskip`, `--showid`, `-e/--seqname`, `-n/--noqual`. **sra-info** (print SRA accession info — schema/columns/rows/sizes) — 8 flags: `-f/--format` 6-value enum (default/csv/xml/json/tab/piped), `-r/--rows`, `-l/--limit`, `--platform`, `--meta`, `--schema`, `--total`. **kdbmeta** (examine/dump VDB metadata nodes) — 5 flags: `-T/--table`, `-X/--output-format` 4-value enum (xml/json/csv/tab), `-A/--as-attributes`, `-U/--tree`, positional node path. **rcexplain** (explain ncbi-vdb / sra-tools return-code values — useful for debugging) — just `_common_kapp` + positional decimal return code. **Hunt-skip log this round**: bam-loader/cg-load/sra-load/sra-sort/fastq-loader/pacbio-load/general-loader/vdb-lock/vdb-unlock/sharq (9 loader binaries in `tools/loaders/`; deferred — heavier specialized surfaces best handled in a dedicated loader-focused round), ngs-pileup (legacy pileup variant — sra-pileup is the modern equivalent and is covered here), ref-variation (reference-variation utility — separate research), test-sra (test harness, not user-facing), driver-tool (internal toolkit driver). **Blacklist additions (9)**: alphabetically distributed. `--no-user-settings`) — extracted into a `_common_kapp` helper. **Per-binary surface**: **prefetch** (retrieve SRA accessions/kart files/URLs) — 17 flags incl. `--cart`/`--text-kart` kart input, (http/fasp/both), `-l/--location` cloud, `--type` 3-value enum (sra/refseq/all), `--eliminate-quals`, `--ascp-options`, `-p/--progress`, `-c/--check-all`, `--check-rs`. **fastq-dump** (legacy SRA → FASTQ; superseded by fasterq-dump) — 22 flags incl. split modes (`--split-spot/--split-files/--split-3`), FASTA output, color-space toggle (`-B/-C`), read IDs (`-I/-F`), Phred offset (`-Q`), filters (`--skip-technical/--read-filter` 4-enum pass/reject/criteria/redacted, `-W/--clip`, `-M/-N/-X` minRead/minSpot/maxSpot, `--aligned/--unaligned`), output (`-O/-Z/--gzip/--bzip2`). **fasterq-dump** (multi-threaded SRA → FASTQ replacement) — 22 flags incl. `-O/-o/-t` output/temp paths, `-f` force, `-e N` threads (default 6), `-b/-c/-m` buffer/cursor/memory sizes, split modes including `--concatenate-reads`, `--fasta`/`--fasta-unsorted`/`--fasta-ref-tbl`, `--seq-defline`/`--qual-defline` custom formats, `--ngc`, `--size-check` 3-value enum (on/off/only), `--disk-limit`/`--disk-limit-tmp`, `--table SEQUENCE` for PacBio. **vdb-dump** (dump VDB / SRA contents in textual form) — 12 flags incl. `-T/--table`, `-C/--columns`, `-R/--rows`, `-f/--format` **14-value enum** (csv/xml/json/piped/tab/fastq/fastq1/fasta/fasta1/fasta2/qual/qual1/hidden/tab1), `-d/--boolean` 2-enum (1/T), `-A/--schema_dump`, `-E/--table_enum`, `-O/--column_enum`. **sam-dump** (dump aligned SRA → SAM/BAM) — 15 flags incl. `-u/--unaligned`, `-1/--primary`, `-c/--cigar-long`, `-r/--header` 2-enum (add/no), `--header-file`/`--header-comment`, `-n/--no-header`, `-s/--seqid`, `-d/--member-stats`, `-b/--bases`, `-m/--meta`, `-p/--progress`. **vdb-validate** (validate SRA structure) — 6 flags incl. `-Q/--table`, `-x/--exhaustive`, `-r/--referential-integrity`, `-B/--consist-check`, `-I/--index`, `-C/--md5-check`. **vdb-config** (configure SRA toolkit) — 11 flags incl. `--cfg`, `-a/--all`, `-p/--proxy URL`, `--proxy-disable`, `--set KEY=VALUE`, `-w/--wd`, `--restore-defaults`, `--root`, `--cfg-dir`, `--fix-default`, `--cloud-provider` 3-value enum (aws/gcp/azure), `-i/--import-ngc`. **vdb-encrypt** / **vdb-decrypt** (legacy NGC-style file encryption) — `-d/-f/-p/-q` for encrypt; `-f/-p` for decrypt. **Hunt-skip log this round**: abi-dump/sff-dump/illumina-dump (legacy format-specific dumpers — less commonly used in modern workflows; deferred for
