- **Subread utility helpers R103 — propmapped/flattenGTF/removeDup/repair (4-stem multi-binary; auxiliary Subread tools)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surface transcribed directly from upstream Subread package man pages at [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/subread/](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/subread/) via WebFetch of `{propmapped,flattenGTF,removeDup,repair}.1.en.html`. Single multi-stem file `_propmapped` is `#compdef propmapped flattenGTF removeDup repair`. **Coverage**: 4-stem multi-binary harvest **completing the R102 deferral** on small Subread auxiliary binaries. Sister tools to the R102-covered aligners (`subread-align`/`subjunc`/`subread-buildindex`/`exactSNP`/`sublong` via `_subread-align`) and the existing `_featureCounts` (the read-counter from this same package). **Per-binary surface**: **propmapped** (calculate the proportion of mapped reads/fragments in a SAM/BAM file) — 4 flags: `-i FILE` (required SAM/BAM), `-o FILE` (stats output), `-f` (count fragments instead of reads, paired-end only), `-p` (only properly paired reads, paired-end only). **flattenGTF** (flatten a GTF/GFF annotation by merging overlapping exons of the same gene into a non-overlapping set; used as a featureCounts preprocessing step) — 5 flags: `-a FILE` (required input annotation), `-o FILE` (required output), `-t TYPE` (feature type default `exon`), `-g ATTR` (group-by attribute default `gene_id`), `-C` (alternative mode that merges into multiple non-overlapping exons but keeps all edges instead of collapsing them — useful for exon-level analyses). **removeDup** (remove duplicate alignments by location-frequency threshold — different from samtools markdup; targets PCR/optical duplicates by counting reads mapping to identical locations) — 5 flags: `-i/-o` required, `-S` SAM output (BAM default), `-r N` duplication threshold (default 10; locations with ≥N hits removed), `-t DIR` temp directory. **repair** (pair-up reads from the same pair so they are adjacent in the output; for downstream featureCounts paired-end analysis after a coordinate-sorted BAM is needed) — 7 flags: `-i/-o` required, `-S` SAM input, `-c` compress output BAM (slower read access), `-T N` threads (default **8** — higher than most Subread tools' default 1), `-d` skip dummy reads for singletons, `-t` omit sequences and quality scores from output. **Hunt-skip log this round**: subindel man page still not located via Debian manpages (the binary exists in Bioconductor Rsubread but not the apt-shipped subread package); subread NOT a real binary (the package name; actual aligner is subread-align — re-noted from R102). **Blacklist additions (4)**: 1 between `prophet` (20977) and `proselint` (20979) for `propmapped`; 1 between `flatpak-spawn` (8273) and `flawfinder` (8275) for `flattenGTF`; 1 between `remove-duplicates` (22470) and `removeSpaces.sh` (22472) for `removeDup`; 1 between `reordercap` (22490) and `repairHomePermissions` (22492) for `repair`. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 108th consecutive clean round. The Subread / featureCounts / Bowtie2 / HISAT2 / RAxML / BEAST 2 / MMseqs2 / HTSeq bioinformatics ecosystem coverage is now ~50 binaries spanning 8 multi-stem files + 5 individual files.
- **Subread suite R102 — 5-stem (subread-align/subread-buildindex/subjunc/exactSNP/sublong; RNA-seq + DNA-seq + SNP-calling alignment toolkit)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surface transcribed directly from upstream Subread package man pages at [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/subread/](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/subread/) via WebFetch of `{subread-align,subread-buildindex,subjunc,exactSNP,sublong}.1.en.html`. Single multi-stem file `_subread-align` is `#compdef subread-align subread-buildindex subjunc exactSNP sublong`. **Coverage**: 5-stem multi-binary harvest of the Subread read alignment / SNP-calling / index-building toolkit. Existing coverage: `featureCounts` (the read-counter sister tool from this same package, `more_src/_featureCounts` since 2026-05-17). Subread-align and subjunc share substantial flag patterns since subjunc is a junction-aware extension of subread-align — captured via a 33-entry `_shared_align_flags` helper array. **Per-binary surface**: **subread-align** (main Subread aligner for both RNA-seq and DNA-seq) — shared aligner flags + `-t` 2-value data-type enum (0=RNA-seq/1=genomic DNA-seq), Dynamic Programming alignment tuning (`--DPGapOpen`/`--DPGapExt`/`--DPMismatch`/`--DPMatch`), `--sv` structural-variant detection. **subjunc** (junction-aware variant for RNA-seq with exon-exon junction + fusion detection) — shared aligner flags + `--allJunctions` for both junctions+fusions; subjunc's `-n` default is 14 (vs 10 for subread-align) and `-m` default is 1 (vs 3). **subread-buildindex** (build a Subread index from FASTA) — `-o BASENAME` (required), `-F` full index (16bp subreads from every position), `-B` one-block index for max mapping speed, `-M MB` memory (default 8000), `-f N` uninformative-subread threshold (default 100), `-c` color-space index. **exactSNP** (SNP caller from SAM/BAM → VCF) — `-i/-g/-o` required, `-a` annotated SNPs for improved calling, `-b` BAM input, `-Q N` Q-value cutoff (default 12), `-f F` min mismatch fraction, `-n/-r/-x/-s/-t` mapping/coverage/depth/quality/trim thresholds, `-C` temp-dir, `-T` threads. **sublong** (long-read aligner for Nanopore/PacBio) — index must be a full+single-block index (i.e. built with `subread-buildindex -F -B`); just 7 flags: `-i/-r/-o` required, `--SAMoutput`, `-T` threads, `-X` RNA-seq mode, `-v` version. **Shared `_shared_align_flags` helper** captures: index/reads/output (`-i/-r/-o/-R`), I/O format toggles (`--SAMinput/--BAMinput/--SAMoutput`), quality/Phred (`-P` 33|64), mapping thresholds (`-n/-m/-p/-M`), multi-mapping (`--multiMapping/-B`), indel detection (`-I/--complexIndels`), read trimming (`--trim5/--trim3`), paired-end config (`-d/-D/-S` ff|fr|rf), performance (`-T`), read-group (`--rg-id/--rg`), output ordering (`--keepReadOrder/--sortReadsByCoordinates`), color-space (`-b`), and annotation flags (`-a/-F/-A/--gtfFeature/--gtfAttr`). **Hunt-skip log this round**: subindel (man page not located at manpages.debian.org subread path; deferred — likely shares subread-align flag patterns), propmapped/flattenGTF/removeDup/repair (4 small Subread utility binaries — verified as present in subread package but minimal/undocumented flag surfaces; deferred for a future low-priority round). subread (NOT a real binary — the package name is "subread" but the actual aligner binary is "subread-align"; verified by upstream man pages). **Blacklist additions (5)**: 2 between `subnetcalc` (25256) and `subrepo` (25259) for `subread-align`/`subread-buildindex`; 1 between `subfinder` (25248) and `subl` (25250) for `subjunc`; 1 between `exabgp` (7668) and `exaile` (7670) for `exactSNP`; 1 between `subliminal` (25254) and `subnetcalc` (25256) for `sublong`. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 107th consecutive clean round.
- **BEAST 2 R101 — 14-stem Bayesian phylogenetic family (beast/beauti/treeannotator/logcombiner/densitree/applauncher/packagemanager + `2` parallel-install variants)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surface transcribed directly from upstream `src/beast/app/beastapp/BeastMain.java` at [github.com/CompEvol/BEAST.app](https://github.com/CompEvol/BEAST.app) plus GUI helpers at [github.com/CompEvol/BeastFX](https://github.com/CompEvol/BeastFX) via `gh api` inspection of the `new Arguments.Option[]` array. Single multi-stem file `_beast` is `#compdef beast beast2 beauti beauti2 treeannotator treeannotator2 logcombiner logcombiner2 densitree densitree2 applauncher applauncher2 packagemanager packagemanager2`. **Coverage**: 14-stem multi-binary harvest of BEAST 2's Bayesian phylogenetic family. The `2` suffix variants exist because some installers ship both `beast` and `beast2` (or `treeannotator`/`treeannotator2`) as parallel binaries to coexist with BEAST 1.x; both variants share the same CLI surface per stem. **Per-binary surface**: **beast / beast2** (main MCMC engine — read XML, run MCMC, write log/tree files; uses jam Arguments parser with **single-dash long options**) — 29 flags incl. `-window` GUI console, `-options` options dialog, `-working` chdir, `-seed N`, `-prefix`, `-statefile`, `-overwrite` xor `-resume` xor `-validate`, `-threads N` (-1 = all cores), `-instances N` (divide site patterns), `-java` (no native), `-noerr`, `-loglevel` 5-value enum (error/warning/info/debug/trace), **BEAGLE library integration** (`-beagle`, `-beagle_info`, `-beagle_order`, `-beagle_CPU`/`_GPU`/`_SSE`, `-beagle_single`/`_double` precision, `-beagle_scaling` 4-value enum default/none/dynamic/always), `-strictversions`, `*-D` XML attribute substitution (repeatable, e.g. `-D "arg1=10,arg2=20"`), `-DF FILE` substitution-pairs file, `-DFout FILE` output XML, `-sampleFromPrior`. **beauti / beauti2** (BEAST 2 XML builder GUI; CLI side accepts `-template`/`-prefix`/`-out`/`-create` headless mode + positional NEXUS/FASTA input). **treeannotator / treeannotator2** (summarize tree set → MCC tree) — `-burnin PCT` or `-burninTrees N`, `-limit P` posterior probability limit, `-heights` 4-value enum (keep/median/mean/ca = Common Ancestor heights), `-target FILE` user target tree, 2 positionals (input trees + output annotated tree). **logcombiner / logcombiner2** (combine multiple BEAST trace/tree files) — repeatable `*-log`/`*-burnin`, `-resample N`, `-renumber`, `-decimal`, `-scale FACTOR`, `-strip` annotations, `-o FILE`. **densitree / densitree2** (visualizer overlaying all posterior trees) — `-fontfile`, `-out FILE` (PNG/SVG/PDF/EPS), `-width PX`, `-height PX`. **applauncher / applauncher2** (invoke BEAST 2 package-installed sub-apps; each package can register tools that show up here) — `-help` lists installed apps, then positional app name + args. **packagemanager / packagemanager2** (install/update/list/remove BEAST 2 packages a.k.a. BEAUti add-ons) — `-list`, `-add NAME`, `-del NAME`, `-update`, `-useAppDir`, `-dir`, `-version`. **Hunt-skip log this round**: tracer (BEAST 1 family GUI — separate non-CompEvol upstream; deferred), figtree (BEAST 1 figure tool from Rambaut lab; deferred), beastlabs (BEAST 2 dependency package not a separate binary), beast-mcmc (alias/variant — `beast` is the canonical name). **Blacklist additions (14)**: alphabetically distributed across the `applauncher`/`beast`/`densitree`/`logcombiner`/`packagemanager`/`treeannotator` ranges + their `*2` parallel variants. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — 106th consecutive clean round.
- **Classic RAxML R100 MILESTONE — raxml/raxmlHPC + 5 build variants (7-stem multi-binary; classic phylogenetic ML tree inference)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surface transcribed directly from upstream `raxmlHPC(1)` man page at [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/raxml/raxmlHPC.1.en.html](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/raxml/raxmlHPC.1.en.html) via WebFetch. Single multi-stem file `_raxml` is `#compdef raxml raxmlHPC raxmlHPC-PTHREADS raxmlHPC-MPI raxmlHPC-PTHREADS-SSE3 raxmlHPC-PTHREADS-AVX raxmlHPC-PTHREADS-AVX2`. **Coverage**: 7-stem multi-binary harvest of the classic (pre-NG) RAxML family. All seven binaries share the same CLI surface; the suffixes denote build variants (PTHREADS for OpenMP, MPI for cluster, SSE3/AVX/AVX2 for SIMD). The successor `raxml-ng` (modern Kozlov rewrite) is covered separately in `more_src/_raxml-ng` (already covered from 2026-05-20). Classic RAxML uses **single-dash legacy options** (`-s/-n/-m/-p/-f/-N/-T` etc., no double-dash for most). Captured **~50 flags** plus 2 unusually-rich enum sets: **`-f` algorithm action selector** (41-value enum: a=rapid-bootstrap+ML/A=pairwise-distances/b=bootstop-convergence/B=optimal-branch-lengths/c=taxon-name-consistency/C=ancestral-state-recon/d=DEFAULT-rapid-hill-climbing/D=RF-distance/e=optimize-model-params/E=experimental/F=fast-search/g=per-site-likelihoods-for-CONSEL/G=improved-per-site/h=help/H=thorough-model-opt/i=likelihood-vector-tests/I=autoMR-placement-test/j=bootstrap-MSA-files/J=majority-rule-consensus/k=bootstrap-bipartition-info/m=compare-bipartitions/M=multiple-tree-ML/n=user-tree-loglh/N=consensus-of-bootstrap-trees/o=old-rapid-hill-climbing/p=pure-stepwise-MP-addition/P=EPA-placement/q=fast-quartets/r=RF-distance/R=binary-tree-to-Newick/s=split-alignments/S=ancestral-states/t=GAMMA-final-opt/T=GAMMA-final-opt-with-X/u=morpho+molecular-co-estimation/U=gene-tree-estimation/v=environmental-sequence-classify/V=matrix-decomp-viz/w=ELW-test/W=SH-aLRT/x=rapid-bootstrap/y=parsimony-starting-tree-only) and **`-m` substitution model** (25-value enum spanning GTRCAT/GTRCATI/GTRGAMMA/GTRGAMMAI/BINCAT/BINGAMMA for nucl/binary, **12 PROT{CAT,GAMMA}\<matrix\>** variants for proteins (DAYHOFF/WAG/BLOSUM62/JTT/LG/MTREV/MTART/MTZOA/GTR/AUTO with both CAT and GAMMA rate-heterogeneity flavors), MULTICAT/MULTIGAMMA for multi-state). Other rich groups: **bootstrap** (`-x`/`-b`/`-#` synonym for `-N`), **search control** (`-i`/`-e`/`-c`/`-D`/`-F`/`-H`), **constraint+starting trees** (`-r`/`-g`/`-t`/`-R`), **partition handling** (`-q`/`-M`), **placement (EPA)** (`-P` + `--epa-keep-placements`/`--epa-accumulated-threshold`/`--epa-prob-threshold`), **majority-rule** (`-J MR|MRE|STRICT`), **ascertainment correction** (`--asc-corr lewis|stamatakis|felsenstein`), specialized models (`--JC69`/`--K80`/`--HKY85`), output (`-w` full-path output directory, `-o` outgroup name or comma-list), parallel (`-T` PTHREADS), miscellaneous (`-X` half-memory for RF, `-O` skip-duplicate-seq check, `-V` no-rate-heterogeneity, `--no-bfgs`, `--no-seq-check`, `--mesquite`, `--silent`). **Hunt-skip log this round**: raxml-ng (FAILSAFE CATCH — `more_src/_raxml-ng` exists from 2026-05-20 with 38 flags; my 79-flag re-extraction was discarded; the existing covers `raxml-ng` only, not `raxml-ng-mpi` which is built from the same source via `-DUSE_MPI=ON`; deferred as a small refresh-round opportunity), 4 remaining bioinformatics queue items (subread/beast2/star-fusion/bcl2fastq2). **Blacklist additions (7)**: 1 between `rax2` (22080) and `raxml-ng` (22081) for `raxml`; 6 between `raxml-ng` (22082) and `ray` (22089) for raxmlHPC + 5 build variants in LC_ALL=C order (raxmlHPC < raxmlHPC-MPI < raxmlHPC-PTHREADS < raxmlHPC-PTHREADS-AVX < raxmlHPC-PTHREADS-AVX2 (empty <`2` at index 19) < raxmlHPC-PTHREADS-SSE3). Single-stem file `_ccwl` is `#compdef ccwl`. **Coverage**: ccwl is a Guile-based compiler that emits CWL (Common Workflow Language) workflows or Graphviz dot graphs from concise `.scm` descriptions. State-machine with a single top-level subcommand `compile SOURCE_FILE` and 3 shared flags: `-t/--to TARGET` 2-value enum (`cwl` for Common Workflow Language output, `dot` for Graphviz; with source-verified explicit `supported = ("cwl" "dot")` validation that raises `formatted-message` on unknown value), `-o/--output FILE` (default stdout), `-h/--help`. **Implementation note**: ccwl is built with Guile Scheme using `srfi-37 args-fold`, so the option syntax follows GNU getopt conventions (`-tcwl` short or `--to=cwl` long). The top-level dispatch is implemented with a `match` on `argv`: `(program "compile" args ...)` invokes the compile path, and any other invocation falls back to the global-usage line `Usage: ~a COMMAND [OPTIONS] [ARGS]`. **Hunt-skip log this round**: rinetd (already covered, blacklist.txt:22649), proxychains (already covered, blacklist.txt:21000), koka (already covered, blacklist.txt:13286), proxychains4-ng (man page documents only `-f configfile` and `--help` — already absorbed by existing `_proxychains` coverage with -f flag), 30+ other speculative `-cli`/`-bin`/`-stats` suffix typo candidates (traefik-cli/haproxy-cli/envoy-cli/envoy-ctl/envoy-bin/contour-cli/ingress-nginx-cli/nginx-amplify/nginx-supervisord/caddy-cli/boringproxy-cli/twistd-py/uwsgi-cli/unit-cli/relayd-cli/yarrrn/ory-cli/authelia/kong-cli/kong-deck/koka-lang/fastly-cli/tailscale-cli/microsocks/rinetd-cli/wireshark-cli/tshark-cli/sandstorm-cli/filtre/stream-cli/redis-cli7/ngrep-test/mdadm-cli — most resolve to already-covered base names like `traefik`/`haproxy`/`envoy`/`caddy`/`tshark`/`tailscale`/`redis-cli`/etc.). **Blacklist additions (1)**: 1 between `ccusage` (3283) and `ccxxmake` (3284) for `ccwl`. Single-stem file `_dvbsnoop` is `#compdef dvbsnoop`. **Coverage**: dvbsnoop decodes DVB SI (Service Information), TS (Transport Stream), PS/PES (Program Stream / Packetized Elementary Stream), bandwidth, signal, and frontend-info modes from a DVB capture device or a binary file. Single-binary CLI with **~30 flags** (legacy `-flag` style, no double-dash; one positional PID argument in decimal or `0xHH` hex). Flag groups: **Mode** `-s` 8-value enum (ts/ps/pes/sec/pidscan/bandwidth/signal/feinfo). **Output verbosity** `-pd N` (0-9, default 6 decoding verbose), `-npd` shorthand for `-pd 0`, `-ph N` (0-4, default 4 hex verbose), `-hexdumpbuffer`/`-nohexdumpbuffer` toggle pair. **Stream control** `-n N` stop after N packets, `-N N` stop after decoding N packets (section mode), `-if FILE` read binary stream from file (`-` for stdin), `-b` binary output. **Timestamps** `-tf`/`-td`/`-tn` (full/delta/none). **DVB device selection** `-adapter N`, `-devnr N`, `-frontend /dev/dvb/...`, `-demux`, `-dvr`, `-buffersize KB`. **Section mode** `-timeout MS`, `-f VALUE` (section filter), `-m MASK`, **CRC checking 4-way toggle** `-crc`/`-nocrc`/`-softcrc`/`-nosoftcrc`, `-spiderpid` recursively follow referenced PIDs, `-privateprovider ID` for private table decoding. **TS mode** `-tssubdecode` (sub-decode SI or PS/PES inside TS) and `-tsraw`. **PID scan mode** `-maxdmx N`. **General** `-help`, `-hideproginfo` (suppress header). **Hunt-skip log this round**: bpfman-rpc/bpfman-agent/bpftop-rs/cmd-bench/tex5/mpv-mpris/pulseview/sigrok-cli-rs/analog-cli/hellaswag/boxes2/bonsai/bonsai-cli/puzzle-cli/aleph-cli/aleph-zero/aleph-bin/libgosphi-cli/zarrita-cli/zarr-cli/rerun-cli/rerun-py/vega-cli/vega-lite-cli/ndarray-cli/arrow-cli/polars-bin/tablito/termpunk/gum-cli/sg2/sg-rust — most are speculative names with `-rs`/`-cli`/`-bin`/`-py` suffixes; real binaries are typically `bpfman`/`bpftop`/`pulseview`/`sigrok-cli`/`bonsai`/`rerun`/`vega`/`gum`/`sg`, which are largely covered. **Verified already covered**: `numbat` (blacklist.txt:18115), `rerun` (blacklist.txt:22508). **Blacklist additions (1)**: 1 between `dvb-format-convert` (6962) and `dvbv5-daemon` (6963) for `dvbsnoop`. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — ninety-eighth consecutive clean round.

Single multi-stem file `_rwallformats` is `#compdef rwallformats rwcompare rwip2cc rwipaexport rwipaimport rwpdedupe rwpdu2silk rwpmatch rwptoflow rwtotal mapsid`. **Coverage**: 11-stem multi-binary harvest **completing the R90 SiLK deferred queue**. Combined with R90, this covers all 19 SiLK binaries identified as fresh in R90's scan. **Per-binary surface**: **rwallformats** (write a test SiLK file in every supported record format/version) — `--basename` + shared I/O. **rwcompare** (compare two SiLK flow files for equality) — `--quiet`, `--site-config-file`; 2 positional files (or `-`/`stdin`). **rwip2cc** (map IPs to country codes — **DEPRECATED since SiLK 3.0** in favor of `rwpmaplookup(1)`) — `--address IP` xor `--input-file FILE`, `--map-file PMAP`, `--print-ips 0|1`, `--integer-ips`, `--zero-pad-ips`, column formatting. **rwipaexport** (export IPA catalog → SiLK IPset or prefix-map) — `--catalog NAME`, `--time TIMESTAMP`, `--prefix-map-name NAME`, repeatable `--note-add`/`--note-file-add`, `--compression-method`. **rwipaimport** (import SiLK IP collections → IPA catalog) — required `--catalog NAME`, `--description TEXT`, `--start-time`/`--end-time`; positional collection files. **rwpdedupe** (drop duplicate packets from tcpdump captures) — mutex `--first-duplicate` xor `--random-duplicate[=SEED]`, `--threshold MS` (0-1,000,000 ms duplicate detection window); positional `.pcap` files. **rwpdu2silk** (NetFlow v5 PDU → SiLK conversion) — `--silk-output FILE`, `--print-statistics`, `--log-destination`, repeatable `--log-flags` (all/bad/default/missing/record-timestamps 5-enum), `--note-add`/`--note-file-add`, `--compression-method`. **rwpmatch** (match packets from tcpdump against a SiLK flow file) — required `--flow-file FILE`, `--msec-compare`, `--ports-compare`; positional tcpdump file. **rwptoflow** (generate SiLK flow records from tcpdump captures) — `*--plugin .so`, `--active-time RANGE`, `--flow-output FILE`, `--packet-pass-output FILE`, `--packet-reject-output FILE`, `--reject-all-fragments`, `--reject-incomplete`, `--set-sensorid ID`, `--compression-method`, `--print-statistics`. **rwtotal** (per-bin record/byte/packet totals) — **17 mutually-exclusive keying-scheme flags**: `--sip-first-{8,16,24}`/`--sip-last-{8,16}` 5 source-IP-slice flags, `--dip-first-{8,16,24}`/`--dip-last-{8,16}` 5 dest-IP-slice flags, `--sport`/`--dport`/`--proto`/`--packets`/`--bytes`/`--duration`/`--icmp-code` 7 other keys; plus `--summation`, `--min-{bytes,packets,records}`/`--max-{bytes,packets,records}` 6 threshold flags, `--skip-zeroes`. **mapsid** (sensor name ↔ numeric ID mapping from silk.conf) — `--print-classes`, `--print-descriptions`, `--site-config-file`; positional sensor names/IDs. **Hunt-skip log this round**: none — clean targeted source-direct extraction completing the R90 deferral. **Blacklist additions (11)**: alphabetically distributed across the `mapsid` and `rw*` ranges. - **CERT NetSA airframe + QoF R88 — airdaemon/filedaemon/qof (3-stem multi-binary; netflow probe + airframe daemon supervisors)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Single multi-stem file `_airdaemon` is `#compdef airdaemon filedaemon qof`. **Coverage**: 3-stem multi-binary harvest resolving the R87 airdaemon hunt-skip mystery (turned out to be CERT NetSA's airframe library, NOT aircrack-ng as my candidate list assumed). **Per-binary surface**: **airdaemon** (generic daemon supervisor — runs a child process and restarts with backoff) — 6 flags: `-r/--retry SEC` minimum retry delay, `-R/--retry-max SEC` maximum retry delay, `-P/--pidfile FILE` supervised-process pidfile, `-A/--airdaemon-pidfile FILE` supervisor pidfile, `--no-daemon` foreground mode, `-h/--help`; args after `--` are passed to the child. **filedaemon** (directory-poll file daemon — watches an input glob, runs a child on each match, then moves files to `nextdir` or `faildir` based on the child's exit status) — 10 flags: `-i/--in GLOB` input file glob, `-o/--out DIR` output directory, `-n/--nextdir DIR` move-processed-here, `-x/--faildir DIR` move-failed-here, `-e/--extension EXT` output extension, `-p/--poll SEC` input poll delay, `-k/--lock` enable airlock for concurrent input, `-P/--pidfile FILE`, `--no-daemon`, `-h/--help`. **qof** (Quality-of-Flow probe — IPFIX-exporting netflow probe) — **21 flags across 4 option groups**. Core: `-i/--in INSPEC` pcap/interface input, `-o/--out OUTSPEC` collector host:port or file, `-F/--filter BPF`, `-R/--rotate SEC`, `-k/--lock`, `--stats SEC` stats interval (default 300), `--ipfix PROTO` (tcp/udp/sctp), `--yaml FILE`. Experimental: `--template-refresh SEC` (default 600), `--observation-domain N`. IPFIX: `--ipfix-port PORT` (default 4739), `--tls`, `--tls-ca FILE`, `--tls-cert FILE`, `--tls-key FILE`. **Detune** (QoF's traffic-shaping torture knobs for testing): `--detune-bucket-max BYTES` (0=disable), `--detune-bucket-rate BPS` drain rate, `--detune-bucket-delay MS` full-bucket delay, `--detune-random-drop P` post-bucket drop probability, `--detune-random-delay MS` max random delay, `--detune-random-alpha N` random-delay alpha shape parameter. **Hunt-skip log this round**: `yafdpi`/`yafzcbalance`/`yafapplabel`/`yafzipdpi`/`yafhost-stats`/`yafmeta`/`yafmark`/`yafmid`/`yafhostchg`/`yafhost2yaf` (YAF tools — checking YAF source `src/` directory at `britram/cert-netsa-yaf` shows most `yaf*.c` files are internal modules not separate binaries; the existing `_yaf` multi-stem already covers `yaf yafscii yafzcbalance`; deferred until proper YAF binary inventory via Makefile.am inspection). **Blacklist additions (3)**: 1 between `aircrack-ng` (812) and `airdecap-ng` (813) for `airdaemon`; 1 between `filecap` (8107) and `filefrag` (8108) for `filedaemon`; 1 between `qodo` (21757) and `qoitopam` (21758) for `qof`. Single multi-stem file `_gri` is `#compdef gri yorick`. **Coverage**: 2-stem multi-binary harvest covering two niche numerical scripting tools without subcommand trees. **gri** (scientific plotting language compiler — compiles `.gri` script files into PostScript) — 17 flags incl. special-form `-creator FILE.ps` (extract Gri commands from PostScript), `-h`/`-help`/`-v`/`-version`, normal-usage `-b`/`-batch`, `-chatty[N]`/`-c`, `-d`/`-debug`, `-warn_offpage` (default) + `-nowarn_offpage`, `-directory DIR`, `-directory_default`, `-no_bounding_box` (full-page bbox), `-no_expecting`, `-no_startup_message`, `-p`/`-publication`, `-s`/`-superuser` (with optional level), `-t`/`-trace`, `-y`/`-true` (auto-yes). Positional `*.gri` script files. **yorick** (numerical interpreter) — just 2 documented flags: `*-i FILE.i` (include source file at startup; repeatable, equivalent to `#include` after startup) and `-batch FILE.i` (batch mode — no `custom.i` loaded, all errors fatal); positional `*.i` script files. **Hunt-skip log this round**: hersheydemo (man page is sparse per upstream "plotutils does not have a full set of useful man pages" notice; interactive Hershey font demo with no documented CLI surface beyond `--help`; deferred — not worth a low-information completion), gle (GLE Graphics Layout Engine — has its own large language; deferred for separate research), labplot (KDE Qt GUI tool, no CLI), julia-cli/matplotlib-cli/scilab-cli/reduce-cli/idl-cli/dx-server/dx-runtime/gnudatalanguage (project names or library wrappers, real binaries are `julia`/`scilab`/`reduce`/`idl` etc. — needs disambiguation), unison-cli/yadm-init/mosh-cli (typo or wrapper variants of `unison`/`yadm`/`mosh`), sup-mail/himalaya-cli/notmuch-cli/alot-mail/neomutt-cli/abook-utils (typo or wrapper variants of `sup`/`himalaya`/`notmuch`/`alot`/`neomutt`/`abook`). **Blacklist additions (2)**: 1 between `greytiff` (10368) and `gridsome` (10369) for `gri`; 1 between `yor` (29656) and `yosay` (29657) for `yorick`. conventions (input converter to plot output format) — its options were transcribed from sister-binary man pages where its own is empty. **Per-binary surface**: **plot** (master metafile-format plot incl. `-f/--input-file`, `-p/--precision`, `-t/--title`, **3 integration schemes** `-R/--runge-kutta` (default, fifth-order RKF), `-A/--adams-moulton` (fourth-order predictor-corrector), `-E/--euler`, (real-time local cubic Bessel, requires -t), `-k/--boundary-condition`, `-n/--no-of-intervals` default 100, `-p/--periodic`, `-T/--tension`, `-t/--t-spacing tmin tmax`, `-d/--y-dimension`, **4-value I/O format enum** `-I`/`-O` (a/f/d/i = ASCII/single-prec/double-prec/integer), `-P/--precision`, `-a/--auto-abscissa`, `-A/--auto-dist-abscissa` (polygonal arclength), `-s/--suppress-abscissa`. `--numbering-font`. **tek2plot** (Tektronix 4010/4014 vector data → plot) — 16 flags incl. `-T/--output-format`, `-p/--page-number`, `-F/--font-name`, `--position-chars`, `-W/--line-width`, `--bg-color`, `--pen-color`, `--bitmap-size`, `--page-size`, `--rotation`, `--emulate-color`, `--max-line-length`, `--use-tek-fonts` (use original Tektronix bitmap fonts), `-O/--portable-output`. **pic2plot** (troff/groff pic → plot) — 15 flags (shared plot/tek2plot conventions). Flags: `-p CLIENT:PORT` (ALSA sequencer destination port; accepts comma/space-separated list for files using >16 channels, e.g. `-p "64:0, 64:1"`), `-l` (list available output ports), `-d SECONDS` (post-song delay; default 2s — prevents the final note from being chopped off). Single multi-stem file `_binny` is `#compdef binny chronicle grant`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`binny`** (state-machine with 6 subcommands): anchore/binny manages a directory of binaries via `.binny.yaml` without a traditional package manager — `install` (deploy all), `check`, `update` (refresh pinned versions within constraints), `list`, `add`, `remove`. Acquisition methods: github-release, go-install, go-build, hosted-shell. Includes supply-chain cooldown for malicious-version detection. **`chronicle`** (5 flag pairs + positional + 4-format enum): anchore/chronicle is a GitHub-aware changelog generator — `-o/--output FORMAT` (`md`/`md-pretty`/`json`/`version`), `-s/--since-tag TAG` (default: last release), `-u/--until-tag TAG` (default: HEAD), `-n/--speculate-next-version` (guess next release), `-q` (suppress logging); positional 1 = repository path. **`grant`** (state-machine with 2 subcommands + repeatable target): anchore/grant is a license scanner for container images, SBOMs, and filesystems — `list` (enumerate licenses), `check` (validate against policy). Targets accept container image refs, `sbom:FILE`, `dir:PATH`, or filesystem paths. **Blacklist additions (3) across 3 insertion blocks**: 1 between `binmiscctl` (2204) and `binocle` (2205) for `binny` (within bin* at index 3 `m` (109, miscctl) < `n` (110, ny) < `o` (111, ocle)); 1 between `chronic` (3659) and `chronoctl` (3660) for `chronicle` (within chronic* at index 7 end-of-string < `l` (108, le); within chron* at index 5 `i` (105, ic*) < `o` (111, octl)); 1 between `granian` (line 10268, post-shift) and `granted` (10269) for `grant` (within gran* at index 4 `i` (105, ian) < `t` (116, t/ted); within grant* at index 5 end-of-string < `e` (101, ed)). Mid-edit slot-misordering caught + fixed: initial placement assumed `grant < granatier` but actual order is `granatier < granian < grant < granted` because at index 4 `granatier`'s `a` (97) precedes `grant`'s `t` (116) — `LC_ALL=C sort -c` caught it; one re-edit + re-verify. LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — thirty-fourth consecutive clean round.
- **Mixed-theme R27 — comfy + sloglint (2 stems; ComfyUI manager + Go log/slog linter)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surfaces transcribed directly from upstream READMEs at [github.com/Comfy-Org/comfy-cli](https://github.com/Comfy-Org/comfy-cli) and [github.com/go-simpler/sloglint](https://github.com/go-simpler/sloglint). Single multi-stem file `_comfy` is `#compdef comfy sloglint`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`comfy`** (state-machine with **12 top-level subcommands**, nested state-machines for `node`/`model`/`generate`/`manager`/`pr-cache`): Comfy-Org/comfy-cli is a Python-based ComfyUI manager (binary `comfy`, installed via `pip install comfy-cli`). Top-level: `install` (with `--skip-manager`/`--fast-deps`/`--workspace`/`--pr`), `launch` (with `--background`/`--frontend-pr`/`-- ARGS` passthrough), `env`, `run`, `set-default PATH`, `which`, `pr-cache` (list/clean sub-actions), `node` (13 sub-actions incl. show/install/update/reinstall/fix/uninstall/install-deps/deps-in-workflow/uv-sync/save-snapshot/restore-snapshot/bisect with show taking 7-value enum installed/enabled/all/disabled/not-installed/snapshot/snapshot-list and bisect taking 4-value action start/good/bad/reset), `model` (download with `--url`/`--set-civitai-api-token`/`--set-hf-api-token`, list, remove with `--model-names`), `generate` (3 utility sub-actions list/schema/resume plus **16 hosted partner models** Flux/Flux-Pro/Ideogram/DALL·E/Recraft/Stability/Runway/Kling/Luma/Pika/Vidu/Hailuo/Seedance/Gemini-Flash-Image; generate flags `--prompt`/`--download`/`--async`/repeatable `--image`/`--api-key`), `manager` (7 sub-actions disable/enable-gui/disable-gui/enable-legacy-gui/clear/migrate-legacy/uv-compile-default), `tracking disable`. Plus core workspace-selector flags `--workspace=PATH`/`--recent`/`--here` available on most subcommands, plus `--install-completion` for typer-style shell-completion install. **`sloglint`** (positional only): go-simpler/sloglint is a Go `log/slog` style linter (enforces global-logger detection, context requirement, static message validation, key-value vs. attribute consistency, key naming conventions snake_case/kebab-case/camelCase/PascalCase); standalone surface is minimal because configuration is golangci-lint primary. **Blacklist additions (2) across 2 insertion blocks**: 1 between `cometbft` (4261) and `comm` (4262) for `comfy` (within com* at index 3 `c` (99, cast/cetbft? no — `cometbft` index 3='e') < `e` (101, et/etbft) < `f` (102, fy) < `m` (109, m)); 1 between `slogkey` (24121) and `slogverify` (24122) for `sloglint` (within slog* at index 4 `k` (107, key) < `l` (108, lint) < `v` (118, verify)). Surfaces transcribed directly from upstream READMEs at [github.com/breml/bidichk](https://github.com/breml/bidichk), [github.com/macabu/inamedparam](https://github.com/macabu/inamedparam), [github.com/tommy-muehle/go-mnd](https://github.com/tommy-muehle/go-mnd), [github.com/4meepo/tagalign](https://github.com/4meepo/tagalign), [github.com/ldez/tagliatelle](https://github.com/ldez/tagliatelle), and [github.com/ldez/usetesting](https://github.com/ldez/usetesting). Single multi-stem file `_bidichk` is `#compdef bidichk inamedparam mnd tagalign tagliatelle usetesting`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`bidichk`** (1 flag + 9-rune enum + positional): breml/bidichk detects Trojan-Source Unicode bidirectional formatting characters (U+202A-U+202E + U+2066-U+2069) — `--disallowed-runes RUNES` (comma-separated; 9-value enum LEFT-TO-RIGHT-EMBEDDING/RIGHT-TO-LEFT-EMBEDDING/POP-DIRECTIONAL-FORMATTING/LEFT-TO-RIGHT-OVERRIDE/RIGHT-TO-LEFT-OVERRIDE/LEFT-TO-RIGHT-ISOLATE/RIGHT-TO-LEFT-ISOLATE/FIRST-STRONG-ISOLATE/POP-DIRECTIONAL-ISOLATE). **`inamedparam`** (1 flag + positional): macabu/inamedparam flags interface methods with unnamed parameters — `-skip-single-param` (exempt single-unnamed-param interfaces). **`mnd`** (4 flags + 6-check enum + positional): tommy-muehle/go-mnd is a magic-number detector — `-checks CHECKS` (6-value enum: `argument`/`assign`/`case`/`condition`/`operation`/`return`, comma-separated), `-ignored-numbers`, `-ignored-functions PATTERNS`, `-ignored-files PATTERNS`. Defaults exclude 0/1, test files, and `time.Date()`. **`tagalign`** (4 flags + positional): 4meepo/tagalign aligns and optionally sorts struct tags — `-fix`, `-sort`, `-order ORDER` (e.g. `json,xml`), `-strict` (dictionary-order grouped-names alignment). **`tagliatelle`** (positional only): ldez/tagliatelle is a struct-tag naming-convention linter; configuration is golangci-lint-primary (camelCase/PascalCase/kebab-case/snake_case/UPPER_SNAKE_CASE/Go-aware variants/header-case/upper/lower per tag), standalone surface is minimal. **`usetesting`** (positional only): ldez/usetesting suggests `t.TempDir`/`t.Setenv`/`t.Chdir`/`t.Context` replacements for `os.*` and `context.Background`/`context.TODO` calls in tests (Go 1.24+ for some); per-detection enable flags configured via golangci-lint primarily. **Blacklist additions (6) across 5 insertion blocks** (tagalign + tagliatelle share one block): 1 between `bicep` (2184) and `biff` (2185) for `bidichk` (within bi* at index 2 `c` (99, cep) < `d` (100, dichk) < `f` (102, ff)); 1 between `inadyn` (11885) and `inbucket` (11886) for `inamedparam` (within ina* at index 3 `d` (100, dyn) < `m` (109, medparam); within in* at index 2 `a` (97, a*) < `b` (98, bucket)); 1 between `mn` (16511) and `mneme` (16512) for `mnd` (within mn* at index 2 end-of-string < `d` (100, d) < `e` (101, eme)); **2 between `taffybar` (25501) and `taglib-config` (25502)** for `tagalign` + `tagliatelle` (within ta* at index 2 `f` (102, ffybar) < `g` (103, g*); within tag* at index 3 `a` (97, align) < `l` (108, liatelle/lib); within tagl* at index 4 `i` (105, both), at index 5 `a` (97, atelle) < `b` (98, b-config)); 1 between `usestdlibvars` (27358) and `usleep` (27359) for `usetesting` (within us* at index 2 `e` (101, e*) < `l` (108, leep); within use* at index 3 `s` (115, stdlibvars) < `t` (116, testing)). LC_ALL=C sort verified directly — thirty-second consecutive clean round.

Single multi-stem file `_forcetypeassert` is `#compdef forcetypeassert gomoddirectives interfacebloat loggercheck mirror nestif nilnil rowserrcheck`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`forcetypeassert`** (positional only): gostaticanalysis/forcetypeassert flags unchecked type assertions, enforcing the 2-return form `value, ok := a.(int)`. **`gomoddirectives`** (3 flags + positional): ldez/gomoddirectives enforces policies on `go.mod` directives (retract/replace/exclude/ignore/tool/toolchain/godebug/go/module) — `-local` (allow local replacements), `-exclude` (forbid Principle. **`loggercheck`** (4 flags + 5-logger enum + positional): timonwong/loggercheck detects odd-arity key-value pairs in structured logging (`kitlog`/`klog`/`logr`/`slog`/`zap`) — `-requirestringkey`, `-disable LOGGERS` (5-value enum, comma-separated), `-fix`, `-rulefile FILE`. **`mirror`** (1 flag + positional): butuzov/mirror suggests mirror stdlib functions to avoid `[]byte`/`string` conversions (e.g. `MatchString` instead of `Match` after string→[]byte) — `--with-tests`. **`nestif`** (4 flags + positional): nakabonne/nestif is a cognitive-complexity-of-nested-if linter — `--min N` (threshold, default 1), `--top N` (default 10), `--json`, `--exclude-dirs DIRS`. **`nilnil`** (3 flags + 7-type enum + positional): Antonboom/nilnil flags `return nil, nil` patterns — `--checked-types TYPES` (7-value enum: `chan`/`func`/`iface`/`map`/`ptr`/`uintptr`/`unsafeptr`, comma-separated), `--detect-opposite` (also flag non-nil errors with valid values), `--only-two=true|false` (restrict to 2-return functions). **`rowserrcheck`** (positional only): jingyugao/rowserrcheck checks `sql.Rows.Err()` is called after iteration (forked from bodyclose, addresses silent data-integrity issues). **Blacklist additions (8) across 8 insertion blocks**: 1 between `force` (8382) and `forego` (8383) for `forcetypeassert` (within force* at index 5 end-of-string < `t` (116, type); within for* at index 3 `c` (99, c*) < `e` (101, ego)); 1 between `gomock` (9992) and `gomodifytags` (9993) for `gomoddirectives` (within gomod* at index 5 `d` (100, diff) < `f` (102, facebloat) < `l` (108, lace)); 1 between `logger` (14966) and `login` (14967) for `loggercheck` (within logger* at index 6 end-of-string < `c` (99, check); within log* at index 5 `e` rrord)); 1 between `nest-cli` (17433) and `nestjs` (17434) for `nestif` (within nest* at index 4 `-` (45, -cli) < `i` (105, if) < `j` (106, js)); 1 between `nilfs_cleanerd` (17663) and `nim` (17664) i < n; i++ {}` patterns. **`ireturn`** (2 flags + positional + 5 shorthand keywords): butuzov/ireturn enforces "accept interfaces, return concrete types" — `--accept INTERFACES` / `--reject INTERFACES` (comma-separated; within err* at index 4 `c` (99, check) < `i` (105, info)); 1 between `errinfo` (7438 → line shifted) and `errno` (7439) for `errname` (within err* at index 4 `i` (105, info) < `n` (110, name/no); within errn* at index 5 `a` (97, name) < `o` (111, no)); 1 between `exfatlabel` (7626) and `exif` (7627) for `exhaustive` (within ex* at index 2 `f` (102, fat) < `h` (104, haustive) < `i` (105, if)); 1 between `gocc` (9929) and `gochopchop` (9930) for `gochecknoglobals` (within goc* at index 4 end-of-string < `h` (104, check/hop); Single multi-stem file `_bodyclose` is `#compdef bodyclose go-errorlint maintidx nonamedreturns testpackage usestdlibvars`, dispatching on `$service`. Each tool is also runnable via `go vet -vettool=$(which TOOL) PKG/...` and through golangci-lint integration. **Per-stem coverage**: **`bodyclose`** (1 flag + positional): timakin/bodyclose verifies HTTP response bodies are properly closed for TCP connection reuse — `-check-consumption` (also verify body is consumed via io.Copy/io.ReadAll/JSON decoders/buffered readers). **`go-errorlint`** (1 flag + positional): polyfloyd/go-errorlint enforces Go 1.13 error-wrapping patterns (flags `%v` for errors → `%w`; `err == ErrFoo` → `errors.Is`; type assertions → `errors.As`) — `-fix` (apply autofixes). *NOTE: upstream archived; moved to Codeberg.* **`maintidx`** (1 flag + positional): yagipy/maintidx computes function maintainability index (cyclomatic + Halstead volume + LOC composite, Microsoft rebased scale) — `-under N` (show functions below threshold; default 20). **`nonamedreturns`** (1 flag + positional): firefart/nonamedreturns flags named-return values (variable shadowing / accidental modifications / unintended scope expansion concerns) — `-report-error-in-defer` (also report named errors used in defer; default false). **`testpackage`** (4 flags + positional): maratori/testpackage enforces separate `_test` packages for blackbox testing — `-skip-regexp PATTERN` (default `(export|internal)_test\.go`), `-allow-packages NAMES` (default `main`), `-test`, `-fix`. **`usestdlibvars`** (22 flags + positional): sashamelentyev/usestdlibvars suggests stdlib constants for hardcoded values across HTTP/time/crypto/OS/RPC/SQL/TLS domains — general `-V` (version), `-h` (help), `-flags` (JSON flags), `-json`, `-fix`, `-test`; 11 detection toggles `-http-method`, `-http-status-code`, `-time-layout`, `-time-month`, `-time-weekday`, `-os-dev-null`, `-crypto-hash`, `-constant-kind`, `-sql-isolation-level`, `-tls-signature-scheme`, `-rpc-default-path`; profiling/debug `-cpuprofile`, `-memprofile`, `-trace`, `-debug` (subset of `fpstv`), `-c N` (context lines, default -1). **Blacklist additions (6) across 6 insertion blocks**: 1 between `bochs` (2374) and `bodyfile.pl` (2375) for `bodyclose` (within bod* at index 4 `c` (99, close) < `f` (102, file)); 1 between `go-enum` (9896) and `go-feature-flag-relay-proxy` (9897) for `go-errorlint` (within go-e* at index 4 `n` (110, enum) < `r` (114, errorlint); within go-* at index 3 `e` (101, e*) < `f` (102, feature)); 1 between `maim` (15507) and `make` (15508) for `maintidx` (within m-a-* at index 2 `i` (105, maim/maintidx) < `k` (107, make); within mai* at index 3 `m` (109, maim) < `n` (110, maintidx)); 1 between `nona` (17815) and `nono` (17816) for `nonamedreturns` (within nona* at index 4 end-of-string < `m` (109, named); within non* at index 3 `a` (97, nona*) < `o` (111, nono)); 1 between `testkube` (25879) and `testparm` (25880) for `testpackage` (within test* at index 4 `k` (107, kube) < `p` (112, package/parm); within testp* at index 5 `a` (97, both); at index 6 `c` (99, package) < `r` (114, parm)); 1 between `users` (27328) and `usleep` (27329) for `usestdlibvars` (within us* at index 2 `e` (101, users/usestdlibvars) < `l` (108, usleep); within use* at index 3 `r` (114, users) < `s` (115, usestdlibvars)). - **Go linter/analyzer sweep R21 — go-consistent + go-critic + perfguard + ruleguard + structlayout-optimize + structlayout-pretty + testifylint (7 stems via single multi-stem `_go-consistent` file)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surfaces transcribed directly from upstream READMEs + main.go source files at [github.com/quasilyte/go-consistent](https://github.com/quasilyte/go-consistent), [github.com/go-critic/go-critic](https://github.com/go-critic/go-critic), [github.com/quasilyte/go-perfguard](https://github.com/quasilyte/go-perfguard), [github.com/quasilyte/go-ruleguard](https://github.com/quasilyte/go-ruleguard), [github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/structlayout-optimize](https://github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/structlayout-optimize) and [structlayout-pretty](https://github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/structlayout-pretty), and [github.com/Antonboom/testifylint](https://github.com/Antonboom/testifylint). Single multi-stem file `_go-consistent` is `#compdef go-consistent go-critic perfguard ruleguard structlayout-optimize structlayout-pretty testifylint`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`go-consistent`** (1 flag + positional): quasilyte/go-consistent identifies inconsistent code patterns where multiple equivalent expressions exist (e.g. `make(map[K]V)` vs `map[K]V{}`) — `-v` (verbose), `--help`, conventional Go-target positional (`std`, `./...`, files, packages). **`go-critic`** (state-machine with 3 subcommands): go-critic/go-critic is a Go linter with ~100 diagnostics — `check <targets>` with `-v` + `-enable CHECKERS_OR_TAGS` (filter via `#diagnostic`/`#style`/`#performance`/`#experimental`/`#opinionated`/`#security` tags) + `-disable`, `version`, `doc <checker>`. **`perfguard`** (state-machine with 2 subcommands): quasilyte/go-perfguard is a Go performance analyzer — `lint` (traditional static analysis) with `--fix`, `optimize` (profile-guided) with `--heatmap CPU_PROFILE` + `--fix`; both take Go-target positional. **`ruleguard`** (5 flags + positional): quasilyte/go-ruleguard is a pattern-based dynamic Go linter — `-rules FILES` (comma-separated ruleguard file paths), `-e RULE` (execute a single rule from a string), `-fix` (apply autofixes), `-c` (display offending lines with context), `-json` (output JSON). **`structlayout-optimize`** (3 flags): dominikh/go-tools cmd/structlayout-optimize reorders struct fields to reduce padding — `-json` (format as JSON), `-r` (break up structs + reorder fields freely), `-version`. **`structlayout-pretty`** (2 flags): dominikh/go-tools cmd/structlayout-pretty pretty-prints structlayout output with ASCII art — `-v` (do not compact consecutive bytes), `-version`. **`testifylint`** (4 flags + positional): Antonboom/testifylint is a testify usage-pattern linter with 25+ checkers — `--enable-all`, `--enable CHECKERS`, `--disable CHECKERS`, `--fix` (autofix). **Blacklist additions (7) across 5 insertion blocks** (go-consistent + go-critic share one block, structlayout-optimize + structlayout-pretty share another): **2 between `go-callvis` (9893) and `go-enum` (9894)** for `go-consistent` + `go-critic` (within go-c* at index 4 `a` (97, callvis) < `o` (111, consistent) < `r` (114, critic); within go-* at index 3 `c` (99, c*) < `e` (101, enum)); 1 between `perf` (19517 → line shifted) and `perfquery` (19518) for `perfguard` (within perf* at index 4 end-of-string < `g` (103, guard) < `q` (113, query)); 1 between `rulegen` (22882 → line shifted) and `rulesync` (22883) for `ruleguard` (within rule* at index 4 `g` (103, both gen/guard); at index 5 `e` (101, gen) < `u` (117, guard); within rul* at index 4 `g` (103, guard) < `s` (115, sync)); **2 between `structlayout` (24987 → line shifted) and `structurizr-cli` (24988)** for `structlayout-optimize` + `structlayout-pretty` (within structlayout* at index 12 end-of-string < `-` (45, layout-*); within structlayout-* at index 13 `o` (111, optimize) < `p` (112, pretty); within struct* at index 6 `l` (108, layout) < `u` (117, urizr)); 1 between `testgdbm` (25870 → line shifted) and `testj1939` (25871) for `testifylint` (within test* at index 4 `g` (103, gdbm) < `i` (105, ifylint) < `j` (106, j1939)). Single multi-stem file `_appinspector` is `#compdef appinspector devskim oss-defog oss-detect-backdoor oss-detect-cryptography oss-diff oss-download oss-find-source oss-find-squats oss-health oss-metadata oss-risk-calculator`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`appinspector`** (state-machine with 7 subcommands; `analyze` carries 4 short flags from README + many additional flags deferred to wiki page 1): microsoft/ApplicationInspector is a .NET-Global-Tool static analyzer with 400+ rule patterns — subcommands `analyze`/`tagdiff`/`exporttags`/`verifyrules`/`packrules`/`help`/`version`; `analyze` carries `-s` (source, required), `-f` (format html/json/sarif/markdown), `-o` (output file), `-g` (glob exclude). **`devskim`** (state-machine with `analyze` subcommand carrying **~30 flags**): microsoft/DevSkim is a .NET-Global-Tool security analyzer with inline IDE integration — required `-I/--source-code PATH`, `-O/--output-file FILE`; rules `--options-json`, `-r`, `--rule-ids`, `--ignore-rule-ids`, `--languages`, `--comments`; output `-o/--output-format`, `-f/--file-format` (text/sarif), `-s/--severity`, `--confidence`, `-g/--ignore-globs`; processing `-d/--disable-supression`, `--disable-parallel`, `-i/--ignore-default-rules`, `-c/--crawl-archives`, `--skip-git-ignored-files`; paths `--base-path`, `--absolute-path`, `--skip-excerpts`; logging `-x/--console-verbosity`, `--disable-console`, `-v/--log-file-level`, `-l/--log-file-path`; utility `-E` (exit code = issue count). **`oss-defog`** (10 flags + PURL): microsoft/OSSGadget oss-defog finds Base64/hex-encoded obfuscated text — `--download-directory`, `--report-blobs`, `--minimum-hex-length N` (default 8), `--minimum-base64-length N` (default 1), three `--save-found-binaries-to`/`--save-archives-to`/`--save-blobs-to` directory flags, `--use-cache`, `--help`, `--version`. **`oss-detect-backdoor`** (6 flag pairs + PURL): oss-detect-backdoor flags potential malicious code (high false-positive rate per upstream) — `-d/--download-directory`, `-f/--format` (text/sarifv1/sarifv2), `-o/--output-file`, `-c/--use-cache`. **`oss-detect-cryptography`** (9 flags + PURL): oss-detect-cryptography finds cryptographic implementations — `--verbose`, `--custom-rule-directory`, `--disable-default-rules`, `--download-directory`, `--use-cache`, `--format`, `--output-file`. **`oss-diff`** (12 flag pairs + PURL): oss-diff compares two package versions — `-d/--download-directory`, `-c/--use-cache`, `-w/--crawl-archives` (default true), `-B/--context-before N`, `-A/--context-after N`, `-C/--context N` (-1 = all, overrides B/A), `-a/--added-only`, `-r/--removed-only`, `-f/--format`, `-o/--output-location`. **`oss-download`** (6 flag pairs + PURL): oss-download retrieves and optionally extracts packages — `-x/--download-directory` (default cwd), `-m/--download-metadata-only`, `-e/--extract`, `-c/--use-cache`. **`oss-find-source`** (5 flag pairs + PURL): oss-find-source locates source repositories — `-f/--format`, `-o/--output-file`, `-S/--single` (top possibility only). **`oss-find-squats`** (6 flag pairs + PURL): oss-find-squats detects typo-squatting candidates — `-o/--output-file`, `-f/--format`, `-q/--quiet`, `-s/--sleep-delay N` (ms between checks). **`oss-health`** (4 flag pairs + PURL): oss-health collects project health metrics — `-f/--format`, `-o/--output-file`. **`oss-metadata`** (3 flag pairs + PURL): oss-metadata fetches package metadata from deps.dev or libraries.io — `-o/--output-file`. **`oss-risk-calculator`** (9 flag pairs + PURL): oss-risk-calculator generates risk assessments — required `-d/--download-directory`, optional `-r/--external-risk N`, `-f/--format`, `-o/--output-file`, `-n/--no-health`, `--verbose`, `-c/--use-cache`. **Blacklist additions (12) across 3 insertion blocks**: 1 between `appimagetool` (1138) and random if omitted) + `--description`, `edit <name>` with `--color`/`--description`/`--new-name`, `delete <name>`, `export <path>` and `import <path>` both with `--format csv|json` (use `-` for stdin/stdout), `list [substring-filter]`. **`gh-projects`** (state-machine with 4 subcommands): heaths/gh-projects is CRUD for Projects V2 — `clone` with `-t/--title NEW_TITLE` + `--private` + `-d DESC`, `edit` with `-d DESC` + `--public` + `--add-issue ISSUES` (comma-separated) + repeatable `-f FieldName=Value`, `list` with `--search QUERY`, `view`. **Blacklist additions (4) across 4 insertion blocks**: 1 between `gh-bofh` (9218) and `gh-changelog` (9219) for `gh-branch` (within gh-b* at index 4 `o` (111, bofh) < `r` (114, branch); Single multi-stem file `_gh-org-clone` is `#compdef gh-org-clone gh-pr-repl gh-provision-envs gh-start gh-submodule-add`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`gh-org-clone`** (10 short/long flag pairs + `--default`): crguezl/gh-org-clone batch-clones all repos in an org via Node + optional fzf interactive selection — `-s/--search`, `-r/--regexp`, `-c/--csr` (comma-separated repo list), `-f/--file` (load repo list from file), `-k/--fork` 3-value enum (`true|only|false`), `-n/--dryrun`, `-o/--org`, `--default` (set org as default for future use), `-D/--depth` (shallow clone), `-p/--parallel`. **`gh-pr-repl`** (interactive REPL with positionals): nobe4/gh-pr-repl is a Ruby-based interactive REPL for managing PRs — bare invocation uses PR from current branch, positionals accept `OWNER/REPO/BRANCH` or PR URLs (one or many for multi-PR sessions). **`gh-provision-envs`** (2 flags): AyogoHealth/gh-provision-envs provisions environment variables + secrets from a JSON config — `-c CONFIG.json` (required) + `-R OWNER/REPO`; upstream documents the JSON shape uses an `environments` object with `variables` + `secrets` arrays of `{name,value}` pairs and will **overwrite** existing values. **`gh-start`** (1 positional): balvig/gh-start (Ruby Cookpad-derived) creates a branch and opens a draft PR — `gh start "description"` for free-text or `gh start [issue-url]` to auto-populate from a GitHub issue. **`gh-submodule-add`** (7 short/long flag pairs): crguezl/gh-submodule-add batch-adds repos as submodules via Node + optional fzf — `-C/--clone` (clone only, skip submodule setup), `-o/--org`, `-s/--search`, `-r/--regexp`, `-k/--fork`, `-p/--parallel` (default 2), `-D/--depth`. **Blacklist additions (5) across 5 insertion blocks**: 1 between `gh-notify` (9253) and `gh-ost` (9254) for `gh-org-clone` (within gh-* at index 3 `n` (110, notify) < `o` (111, org/ost); within gh-o* at index 4 `r` (114, org) < `s` (115, ost)); 1 between `gh-poi` (9256 — line shifted) and `gh-prism` (9257) for `gh-pr-repl` (within gh-p* at index 4 `o` (111, poi) < `r` (114, pr*); within gh-pr* at index 5 `-` (45, pr-repl) < `i` (105, prism)); 1 between `gh-project-item-move` (9259 — line shifted) and `gh-prpeek` (9260) for `gh-provision-envs` (within gh-pr* at index 5 `o` (111, project/provision); at index 6 `j` (106, project) < `v` (118, provision); `auth` subcommand with `login`/`logout` positional sub-action. **`gh-feed`** (2 flags): jo-es/gh-feed is a TUI for PR discussion reading and replying — `--pr NUMBER` (preselect) + `--repo OWNER/REPO`. **`gh-ghq-cd`** (5 flags): cappyzawa/gh-ghq-cd is a ghq-managed repo navigator with tmux/zellij integration — `-w` (new window/tab), `-p` (pane split), **`-H` ↔ `-V` mutex** for split direction, `-c COMMAND` for command-to-run-in-new-pane. **`gh-ranking`** (2 flags + 2 positionals): yukukotani/gh-ranking displays org-wide activity rankings — positional 1 = organization, positional 2 = action enum (`open-pr|review-pr`), `--team TEAM` filter, `--query QUERY` for additional GitHub search filters. **`gh-sparkle`** (5 flags): dyxushuai/gh-sparkle is an AI-driven commit-message generator via GitHub Models — `--language LANG` (description language; header stays English), `--examples N` (1-20, default 3), `--model MODEL` (defaults to `openai/gpt-4o-mini` per upstream), `--dry-run`, `--summary-only` (skip diff details for sensitive code). **Blacklist additions (6) across 6 insertion blocks**: 1 between `gh-board` (9215) and `gh-changelog` (9216) for `gh-bofh` (within gh-b* at index 4 `o` (111, both); Surfaces transcribed directly from upstream READMEs at [github.com/github/gh-stack](https://github.com/github/gh-stack), [github.com/gennaro-tedesco/gh-s](https://github.com/gennaro-tedesco/gh-s), [github.com/Link-/gh-token](https://github.com/Link-/gh-token), and [github.com/gennaro-tedesco/gh-f](https://github.com/gennaro-tedesco/gh-f). **Hunt-defer log this round**: `gh-repo-stats` and `gh-actions-cache` — both listed in the topics index but my speculated `owner/repo` paths 404'd; without the correct upstream owner-prefix the README is unreachable, so defer until the right owner surfaces. Single multi-stem file `_gh-stack` is `#compdef gh-stack gh-s gh-token gh-f`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`gh-stack`** (state-machine with **19 documented subcommands** + 5 flags): github/gh-stack manages stacked PRs as ordered branch chains with linked GitHub PRs and metadata stored in `.git/gh-stack/*.json` — subcommands span 4 categories: Stack Management (`init`/`add`/`modify`/`submit`), Navigation (`up`/`down`/`top`/`bottom`/`trunk`/`switch`), Sync (`rebase`/`sync`/`push`), Utilities (`view`/`checkout`/`link`/`unstack`/`feedback`/`alias`); flags `--auto` (skip PR title prompts), `--force-with-lease` (safe force-push), `--numbered` (auto-increment `feat/01`/`feat/02`), and **`--downstack` ↔ `--upstack` mutex** for partial-stack rebases. **`gh-s`** (7 flag pairs + 1 positional): gennaro-tedesco/gh-s is an fzf-driven interactive repository search — `-l/--lang LANGUAGE`, `-d/--desc DESC`, `-u/--user USER`, `-t/--topic TOPIC`, `-c/--colour COLOUR`, `-L/--limit N` (default 20), `-E/--empty` (search by flags alone, no name prompt), plus a positional search term that can replace the interactive prompt; output is the selected repo's URL to stdout. **`gh-token`** (state-machine with 4 subcommands + per-subcommand flags): Link-/gh-token generates short-lived GitHub App installation tokens (1-hour expiry) — `generate` carries **`--key FILE` ↔ `--base64-key VALUE` mutex** plus `--app-id ID` + `--installation-id ID` + optional `--hostname HOST` (for GHES); `revoke` takes the token as a positional; `installations` lists GitHub App installations; `help` shows command docs. **`gh-f`** (11 single-letter subcommand aliases — mutex set + 11 long-form subcommand names): gennaro-tedesco/gh-f is an fzf-extension covering everyday Git/GitHub workflows — each subcommand has both a short alias (`-a`/`-p`/`-b`/`-l`/`-t`/`-R`/`-r`/`-g`/`-s`/`-m`/`-k`, all in a single `_arguments` mutex group) and a long name (`adds`/`prs`/`branches`/`logs`/`tags`/`releases`/`runs`/`greps`/`search`/`myissue`/`pick`); running `gh f` with no arg prints help. **Blacklist additions (4) across 4 insertion blocks**: 1 between `gh-dash` (9219) and `gh-fzf` (9220) for `gh-f` (within gh-f* at index 4 end-of-string < `z` (122, fzf); at index 3 `d` (100, dash) < `f` (102, f*)); 1 between `gh-pv` (9228) and `gh-signoff` (9229) for `gh-s` (within gh-s* at index 4 end-of-string < `i` (105, signoff); at index 3 `p` (112, pv) < `s` (115, s*)); 1 between `gh-skyline` (9230) and `gh-sub-issue` (9231) for `gh-stack` (within gh-s* at index 4 `k` (107, skyline) < `t` (116, stack) < `u` (117, sub-issue)); 1 between `gh-todo` (9233) and `ghalint` (9234) for `gh-token` (within gh-to* at index 5 `d` (100, todo) < `k` (107, token); at index 2 within ghX `-` (45, gh-*) < `a` (97, ghalint)). Single multi-stem file `_gh-skyline` is `#compdef gh-skyline gh-sub-issue gh-not gh-tidy`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`gh-skyline`** (8 flag pairs, no positionals): generate a 3D-printable STL of a GitHub contribution graph — `-h/--help`, `-d/--debug`, `-f/--full` (from join year), `-o/--output FILE`, `-u/--user USERNAME`, `-y/--year YEAR_OR_RANGE` (2008..current), `-w/--web`, `-a/--art-only` (ASCII preview only). **`gh-sub-issue`** (state-machine with 4 subcommands, each with its own flag set): `add` links existing issue to parent (`-R/--repo` + 1+ issue positional); `create` builds new linked issue (`-p/--parent` required + `-t/--title` required + `-b/--body` + repeatable `*-l/--label` + repeatable `*-a/--assignee` + `-m/--milestone` + `--project` + `-R/--repo`); `list` shows sub-issues (`-s/--state open|closed|all` + `-L/--limit N` + `--json FIELDS` + `-w/--web` + `-R/--repo` + parent positional); `remove` unlinks without deletion (`-f/--force` + `-R/--repo` + sub-issue positional). **`gh-not`** (1 flag): rule-based GitHub notification manager — uses YAML config + jq-syntax rules so most behavior is config-file driven; CLI surface is minimal: `-h/--help` and `--config FILE`. Upstream notes the project is "mostly done" so the surface is stable. **`gh-tidy`** (2 flags): checkout main + gc + prune merged branches — `--auto-delete-merged` for non-interactive automation, `--trunk BRANCH` to override the default `main`/`master`. **Blacklist additions (4) across 2 insertion blocks** (gh-skyline + gh-sub-issue + gh-tidy share one block): 1 between `gh-md-toc` (9222) and `gh-notify` (9223) for `gh-not` (within gh-* at index 3 `m` (109, md) < `n` (110, not/notify); within gh-not* at index 6 end-of-string < `i` (105, notify)); **3 between `gh-pv` (9226) and `gh-todo` (9227)** for `gh-skyline` + `gh-sub-issue` + `gh-tidy` (within gh-* at index 3 `p` (112, pv) < `s` (115, skyline/sub-issue) < `t` (116, tidy/todo); within gh-s* at index 4 `k` (107, skyline) < `u` (117, sub-issue); within gh-t* at index 4 `i` (105, tidy) < `o` (111, todo)). Single standalone file `_tfnotify` is `#compdef tfnotify`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`tfnotify`** (3 global flags + 3 subcommands, stdin-driven): Mercari's Go-based wrapper that pipes Terraform output through template processing and posts to GitHub/GitLab/Bitbucket as PR comments. the surface is entirely stdin-driven so no CLI completion content. **`git-reset-file`** (2 positionals): `[<filename>] commit-hash` — reset a single file to a given commit (default `HEAD`). **`git-unlock`** (1 positional): undo `git lock` (re-enables tracking of the assume-unchanged file). **Blacklist additions (6) across 5 insertion blocks** (git-repl + git-reset-file share one block): 1 between `git-browse` (9331) and `git-brv` (9332) for `git-browse-ci` (within git-browse* at index 9 end-of-string < `-` (45, ci); Single multi-stem file `_git-psykorebase` is `#compdef git-psykorebase git-rebase-patch git-rename-branch git-rename-remote git-sed git-squash`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`git-psykorebase`** (2 flags + 2 positionals): "psyko rebase" workflow — `--no-ff` forces a merge commit message even when conflicts are absent; `--continue` resumes after manual conflict resolution and is a `(- *)` mutex against everything else; positional 1 = target branch, positional 2 = optional feature branch (default current). **`git-rebase-patch`** (1 positional): apply a single patch file as a rebase. **`git-rename-branch`** (2 positionals): `[<old-branch>] <new-branch>` — with 1 arg the current branch is renamed to that arg, with 2 args the named branch is renamed. **`git-rename-remote`** (2 positionals): `<old-remote-name> <new-remote-name>`. **`git-sed`** (2 flags + variable positionals): bulk sed across tracked files — `-c` commits with a standard auto-message (fails on unstaged changes), `-f FLAGS` passes sed regex flags (e.g. `-f g` enables global-per-line); positionals are `<search> <replacement> [-- <pathspec>]`. **`git-squash`** (1-flag mutex + 2 positionals): `[--squash-msg] <source-branch|commit-ref> [<commit-message>]` — `--squash-msg` (concatenated squashed messages as the commit message) is explicitly mutually exclusive with a custom commit-message positional, encoded as `(--squash-msg 2)` in `_arguments` syntax so a 2nd-positional candidate disables `--squash-msg` and vice-versa. **Blacklist additions (6) across 5 insertion blocks** (git-rename-branch + git-rename-remote share one block): 1 between `git-pr` (9435) and `git-pull-request` (9436) for `git-psykorebase` (within git-p* at index 5 `r` (114, pr) < `s` (115, psykorebase) < `u` (117, pull)); 1 between `git-quickfix` (9439) and `git-rec` (9440) for `git-rebase-patch` (at index 4 `q` (113, quickfix) < `r` (114, rebase/rec); within git-re* at index 6 `b` (98, rebase) < `c` (99, rec)); **2 between `git-remote-hg` (9447) and `git-rename-tag` (9448)** for `git-rename-branch` + `git-rename-remote` (within git-re* at index 6 `m` (109, remote) < `n` (110, rename); within git-rename-* at index 11 `b` (98, branch) < `r` (114, remote) < `t` (116, tag)); 1 between `git-secrets` (9455) and `git-series` (9456) for `git-sed` (within git-se* at index 6 `c` (99, secret/secrets) < `d` (100, sed) < `r` (114, series)); 1 between `git-split-diffs` (9465) and `git-ssh` (9466) for `git-squash` (within git-s* at index 5 `p` (112, spice/split) < `q` (113, squash) < `s` (115, ssh)). LC_ALL=C sort verified directly (no mid-round corrections — fourth consecutive clean round).

Single multi-stem file `_git-brv` is `#compdef git-brv git-clear git-clear-soft git-contrib git-cp git-create-branch git-delete-branch git-delete-squashed-branches git-delete-submodule git-delete-tag git-force-clone git-pull-request`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`git-brv`** (no flags): list branches sorted by last commit date. **`git-clear`** (2 flag pairs): combined hard reset + clean — `-f/--force` (no warning) + `-h/--help/?`. **`git-clear-soft`** (no flags): `git-clear` that respects `.gitignore`. **`git-contrib`** (1 optional positional): show commits by username or email. **`git-cp`** (2 positionals): copy a file preserving git history. **`git-create-branch`** (3 flags + branchname): `-r/--remote [name]` for remote tracking (defaults to `origin`) + `--from START` (defaults to current branch) + variable branch names. **`git-delete-branch`** (1+ positionals): delete one or more local + remote branches. **`git-delete-squashed-branches`** (1 flag pair + 1 optional positional): `-p/--proceed` to continue on errors + target branch (default current). **`git-delete-submodule`** (1 positional): full submodule removal by path. **`git-delete-tag`** (1+ positionals): delete one or more tags locally + remotely. **`git-force-clone`** (2 flags + 2 positionals): `--help` + `--branch=NAME` (post-clone checkout) + remote URL + destination path (replaces destination if it exists). **`git-pull-request`** (1 optional positional): file a PR against an optional target branch. **Blacklist additions (12) across 8 insertion blocks**: 1 between `git-browse` (9331) and `git-bug` (9332) for `git-brv` (within git-br* at index 6 `a` (97, branch) < `o` (111, browse) < `v` (118, brv)); 1 between `git-conflict` (9347) and `git-count` (9348) for `git-contrib` (within git-con* at index 7 `f` (102, conflict) < `t` (116, contrib); at index 6 `n` (110, contrib) < `u` (117, count)); **2 between `git-count` (9348) and `git-credential-gcloud` (9349)** for `git-cp` + `git-create-branch` (at index 4 `o` (111, count) < `p` (112, cp/create) < `r` (114, credential); within git-cp* at index 5 end-of-string < `r` (114, create); at index 6 `a` (97, create) < `d` (100, credential)); 1 between `git-dag` (9356) and `git-delete-merged-branches` (9357) for `git-delete-branch` (within git-d* at index 5 `a` (97, dag) < `e` (101, delete); - **git-extras Round 5 — git-gh-pages + git-ignore-io + git-lock + git-locked + git-local-commits + git-show-merged-branches + git-show-unmerged-branches + git-show-tree + git-stamp + git-utimes (10 more tj/git-extras subcommands via single multi-stem `_git-gh-pages` file; cumulative git-extras coverage now 40 stems across rounds 150–153 + the pre-existing `_git-changelog`/`_git-info`/`_git-ignore`)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Surfaces transcribed directly from upstream manpages at [github.com/tj/git-extras](https://github.com/tj/git-extras) — `man/git-gh-pages.1` / `man/git-ignore-io.1` / `man/git-lock.1` / `man/git-locked.1` / `man/git-local-commits.1` / `man/git-show-merged-branches.1` / `man/git-show-unmerged-branches.1` / `man/git-show-tree.1` / `man/git-stamp.1` / `man/git-utimes.1`. Single multi-stem file `_git-gh-pages` is `#compdef git-gh-pages git-ignore-io git-lock git-locked git-local-commits git-show-merged-branches git-show-unmerged-branches git-show-tree git-stamp git-utimes`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`git-gh-pages`** (no flags): creates the gh-pages branch with a default initial index.html. **`git-ignore-io`** (7 flag pairs with 4 mutex groups): manages `.gitignore` via gitignore.io types — repeatable mutex `--append=TYPES` ↔ `--replace=TYPES` (both with short forms `-a`/`-r`), mutex `--list-in-table` ↔ `--list-alphabetically` (`-l`/`-L`), `-s/--search WORD`, `-t/--show-update-time`, `-u/--update-list` (each long-form ↔ short-form pair encoded as its own `_arguments` mutex). **`git-lock`** (1 positional): mark a file as locked via the assume-unchanged bit. **`git-locked`** (no flags): list all locked files. **`git-local-commits`** (no flags, all args passthrough): show commits not yet pushed; all args passed directly to `git log`. **`git-show-merged-branches`** / **`git-show-unmerged-branches`** / **`git-show-tree`** (each: no flags, no positionals): display merged/unmerged branch lists and the decorated commit-history graph respectively. **`git-stamp`** (1 flag + id + variable messages): append issue references to the last commit message — `git stamp [-r|--replace] <id> [<messages>]`; `-r` eliminates previous stamps sharing the same case-insensitive identifier. **`git-utimes`** (1 flag): restore file mtimes to last-commit dates; `--newer` only touches files newer than their last commit. **Blacklist additions (10) across 6 insertion blocks** (git-local-commits + git-lock + git-locked share one block; git-show-merged-branches + git-show-tree + git-show-unmerged-branches share another): 1 between `git-get` (9374) and `git-gone` (9375) for `git-gh-pages` (within git-g* at index 5 `e` (101, get) < `h` (104, gh) < `o` (111, gone)); 1 between `git-ignore` (9385) and `git-imerge` (9386) for `git-ignore-io` (within git-ignore* at index 10 end-of-string < `-` (45, io); at index 5 `g` (103, ignore) < `m` (109, imerge)); **3 between `git-lfs` (9396) and `git-machete` (9397)** for `git-local-commits` + `git-lock` + `git-locked` (within git-loc* at index 7 `a` (97, local) < `k` (107, lock/locked); within git-lock* at index 8 end-of-string < `e` (101, locked); at index 4 `l` (108, l*) < `m` (109, machete)); **3 between `git-shell` (9441) and `git-sim` (9442)** for `git-show-merged-branches` + `git-show-tree` + `git-show-unmerged-branches` (within git-sh* at index 6 `e` (101, shell) < `o` (111, show); within git-show-* at index 9 `m` (109, merged) < `t` (116, tree) < `u` (117, unmerged); within git-s* at index 5 `h` (104, shell/show) < `i` (105, sim)); 1 between `git-stack` (9447) and `git-standup` (9448) for `git-stamp` (within git-sta* at index 7 `c` (99, stack) < `m` (109, stamp) < `n` (110, standup)); 1 between `git-url-sub` (9465) and `git-vendor` (9466) for `git-utimes` (within git-u* at index 5 `r` (114, url) < `t` (116, utimes); at index 4 `u` (117, utimes) < `v` (118, vendor)). Surfaces transcribed directly from upstream manpages at [github.com/tj/git-extras](https://github.com/tj/git-extras) — `man/git-magic.1` / `man/git-merge-repo.1` / `man/git-missing.1` / `man/git-obliterate.1` / `man/git-pr.1` / `man/git-rename-tag.1` / `man/git-root.1` / `man/git-scp.1` / `man/git-setup.1`. **Hunt-skip log this round**: `git-undo` shows `existing=more_src/_ugit` on the `^#compdef` recheck — the pre-existing `_ugit` completion (for the `ugit` interactive git tool) carries `git-undo` in its `#compdef` line, so the round-152 multi-stem excludes `git-undo` to avoid collision; the user already has `git-undo` completions via `_ugit` even though the upstream `tj/git-extras` shipping path is distinct. Single multi-stem file `_git-magic` is `#compdef git-magic git-merge-repo git-missing git-obliterate git-pr git-rename-tag git-root git-scp git-setup`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`git-magic`** (5 flags + `-h`): quick commit-and-push helper — `-a` adds untracked, repeatable `*-m msg` (concatenated as paragraphs per upstream), `-e` for editor-edit of the auto-message, `-p` for push, `-f` adds `-f` to the push. **`git-merge-repo`** (1 flag + 3 positionals): external-repo subtree merge — `<repo> <branch> <directory> [--squash]`; `--squash` collapses history to a single merge commit. **`git-missing`** (0 flags + 2 positionals + trailing `git log` opts): commit diff between branches — `[<first branch>] <second branch> [<git log options>]`; first defaults to current. **`git-obliterate`** (0 flags + files + trailing rev-list opts): erase files from entire history — `<files...> [-- <rev-list options...>]`; rev-list options after `--` per upstream's `git help rev-list`. **`git-pr`** (1-flag mutex + variable positional shapes): GitHub PR checkout — 4 synopsis shapes (number+remote, [remote]:number..., url..., `clean`) all dispatched via the same `*:` positional; `-m/--merge` switches between branch-tip vs merge-commit checkout. **`git-rename-tag`** (0 flags + 2 positionals): `<old-tag-name> <new-tag-name>` — local + remote tag rename. **`git-root`** (1 flag): `-r/--relative` for relative-from-root output, otherwise absolute root path. **`git-scp`** (1 flag + 2 positionals): secure-copy git changes via remote — `-h` for help; positional 1 = remote, positional 2+ = commits or paths; per upstream `git rscp` is the reverse-direction sibling that swaps the transfer direction (deliberately not stemmed by this completion since it's a separate command). **`git-setup`** (1 optional positional): `[<directory>]` — initialize a new repo in DIR (default cwd). **Blacklist additions (9) across 8 insertion blocks** (git-merge-repo + git-missing share one block): 1 between `git-machete` (9397) and `git-mediate` (9398) for `git-magic` (within git-ma* at index 5 `a` (97, both); at index 6 `c` (99, machete) < `g` (103, magic)); **2 between `git-merge-into` (9399) and `git-mob` (9400)** for `git-merge-repo` + `git-missing` (within git-merge-* at index 10 `i` (105, into) < `r` (114, repo); within git-m* at index 5 `e` (101, merge) < `i` (105, missing) < `o` (111, mob)); 1 between `git-number` (9408) and `git-octopus` (9409) for `git-obliterate` (at index 4 `n` (110, number) < `o` (111, both); within git-o* at index 5 `b` (98, obliterate) < `c` (99, octopus)); 1 between `git-pkgs` (9414) and `git-pulls` (9415) for `git-pr` (within git-p* at index 5 `k` (107, pkgs) < `r` (114, pr) < `u` (117, pulls)); 1 between `git-remote-hg` (9425) and `git-review` (9426) for `git-rename-tag` (within git-re* at index 6 `m` (109, remote) < `n` (110, rename) < `v` (118, review)); 1 between `git-revise` (9427) and `git-router` (9428) for `git-root` (within git-r* at index 5 `e` (101, revise) < `o` (111, root/router); within git-ro* at index 6 `o` (111, root) < `u` (117, router)); 1 between `git-router` (9428) and `git-secret` (9429) for `git-scp` (at index 4 `r` (114, router) < `s` (115, both scp/secret); within git-s* at index 5 `c` (99, scp) < `e` (101, secret)); 1 between `git-series` (9431) and `git-shell` (9432) for `git-setup` (within git-se* at index 6 `r` (114, series) < `t` (116, setup); within git-s* at index 5 `e` (101, setup) < `h` (104, shell)). LC_ALL=C sort verified directly (no mid-round corrections this round, in contrast to round 151's git-count fix).
- **git-extras Round 3 — git-abort + git-alias + git-authors + git-browse + git-bulk + git-coauthor + git-commits-since + git-count + git-fork + git-fresh-branch + git-graft + git-guilt + git-merge-into (13 more tj/git-extras subcommands via single multi-stem `_git-abort` file; cumulative git-extras coverage now 21 stems across rounds 150–151 + the pre-existing `_git-changelog`/`_git-info`/`_git-ignore`)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep; `git-info` and `git-ignore` are both pre-existing at `more_src/_git-info` and `more_src/_git-ignore` and were excluded from this round to avoid `#compdef` collisions). Surfaces transcribed directly from upstream manpages at [github.com/tj/git-extras](https://github.com/tj/git-extras) — `man/git-abort.1` / `man/git-alias.1` / `man/git-authors.1` / `man/git-browse.1` / `man/git-bulk.1` / `man/git-coauthor.1` / `man/git-commits-since.1` / `man/git-count.1` / `man/git-fork.1` / `man/git-fresh-branch.1` / `man/git-graft.1` / `man/git-guilt.1` / `man/git-merge-into.1`. **GitHub API `man/` directory listing now used as the canonical source-of-truth** (the listing for `tj/git-extras/contents/man?ref=master` returns reliable file presence in 130+-entry pages; this round verified by cross-checking each candidate against that listing before fetching). Single multi-stem file `_git-abort` is `#compdef git-abort git-alias git-authors git-browse git-bulk git-coauthor git-commits-since git-count git-fork git-fresh-branch git-graft git-guilt git-merge-into`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`git-abort`** (no flags, no positionals): aborts the current operation per upstream "There are no options, it just aborts current operation." **`git-alias`** (2-flag mutex + variable positionals): `--global` ↔ `--local` mutex; 9 synopsis shapes collapse to (optional flag) + (search-pattern or alias-name + command). **`git-authors`** (3 flags): `-l/--list` and `--no-email`. **`git-browse`** (4 positionals): `[remote_name] [file_name] [line_1] [line_2]` — remote defaults to first remote when omitted; line_2 forms a range with line_1. **`git-bulk`** (10 flags + variable positionals — the most-complex surface of this round): 6 distinct synopsis shapes encoded as a single 7-way mutex `(-a -w --addworkspace --removeworkspace --addcurrent --purge --listall)` with the modifier flag `-g` (confirmation prompt) usable across all execute-modes and the auxiliary flag `--from URL_OR_FILE` only meaningful with `--addworkspace`. **`git-coauthor`** (2 positionals): `<co-author> <co-author-email>`. **`git-commits-since`** (1 optional positional): date string (defaults to "last week" when omitted). **`git-count`** (1 flag): `--all` switches between total-commit-count and per-author breakdown. **`git-fork`** (1 optional positional): GitHub repo URL — works without args inside an existing GitHub repo directory. **`git-fresh-branch`** (1 positional): branch name for the new orphan branch. **`git-graft`** (2 positionals): `<src-branch> <dest-branch>` — merge src into dest. **`git-guilt`** (4 flags + 2 optional positionals): `-h` for usage, `-e/--email`, `-w/--ignore-whitespace`, `-d/--debug`; positional `<since> [<until>]` revisions. **`git-merge-into`** (1 flag + 2 positionals): `--ff-only` + `[src] <dest>` — src defaults to current branch when omitted. **Blacklist additions (13) across 13 insertion blocks** — **with one mid-round sort fix** caught by `LC_ALL=C sort -c` for `git-count`: 1 between `git` (9316) and `git-absorb` (9317) for `git-abort` (within git-* at index 5 `b` (98, both abort/absorb) consistent; at index 6 `o` (111, abort) < `s` (115, absorb)); 1 between `git-ai` (9318) and `git-annex` (9319) for `git-alias` (within git-a* at index 5 `i` (105, ai) < `l` (108, alias) < `n` (110, annex)); 1 between `git-archive-file` (9324) and `git-autofixup` (9325) for `git-authors` (within git-a* at index 5 `r` (114, archive) < `u` (117, both authors/autofixup);
