- **git-extras Round 2 — git-effort + git-summary + git-feature + git-release + git-mr + git-archive-file + git-touch (7 tj/git-extras subcommands via single multi-stem `_git-effort` file; extends the pre-existing `more_src/_git-changelog` to an 8-stem git-extras corpus, with Round 149's `_git-foresta`/`_git-stein` standalone files for adjacent git plugin coverage)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep; the existing `_git-changelog` covers the eighth main git-extras subcommand and was specifically excluded from this round to avoid `#compdef` collision). Surfaces transcribed directly from upstream manpages at [github.com/tj/git-extras](https://github.com/tj/git-extras) — `man/git-effort.1` / `man/git-summary.1` / `man/git-feature.1` / `man/git-release.1` / `man/git-mr.1` / `man/git-archive-file.1` / `man/git-touch.1`. **Source-404 deferrals**: `man/git-cleanup.1`, `man/git-hotfix.1`, `man/git-publish.1`, `man/git-unpublish.1`, `man/git-recall.1`, `man/git-since.1` — all 404 on direct fetch from the tj/git-extras `master` branch despite the subcommands being listed in the project README; defer per the source-404 precedent, will revisit if/when the man pages land. Single multi-stem file `_git-effort` is `#compdef git-effort git-summary git-feature git-release git-mr git-archive-file git-touch`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage** (each transcribed from the exact SYNOPSIS line in the corresponding upstream `.1` manpage): **`git-effort`** (1 flag + path positionals + post-`--` git log opts): `git-effort [--above <value>] [<path>...] [-- [<log options>...]]` — `--above N` ignores files with commits ≤ N; the `--` separator marks the boundary between effort options and `git log` options (the "Commit Limiting" section of `git-log` is the relevant subset per upstream). **`git-summary`** (4 flags + optional committish/path): two synopsis shapes — `git-summary [--dedup-by-email] [--no-merges] [<committish>]` and `git-summary --line [<path>]` — encoded as a 3-way mutex: `--line` cannot combine with `--dedup-by-email` or `--no-merges`; `--output-style tabular|oneline` is a 2-value enum applied across both shapes. **`git-feature`** (6 flags + NAME or `finish`): two synopsis shapes — create form `git-feature [-a PREFIX] [-s SEP] [-r [REMOTE]] [--from START] NAME...` and finish form `git-feature [-a PREFIX] [-s SEP] finish [--squash] NAME...`; `-a/--alias` defaults to `feature`, `-s/--separator` defaults to `/`, `-r/--remote` defaults to `origin` when its optarg is omitted, `--from` defaults to current branch when omitted; the `finish` literal positional triggers `--squash` availability. **`git-release`** (9 flags + tagname or hook args): semver-aware release with pre/post-release hooks; `--semver major|minor|patch` (3-value enum) drives auto-increment; `--prefix STRING` prepends to semver tags (e.g. `r4.4.0` → `r4.5.0` with `--prefix r`); `-r REMOTE` push destination; `-m MESSAGE` custom commit message; `--no-empty-commit`; `-c` generates/updates changelog; `-s` creates signed annotated tag; `-u KEY-ID` GPG key for signed tag; any arguments after the `--` are passed to pre/post-release hooks. **`git-mr`** (0 flags, 3 shapes): GitLab merge-request checkout — `git-mr <number> [<remote>]` (remote defaults to `origin`), `git-mr <url>` (parses full GitLab MR URL), `git-mr clean` (removes local MR-checkout branches). **`git-archive-file`** (no options): creates a ZIP of the current HEAD; upstream manpage explicitly states "This command does not take any options." **`git-touch`** (1 positional): creates + stages a new file in one operation. **Blacklist additions (7) across 7 insertion blocks**: 1 between `git-archive-all` (9323) and `git-autofixup` (9324) for `git-archive-file` (within git-archive-* at index 12 `a` (97, all) < `f` (102, file); within git-a* at index 5 `r` (114, archive) < `u` (117, autofixup)); 1 between `git-delta` (9349) and `git-extras` (9350) for `git-effort` (at index 4 `d` (100, delta) < `e` (101, effort) and `e` < `e` then at index 5 within git-e* `f` (102, effort) < `x` (120, extras)); 1 between `git-fame` (9351) and `git-filter-repo` (9352) for `git-feature` (within git-fa* at index 5 `a` (97, fame) consistent; within git-f* at index 5 `a` (97, fame) < `e` (101, feature) < `i` (105, filter)); 1 between `git-modified-branches.sh` (9386) and `git-multi` (9387) for `git-mr` (within git-m* at index 5 `o` (111, modified) < `r` (114, mr) < `u` (117, multi)); 1 between `git-relation` (9404) and `git-remote-codecommit` (9405) for `git-release` (within git-rel* at index 7 `a` (97, relation) < `e` (101, release); within git-re* at index 6 `l` (108, release) < `m` (109, remote)); 1 between `git-suggest-coauthors` (9428) and `git-svn` (9429) for `git-summary` (within git-su* at index 6 `g` (103, suggest) < `m` (109, summary); within git-s* at index 5 `u` (117, su*) < `v` (118, svn)); 1 between `git-sync` (9430) and `git-town` (9431) for `git-touch` (within git-t* at index 5 `o` (111, both); within git-to* at index 6 `u` (117, touch) < `w` (119, town); within git-s* at index 5 `u` (117, sync) < git-t* `t` (116) — wait, **'s' (115) < 't' (116)** so git-sync < git-touch). All position-by-position; sort verified directly via `LC_ALL=C sort -c` (no mid-round corrections needed this round, in contrast to round 149). LC_ALL=C sort verified.
- **JtR final mop-up Round 6 + git-* extras Round 1 — telegram2john + ios7tojohn + itunes_backup2john (3 last JtR helpers in `_telegram2john` multi-stem) + git-foresta + git-stein (2 fresh standalone git extensions, each in its own file)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). **JtR-side**: 3 stems verified via direct fetch of `run/telegram2john.py` / `run/ios7tojohn.pl` / `run/itunes_backup2john.pl`. This round flushes the long-running JtR campaign — the broader run/ directory listing on GitHub appears to have **substantial hallucinated entries** (the api/tree listings claim files like `openvpn2john`/`pgp2john`/`putty2john`/`raw2john`/`vdi2john`/`wallet2john`/`whirlpool2john`/`wincreds2john`/`sxc2john`/`dominosec2john`/`o5logon2john`/`odf2john` but every one of these 404s on direct raw fetch — the source-of-truth is the raw URL, not the listing API). **Source-404 deferrals**: all 12 of the above plus `racf2john` (deferred since round 145). **Already-covered skip log**: `truecrypt2john` (at `src/_truecrypt2john`) and `pwsafe2john` (at `src/_pwsafe2john`) — both source-verified this round but pre-existing in `src/`. **git-extras side**: 2 standalone tools picked from a broader hunt where most names 404 on upstream fetch (`git-bonsai`/`git-codeowners`/`git-friendly`/`git-tidy`/`git-tools`/`git-trial`/`git-clone-quick`/`git-lab` are all in the FRESH hit set but the first two 404 their READMEs on direct fetch; git-friendly's surface is 5 git-subcommands rather than a single binary so the JtR-style positional-file completion doesn't fit). Both verified surfaces transcribed from upstream READMEs: [github.com/takaaki-kasai/git-foresta](https://github.com/takaaki-kasai/git-foresta) and [github.com/sh5i/git-stein](https://github.com/sh5i/git-stein). **Per-stem coverage**: **`_telegram2john` multi-stem** `#compdef telegram2john ios7tojohn itunes_backup2john`. **`telegram2john`** (0 flags, 1+ positional files-or-dirs): Telegram Desktop hash extractor accepting either a Telegram data dir (recursively searched) or individual `userconfig.xml`/`map0`/`map1`/`key_datas` files; upstream strips trailing quote characters. Linux: `~/.local/share/TelegramDesktop`; Windows: `C:/Users/<Name>/AppData/Roaming/Telegram Desktop`. **`ios7tojohn`** (0 flags, 1+ `.plist` positionals): Apple iOS 7 restrictions-password plist parser; outputs PBKDF2-HMAC-SHA1 hashes; handles both single-line and multi-line XML `<data>` elements. **`itunes_backup2john`** (0 flags, 1+ `Manifest.plist` positionals): iTunes backup parser with two output formats by iOS version — pre-iOS 10 `$itunes_backup$*9*<wpky>*<iter>*<salt>**`, iOS 10.x+ `$itunes_backup$*10*<wpky>*<iter>*<salt>*<dpic>*<dpsl>`; WPKY/SALT/DPSL field lengths validated upstream (40/20/20 bytes). **`_git-foresta` single-stem**: 11 named flags — `--help`/`--version`, `--style 1|2|10|15` (4-value enum), `--svdepth=N` (default 2), `--graph-margin-left=N` (default 2), `--graph-margin-right=N` (default 1), 5 symbol-customization flags (`--graph-symbol-commit/merge/overpass/root/tip` with their respective `●`/`◎`/`═`/`■`/`○` defaults), `--no-status` — plus a final `*:git log argument:` catch-all because the script passes through to `git log` (and explicitly rejects `--pretty`/`--format` per upstream). **`_git-stein` single-stem**: 19 named flags + 1 source positional — covers all 3 documented modes (Overwrite = source only; Transform = source + `-o target`; Duplicate = source + `-o target` + `-d`); the completion encodes the `-o/--output`/`-d/--duplicate`/`-j/--jobs`/`-n/--dry-run`/`-q/--quiet`/`-v/--verbose` long-form ↔ short-form mutex pairs explicitly; `--log` carries a 9-value enum drawn from `java.util.logging.Level` (`OFF`/`SEVERE`/`WARNING`/`INFO`/`CONFIG`/`FINE`/`FINER`/`FINEST`/`ALL`). **Blacklist additions (5) across 5 insertion blocks** — and **one mid-round sort fix** caught by `LC_ALL=C sort -c` during the verification step: 1 between `git-flow` (9354) and `git-format-staged` (9355) for `git-foresta` (initially incorrectly placed AFTER `git-format-staged`; the `sort -c` recheck reported "disorder: git-foresta at 9356"; within git-f* at index 5 `l` (108, flow) < `o` (111, format/foresta); within git-fo* at index 7 `e` (101, foresta) < `m` (109, format) — so `git-foresta` < `git-format-staged`); 1 between `git-stats` (9421) and `git-submodule-move` (9422) for `git-stein` (also initially incorrectly placed BETWEEN `git-stack` and `git-standup`; `sort -c` reported "disorder: git-standup at 9422"; within git-s* at index 5 `t` (116, st*) < `u` (117, submodule)); 1 between `ios-deploy` (11890) and `ios_webkit_debug_proxy` (11891) for `ios7tojohn` (within ios* at index 3 `-` (45, deploy) < `7` (55, ios7tojohn) < `_` (95, webkit)); Single multi-stem file `_DPAPImk2john` is `#compdef DPAPImk2john adxcsouf2john apop2john diskcryptor2john ejabberd2john encdatavault2john fvde2john geli2john gitea2john ibmiscanner2john iwork2john keplr2john known_hosts2john krb2john`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage** — this round contains the **most-complex single surface added to the JtR helpers so far** (`DPAPImk2john`) plus several that are still simple positional extractors: **`DPAPImk2john`** (~6 flags, 0 positionals — the only round-147 stem with non-trivial flag handling): Windows DPAPI masterkey extractor with two mutually exclusive operating modes — the **Standard mode** requires all three of `-S/--sid SID` + `-mk/--masterkey FILE` + `-c/--context CONTEXT` (where CONTEXT is the 4-value enum `domain|domain1607+|domain1607-|local`), while the **Preferred mode** takes `-P/--preferred FILE` alone and the completion encodes mutual exclusion by listing `(-P --preferred)` on each Standard-mode flag and `(-mk --masterkey -S --sid -c --context)` on each Preferred-mode flag; shared across both modes: `-d/--debug` and `--password=PASSWORD`. **`adxcsouf2john`** (0 flags, 1+ `*.DAT` positionals): IBM/Toshiba 4690 OS ADXCSOUF.DAT/ADXEPW0F.DAT password-hash extractor; upstream prints "Tip: Maximum password length is 8 on IBM/Toshiba 4690 systems" to stderr. **`apop2john`** (0 flags, 1+ pcap positionals): APOP challenge/response extractor from packet captures; output format `username:$dynamic_1017$hash$HEX$salt`; requires `scapy`. **`diskcryptor2john`** (0 flags, 1+ device/raw-image positionals): DiskCryptor volume-header extractor; reads first 2048 bytes, calculates entropy, warns if <6 bits/byte unless env-var `FORCE=1` is set; cascaded ciphers explicitly not supported per upstream comment. **`ejabberd2john`** (0 flags, 1+ positionals): parses files generated by `ejabberdctl dump`. **`encdatavault2john`** (0 flags, **1 directory** positional): ENCSecurity DataVault folder extractor — takes a directory not a file, so the completion uses `_files -/` to restrict completion to dirs. **`fvde2john`** (0 flags, exactly 1 positional via argparse): FileVault Drive Encryption disk-image extractor. **`geli2john`** (0 flags, 1+ disk-image positionals): FreeBSD GELI metadata extractor; seeks to last 1024 bytes, looks for `GEOM::ELI` magic, supports AES-XTS and AES-CBC, metadata versions 0-7. **`gitea2john`** (1 flag, **stdin-driven**): `-h/--help` plus stdin input format `username:hex_salt:hex_hash:algorithm` where algorithm follows `pbkdf2$iterations$keylen`; typical pipeline `sqlite3 gitea.db 'SELECT name,salt,passwd,passwd_hash_algo FROM user;' | gitea2john.py`. **`ibmiscanner2john`** (0 flags, 1+ positionals): IBM iSeries (ibmiscanner output) → AS400-SHA converter; transforms `username:hexhash` → `username:$as400ssha1$hexhash$username`. **`iwork2john`** (0 flags, 1+ Apple-iWork positionals — `.key`/`.numbers`/`.pages`): handles both iWork '09 and 2013/2014 formats. **`keplr2john`** (0 flags, **2 positionals** — 1 required folder + 1 optional password): Keplr Chrome-extension LevelDB extractor; when the optional 2nd arg (password) is supplied the script attempts scrypt-KDF + AES-128-CTR decryption rather than just dumping; upstream comment requires that the first arg must **not** begin with a hyphen. **`known_hosts2john`** (0 flags, 1+ positionals): hashed-entry extractor from SSH known_hosts files; lines starting `|1|` go to stdout as `$known_hosts$<data>`, non-hashed entries go to stderr. **`krb2john`** (0 flags, 1+ `.pdml` positionals): Kerberos hash extractor from PDML (packet description markup language) files generated by `tshark -r capture.pcap -T pdml`. **Blacklist additions (14) across 14 insertion blocks** — verified position-by-position: 1 between `DP3` (69) and `DPPP` (70) for `DPAPImk2john` (within DP* at index 2 `3` (51) < `A` (65) < `P` (80) — the only round-147 insert in the uppercase block); 1 between `adwaita-1-demo` (637) and `aea` (638) for `adxcsouf2john` (within ad* at index 2 `v` (118, adv) < `w` (119, adw) < `x` (120, adx); at index 1 `d` (100, ad) < `e` (101, ae)); 1 between `apollo` (1125) and `app-sso` (1126) for `apop2john` (within apo* at index 3 `l` (108, llo) < `p` (112, pop); at index 2 `o` (111, apo) < `p` (112, app)); 1 between `diskard` (6276) and `diskinfo` (6277) for `diskcryptor2john` (within disk* at index 4 `a` (97, ard) < `c` (99, cryptor) < `i` (105, info)); 1 between `eix` (7165) and `ejabberdctl` (7166) for `ejabberd2john` (within e* at index 1 `i` (105, eix) < `j` (106, ejabb); within ejabberd* at index 8 `2` (50, john) < `c` (99, ctl)); 1 between `enca` (7286) and `encfs` (7287) for `encdatavault2john` (within enc* at index 3 `a` (97, enca) < `d` (100, encdata) < `f` (102, encfs)); 1 between `fuzztran` (8605) and `fvdeinfo` (8606) for `fvde2john` (within f* at index 1 `u` (117, fuzz) < `v` (118, fvde); within fvde* at index 4 `2` (50, john) < `i` (105, info)); 1 between `geli` (8986) and `gem` (8987) for `geli2john` (within g* at index 2 `l` (108, geli) < `m` (109, gem); validates magic byte (`0x5` = standard, `0x76` = untested alt). **`cisco2john`** (1 flag, 0+ positionals — **stdin-fallback**): `cisco2john [-h] [cisco config file(s)]` — `-h` shows usage and exits; with 0 file args the script reads stdin via `while (<>)`. Output goes to stdout (extracted hashes) and stderr (plaintext + seed data for a wordlist-rules workflow). **`coinomi2john`** (0 flags, 1+ positionals): Coinomi wallet parser; uses protobuf + scrypt + AES output format. **`cracf2john`** (0 flags, 1+ positionals): IBM RACF CRACF.TXT converter; - **John the Ripper `*2john` family Round 1 — unshadow + ssh2john + keepass2john + 7z2john + bitcoin2john + pdf2john + keychain2john + keystore2john + bitwarden2john + htdigest2john + monero2john (11 hash-extractor stems via single multi-stem file; extends the existing `_john` + `_zip2john` + `_rar2john` + `_wpapcap2john` coverage to a 15-stem JtR-helper corpus)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep; the pre-existing `_john` is also dup'd by stock zsh at `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh/site-functions/_john` but the 11 stems in this round are all stock-clean). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream JtR sources at [github.com/openwall/john (bleeding-jumbo)](https://github.com/openwall/john) — `src/*.c` for compiled helpers (`unshadow.c`/`keepass2john.c`) and `run/*.py`/`run/*.pl` for script helpers (`ssh2john.py`/`7z2john.pl`/`bitcoin2john.py`/`pdf2john.pl`/`keychain2john.py`/`keystore2john.py`/`bitwarden2john.py`/`htdigest2john.py`/`monero2john.py`). **The Debian-shipped manpages.debian.org pages all 302-redirect to a `dyn.manpages.debian.org` host that 404s the same content**, so this round abandoned man-page-based verification in favor of direct source-tree reading — the JtR sources display canonical usage strings (`fprintf(stderr, "Usage: %s …")`) that yield reliable surfaces. **Conflict-avoidance during writing**: initially the multi-stem `#compdef` line included `rar2john` and `wpapcap2john`, but the `^#compdef( |.* )<name>( |$)` recheck caught that both already have dedicated single-stem files at `src/_rar2john` and `src/_wpapcap2john`; both were removed from the new file before commit (would have produced double-#compdef registrations and broken at compinit time). **Hunt-dup-skip log this round**: ~25 candidates from a broader hunt of `*2john` helpers in `openwall/john/run/` — `ethereum2john`/`lastpass2john`/`pcap2john`/`gpg2john`/`dmg2john`/`bitlocker2john`/`androidfde2john`/`axcrypt2john`/`dashlane2john`/`ecryptfs2john`/`encfs2john`/`filezilla2john`/`ikescan2john`/`lotus2john`/`mongodb2john`/`office2john`/`pfx2john`/`pgpdisk2john`/`pwsafe2john`/`racf2john`/`sap2john`/`sipdump2john`/`sshng2john`/`uaf2john`/`vmx2john`/`zed2john` — these are deferred not because they don't exist (the GitHub `run/` directory listing confirms many do) but because their source files were not individually read this round to verify surface; per the no-vibe-coding rule the harvest claims only what's verified, and a future round can extend the multi-stem after reading each `.py`/`.pl`/`.c` source. Single multi-stem file `_unshadow` is `#compdef unshadow ssh2john keepass2john 7z2john bitcoin2john pdf2john keychain2john keystore2john bitwarden2john htdigest2john monero2john`, dispatching on `$service`. **Per-stem coverage** (each transcribed from the exact `Usage:` string in upstream source): **`unshadow`** (0 flags, exactly 2 positionals): `unshadow PASSWORD-FILE SHADOW-FILE` — the JtR helper that merges a Unix `/etc/passwd` and `/etc/shadow` into the JtR-cracking-friendly combined format. **`ssh2john`** (0 flags, 1+ positionals): `ssh2john <RSA/DSA/EC/OpenSSH private key file(s)>` — extracts crackable hashes from SSH private keys; the `.py` script iterates `sys.argv[1:]` with no option parsing. **`keepass2john`** (1 flag, 1+ positionals): `keepass2john [-k <keyfile>] <.kdbx database(s)>` — `-k` registers an optional KeePass keyfile for two-factor crack inputs. **`7z2john`** (1 flag, 1+ positionals): `7z2john.pl [--skip-sensitive-data-warning] <7-Zip file>...` — the single flag suppresses the default "hashes may contain sensitive encrypted data" warning printed to stderr. **`bitcoin2john`** (0 flags, 1+ positionals): `bitcoin2john [Bitcoin/Litecoin/PRiVCY wallet (.dat) files]` — the same `.py` extracts wallet hashes from Bitcoin, Litecoin, and PRiVCY-format `.dat` files. **`pdf2john`** (treated as 0 flags + 1+ positionals): the upstream `pdf2john.pl` is wired through ExifTool which exposes ExifTool's full flag surface, but the canonical contract documented in the synopsis is `pdf2john.pl <.pdf file(s)>` — keeping the completion to the documented contract avoids advertising ExifTool's incidental flags as if they were `pdf2john`'s own. **`keychain2john`** (0 flags, 1+ positionals): `keychain2john [keychain files]` — extracts hashes from macOS `*.keychain*` files. **`keystore2john`** (0 flags, 1+ positionals): `keystore2john.py <.keystore / .jks file(s)>` — extracts hashes from Java KeyStore files. **`bitwarden2john`** (0 flags, 1+ positional files-or-dirs): `bitwarden_extract.py <Bitwarden storage.js / com.x8bit.bitwarden_preferences.xml / Google Chrome's 'nngceckbap…' path>` — accepts any of three input shapes (Firefox extension storage, Android preferences XML, or a Chrome LevelDB directory path). **`htdigest2john`** (0 flags, 1+ positionals): `htdigest2john.py <htdigest file(s)>` — Apache htdigest hash extractor. **`monero2john`** (0 flags, 1+ positionals): `monero2john.py [Monero .keys file(s)]` — extracts hashes from Monero wallet `.keys` files. **Blacklist additions (11) across 11 insertion blocks**: 1 between `7z` (36) and `7za` (37) for `7z2john` (within 7z* at index 2 digit `2` (50) < lowercase `a` (97)); 1 between `bitcoin-wallet` (2224) and `bitcoind` (2225) for `bitcoin2john` (within bitcoin* at index 7 `-` (45) < `2` (50) < `d` (100)); 1 between `bitwarden-cli` (2234) and `bitwise` (2235) for `bitwarden2john` (within bitwarden* at index 9 `-` (45) < `2` (50); at index 4 within bitw* `a` (97, warden) < `i` (105, wise)); 1 between `htdigest2` (11078) and `htlatex` (11079) for `htdigest2john` (within htdigest2* at index 9 end-of-string < `j` (106); at index 2 within ht* `d` (100, digest) < `l` (108, latex)); 1 between `keepass2` (12751) and `keepassxc` (12752) for `keepass2john` (within keepass* at index 7 `2` (50) but within keepass2* at index 8 end < `j` (106); at index 7 within keepass* `2` (50) < `x` (120)); 1 between `keychain` (12789) and `keycloak` (12790) for `keychain2john` (within keychain* at index 8 end < `2` (50); at index 4 within keyc* `h` (104, chain) < `l` (108, cloak)); 1 between `keystone-wsgi-public` (12811) and `keytool` (12812) for `keystore2john` (within keysto* at index 6 `n` (110, stone) < `r` (114, store); at index 3 within key* `s` (115, store) < `t` (116, tool)); 1 between `monero-wallet-rpc` (16375) and `monerod` (16376) for `monero2john` (within monero* at index 6 `-` (45) < `2` (50) < `d` (100)); 1 between `pdf2htmlex` (19166) and The `ALGORITHM` value is currently always `1` (SHA-1, the only NSEC3-defined algorithm). **File 2 — `_zkg` single-stem state-machine completion for the Zeek package manager**. **`load`** (`--nodeps`); **`unload`** (`--force`/`--nodeps`); **`list`** (`--nodesc`/`--include-builtin`, positional category enum `installed|not_installed|loaded|unloaded|outdated|all`); **`info`** (`--version`/`--nolocal`/`--include-builtin`/`--json`/`--jsonpretty SPACES`/`--allvers`); **`autoconfig`** (`--force`); **`create`** (`--packagedir DIR` required/`--version`/repeatable `*--features`/`--template URL`/`--force`/repeatable `*--user-var`); **`template`** has its own nested state machine with a single sub-subcommand `template info` (`--json`/`--jsonpretty SPACES`/`--version`). **Blacklist additions (4) across 4 insertion blocks**: 1 between `arpalert` (1363) and `arpd` (1364) for `arpaname` (within arpa* at index 4 `l` (108, alert) < `n` (110, name); **`_strip_dsr` (13 values)** — `rastrip -M` Data Source Record names (`flow`/`time`/`metric`/`agr`/`net`/`vlan`/`mpls`/`jitter`/`ipattr`/`suser`/`duser`/`mac`/`icmp`/`encaps`). **Per-stem coverage**: **`racluster`** (5 flags beyond shared): `-f racluster.conf`, repeatable `*-m OBJECT` (from `_agg`), repeatable **`*-M MODE`** 6-value enum (`correct`/`nocorrect`/`norep`/`rmon`/`ind`/`replace`), `-P N` (parallel processors, default 1), `-V` verbose; cluster (`--tls`, `--tls-ca`, `--tls-cert`, `--tls-key`), Spread (repeatable `*--group`, **`--groupby` 5-value enum** `port|vlan|applabel|protocol|version`), privilege drop cluster (repeatable `*--plugin-name` + `--plugin-opts` + repeatable `*--plugin-conf`), p0f passive-OS-fingerprinting cluster (`--p0fprint` + `--p0f-fingerprints` + `--fpexport`). **`yafscii`** (IPFIX Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream CERT NetSA per-tool docs at [tools.netsa.cert.org/silk/rwappend.html](https://tools.netsa.cert.org/silk/rwappend.html) + `rwcombine.html`/`rwdedupe.html`/`rwmatch.html`/`rwnetmask.html`/`rwrandomizeip.html`/`rwgeoip2ccmap.html`/`rwpackchecker.html`. **Deferred per the source-404 precedent**: `rwconvert` and `rwallroute` — both pages return HTTP 404 upstream; will revisit when archives expose them. Single multi-stem file `_rwappend` is `#compdef rwappend rwcombine rwdedupe rwmatch rwnetmask rwrandomizeip rwgeoip2ccmap rwpackchecker`, dispatching on `$service`. Shared `_meta` (6 flags) carries the standard CERT NetSA header-annotation + compression + help/version cluster — applied only where the per-tool doc explicitly lists those flags, since `rwgeoip2ccmap` and `rwpackchecker` have stripped-down surfaces. **Per-stem coverage**: **`rwappend`** (3 flags beyond shared): `--create=-` (optional TEMPLATE_FILE; format/version/byte-order is inherited from template if given), `--print-statistics` (stderr report of per-source record counts + total appended), positional 1 = target SiLK file + repeatable positional sources. **`rwcombine`** (11 flags beyond shared): `--actions all|timeout` (combination strategy), **`--ignore-fields`** 12-value `_values -s ,` enum (`sIP`/`dIP`/`sPort`/`dPort`/`protocol`/`sensor`/`in`/`out`/`nhIP`/`class`/`type`/`application`), `--max-idle-time N` (seconds), `--print-statistics=-` (optional FILE), `--temp-directory`, `--buffer-size` (K/M/G suffixes, default ~2GB), `--print-filenames`, `--output-path`, repeatable `*--xargs`, `--help-fields`. **`rwdedupe`** (12 flags beyond shared): **`--ignore-fields`** 20-value `_values -s ,` enum (the dedupe surface extends combine's 12 with `packets`/`bytes`/`flags`/`sTime`/`duration`/`initialFlags`/`sessionFlags`/`attributes`), per-field delta tolerances (`--packets-delta N`/`--bytes-delta N`/`--stime-delta FLOAT_ms`/`--duration-delta FLOAT_ms`), `--temp-directory`, `--buffer-size`, `--print-filenames`, `--output-path`, repeatable `*--xargs`, `--help-fields`. **`rwmatch`** (10 flags beyond shared, 3 positionals): **repeatable `*--relate FIELD_PAIR`** (required ≥1), `--time-delta` (seconds), **3-flag time-mode mutex** `--absolute-delta` (default) ↔ `--relative-delta` ↔ `--infinite-delta`, `--symmetric-delta` (allow initial flow in response), `--unmatched q|r|b` (3-value enum), `--ipv6-policy ignore|asv4|mix|force|only`, `--help-relate`, positional 1 = query / 2 = response / 3 = output SiLK file. **`rwnetmask`** (13 flags beyond shared): per-axis IPv4/IPv6 prefix-length controls — `--4sip-prefix-length`/`--4dip-prefix-length`/`--4nhip-prefix-length` + their IPv6 counterparts `--6sip-`/`--6dip-`/`--6nhip-prefix-length` + 3 deprecated aliases (`--sip-prefix-length` = `--4sip-prefix-length`, etc), `--output-path`, `--print-filenames`, `--ipv6-policy`, repeatable `*--xargs`. **`rwrandomizeip`** (7 flags beyond shared, 2 positionals): `--seed N`, IPset filtering (`--only-change-set IPSET` ↔ `--dont-change-set IPSET`), `--consistent` (deterministic input → output IP mapping), state persistence (`--save-table FILE` / `--load-table FILE`), positional 1 = input / 2 = output. **`rwgeoip2ccmap`** (10 flags + 5 deprecated, **no shared `_meta`** — distinct annotation/help cluster matching upstream): **`--mode`** 7-value enum `auto|ipv4|ipv6|csv|binary|geoip2|legacy`, `--input-path`, `--output-path` (binary CC prefix-map), `--dry-run`, **`--fields`** 5-value `_values -s ,` enum (`location`/`registered`/`represented`/`flags`/`continent` — GeoName field priority), `--note-add`, `--note-file-add`, `--invocation-strip`, plus 5 deprecated legacy flags (`--csv-input`/`--v6-csv-input`/`--encoded-input`/`--input-file`/`--output-file`). **`rwpackchecker`** (5 flags + help/version — **stripped-down surface, no shared `_meta`**): repeatable `*--value TEST=VALUE`, repeatable `*--allowable-count TEST=ALLOWED`, `--print-all`, repeatable `*--xargs`, positional input SiLK files. **Blacklist additions (8)**: 1 inserted between `rwall` (22761) and `rwbagbuild` (22762) for `rwappend`; 1 between `rwcat` (22767) and `rwcount` (22768) for `rwcombine`; 1 between `rwcount` (22768) and `rwfileinfo` (22769) for `rwdedupe`; 1 between `rwflowpack` (22772) and `rwgroup` (22773) for `rwgeoip2ccmap`; 3 between `rwipfix2silk` (22776) and `rwpmapbuild` (22777) for `rwmatch` + `rwnetmask` + `rwpackchecker`; 1 between `rwpollexec` (22780) and `rwreceiver` (22781) for `rwrandomizeip`. Sort verified position-by-position: at index 2 within rw* 'a' (97) < 'b' (98) so `rwappend` < `rwb*`; at index 3 within rwc* 'a' (cat) < 'o' (combine, count) and at index 4 within rwco* 'm' (109, combine) < 'u' (117, count) so `rwcat` < `rwcombine` < `rwcount`; at index 2 within rw* 'c' (count) < 'd' (dedupe) < 'f' (fileinfo); at index 2 'f' (flowpack) < 'g' (geoip2ccmap) and at index 3 within rwg* 'e' (101, geoip) < 'r' (114, group) so `rwgeoip2ccmap` < `rwgroup`; at index 2 'i' (ipfix) < 'm' (match) < 'n' (netmask) < 'p' (packchecker, pmap) and at index 3 within rwp* 'a' (97, packchecker) < 'm' (109, pmap) so `rwpackchecker` < `rwpmapbuild`; at index 2 within rwp/rwr 'p' (pollexec) < 'r' (randomizeip) and at index 3 within rwr* 'a' (97, randomizeip) < 'e' (101, receiver) so `rwrandomizeip` < `rwreceiver`. Single multi-stem file `_rwflowpack` is `#compdef rwflowpack rwflowappend rwpollexec rwsender rwreceiver`, dispatching on `$service` — covers the SiLK daemon pipeline (probe-side packing → hourly-file appending → directory-scan exec → encrypted file transfer). Three shared sub-arrays collapse the repetitive surfaces: **`_log` (7 flags)** carries the canonical 3-flag log-destination mutex (`--log-destination none|stdout|stderr|syslog|both` ↔ `--log-pathname FILE` ↔ `--log-directory DIR`) plus rotation/severity config (`--log-basename`, `--log-level emerg|alert|crit|err|warning|notice|info|debug`, `--log-sysfacility`, `--log-post-rotate`); **`_daemon` (5 flags)** carries `--pidfile`, `--no-chdir`, `--no-daemon`, `--help`, `--version`; **`_tls` (8 flags)** carries the GnuTLS cluster (`--tls-ca`/`--tls-cert`/`--tls-key`/`--tls-pkcs12`/`--tls-priority`/`--tls-security low|medium|high|ultra`/`--tls-crl`/`--tls-debug-level`). **Per-stem coverage**: **`rwflowpack`** (24 flags beyond shared): **`--input-mode` 4-value enum** `stream|fcfiles|pdufile|respool` driving four conditional flag groups, **`--output-mode` 3-value enum** `local-storage|incremental-files|sending`, `--sensor-configuration`, `--packing-logic`, `--sensor-name`, `--polling-interval`, `--incoming-directory`, `--netflow-file` (pdufile mode), `--root-directory`, `--incremental-directory`, `--sender-directory`, `--no-file-locking`, `--flush-timeout` (default 120s), `--file-cache-size` (default 128 open files), `--pack-interfaces`, `--byte-order native|big|little`, `--compression-method none|zlib|lzo1x|snappy|best`, `--site-config-file`, `--error-directory`, `--archive-directory`, `--flat-archive`, `--post-archive-command`, `--verify-sensor-config`. **`rwflowappend`** (15 flags beyond shared): `--incoming-directory` + `--root-directory` + `--error-directory` (all required), `--archive-directory`, `--flat-archive`, `--post-command`, `--hour-file-command`, `--threads` (default 1), `--reject-hours-past`/`--reject-hours-future`, `--no-file-locking`, `--polling-interval` (default 15s), **`--byte-order` 4-value enum** `as-is|native|big|little` (the `as-is` extra value distinguishes it from rwflowpack's 3-value enum), `--compression-method`, `--site-config-file`. **`rwpollexec`** (8 flags beyond shared): `--incoming-directory` + `--command` (with `%s` file substitution) + `--error-directory` (all required), `--archive-directory`, `--flat-archive`, `--simultaneous` (1-50, default 1), **repeatable `*--timeout=SIGNAL,SECS`** (send signal after timeout), `--polling-interval`. **`rwsender`** (17 flags beyond shared+tls, 7 of them repeatable): `--identifier`, **2-flag mutex** `--mode server|client`, `--incoming-directory`, `--processing-directory`, `--error-directory`, `--server-port` (server mode), repeatable `*--client-ident` (server mode), repeatable `*--server-address IDENT:HOST:PORT` (client mode), repeatable `*--local-directory [IDENT:]DIR` (duplicate copies), `--unique-local-copies`, repeatable `*--filter IDENT:REGEXP` (routing), repeatable `*--priority NUM:REGEXP` (0-100, default 50), `--polling-interval`, `--send-attempts` (0=unlimited), `--block-size` (256-65535, default 8192). **`rwreceiver`** (12 flags beyond shared+tls): `--identifier`, `--mode server|client`, `--destination-directory`, server flags (`--server-port` + repeatable `*--client-ident`), client flag (repeatable `*--server-address`), `--post-command` (supports `%s` for path, `%I` for sender ID, `%%` for literal %), repeatable `*--duplicate-destination`, `--unique-duplicates`, `--freespace-minimum` (supports K/M/G/T suffixes), `--space-maximum-percent` (default 100). **Blacklist additions (5)**: 2 inserted between `rwfilter` (22770) and `rwgroup` (22771) for the `rwflow*` block (`rwflowappend` → `rwflowpack`); 3 between `rwpmaplookup` (22777) and `rwsetbuild` (22778) for the `rwpollexec`+`rwreceiver`+`rwsender` block. Sort verified position-by-position: at index 3 within rwf* 'i' (filter, 105) < 'l' (flow, 108) so `rwflow*` > `rwfilter`; at index 6 within rwflow* 'a' (append, 97) < 'p' (pack, 112) so `rwflowappend` < `rwflowpack`; at index 2 'p' (pollexec) < 'r' (receiver) < 's' (sender), at index 3 within rws* `rwsender` 'e' then index 4 'n' (110) < 't' (rwsetbuild, 116) so `rwsender` < `rwsetbuild`. - **SiLK Round 2 — rwsetbuild + rwsetcat + rwsetmember + rwsetintersect + rwsetunion + rwsettool + rwbagbuild + rwbagcat + rwbagtool (9 binary stems via single multi-stem file, extends round-135 SiLK coverage to 17)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream CERT NetSA docs at [tools.netsa.cert.org/silk/rwsetbuild.html](https://tools.netsa.cert.org/silk/rwsetbuild.html) plus per-tool pages (`rwsetcat.html`/`rwsettool.html`/`rwbagbuild.html`/`rwbagcat.html`/`rwbagtool.html`). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (15 already-covered)**: LVM family `lvm`/`lvchange`/`lvcreate`/`lvremove`/`lvdisplay`/`lvs`/`vgcreate`/`vgremove`/`pvcreate`/`pvremove`/`pvs`/`vgs`/`lvconvert`/`lvextend`/`lvreduce` all at `man_src/_*` (a beautifully-comprehensive man-page-derived LVM corpus already in the repo). Single multi-stem file `_rwsetbuild` is `#compdef rwsetbuild rwsetcat rwsetmember rwsetintersect rwsetunion rwsettool rwbagbuild rwbagcat rwbagtool`, dispatching on `$service` — covers the IPset + Bag construction/manipulation half of the SiLK suite. The 9 tools share metadata + display flag sub-arrays. **Shared `_meta` array** (6 flags): `--note-add`/`--note-file-add`/`--invocation-strip` (header annotations), `--compression-method none|zlib|lzo1x|snappy|best`, `--help`/`--version`. **Shared `_disp` array** (8 flags, used in cat/display tools): `--output-path`, `--pager`, `--print-filenames`, `--no-columns`, `--column-separator`, `--no-final-delimiter`, `--delimited`, `--ip-format` (6-value enum: `canonical`/`decimal`/`hex`/`zero-padded`/`any-cidr`/`force-ipv6`). **Per-stem coverage**: **`rwsetbuild`** (text → IPset): `--ip-ranges[=DELIM]` (allow range pairs, default hyphen), `--record-version 0|2|3|4|5` (IPset format), positional `infile`/`outfile`. **`rwsetcat`** (print IPset contents): inherits `_disp`, plus `--count-ips`, `--print-ips`, `--print-statistics`, **3-flag mutex** `--cidr-blocks` ↔ `--ip-ranges` ↔ `--network-structure` (output style), deprecated `--integer-ips`/`--zero-pad-ips`. **`rwsetmember`** (test IPs against IPset): inherits `_disp`, `--count-records`, positionals 1=CIDR/IP pattern + repeatable IPset files. **`rwsetintersect`/`rwsetunion`** (thin wrappers — pre-set `rwsettool` mode): `--output-path`, `--record-version`, repeatable IPset inputs. **`rwsettool`** (general set arithmetic, 17 flags + 7-flag operation mutex): `--union` ↔ `--intersect` ↔ `--difference` ↔ `--symmetric-difference` ↔ `--sample` ↔ `--mask BLOCK-SIZE` ↔ `--fill-blocks BLOCK-SIZE`; sample modifiers `--size`/`--ratio 0.0..1.0`/`--seed`; output `--output-path`, `--modify-inplace` (atomic in-place via tmpfile), `--backup-path`, `--record-version`, `--note-strip`. **`rwbagbuild`** (text or IPset → Bag): `--set-input` ↔ `--bag-input` (2-flag input-source mutex), `--delimiter` (default `|`), `--proto-port-delimiter`, `--default-count`, **`--key-type` 12-value enum** (`sIPv4`/`dIPv4`/`sIPv6`/`dIPv6`/`sip-country`/`dip-country`/`sport`/`dport`/`protocol`/`stcpflags`/`dtcpflags`/`input`/`output`), **`--counter-type` 6-value enum** (`packets`/`bytes`/`records`/`sum-packets`/`sum-bytes`/`any-flag`), `--pmap-file MAPNAME:PATH`. **`rwbagcat`** (print Bag contents, ~14 flags): inherits `_disp` plus Bag-specific `--network-structure`, `--bin-ips` (invert: counter-bins by frequency), `--sort-counters increasing|decreasing`, range filters (`--minkey`/`--maxkey`/`--mincounter`/`--maxcounter`), `--mask-set FILE` (IPset filter), `--zero-counts` (include zero records), `--key-format` 7-value enum (`decimal`/`canonical`/`hex`/`zero-padded`/`timestamp`/`duration`/`epoch`), `--pmap-file`, `--print-statistics`, `--site-config-file`. **`rwbagtool`** (Bag arithmetic + filtering, 19 flags + 7-flag operation mutex): `--add` ↔ `--subtract` ↔ `--minimize` ↔ `--maximize` ↔ `--divide` ↔ `--scalar-multiply N` ↔ `--compare lt|le|eq|ge|gt`; masking `--intersect SETFILE`/`--complement-intersect SETFILE`, range filters (`--mincounter`/`--maxcounter`/`--minkey`/`--maxkey`), output transforms `--invert` (swap keys/counters), `--coverset` (output IPset instead of Bag) + `--ipset-record-version`, atomic write `--modify-inplace`/`--backup-path`, `--note-strip`. **Blacklist additions (9)**: 3 between `rwall` (22757) and `rwbypid.d` (22758) for the `rwbag*` block (`rwbagbuild`/`rwbagcat`/`rwbagtool`) and 6 between `rwhod` (22766) and `rwsnoop` (22767+) for the `rwset*` block (`rwsetbuild`/`rwsetcat`/`rwsetintersect`/`rwsetmember`/`rwsettool`/`rwsetunion`). Sort verified position-by-position: at index 2 the rw* block resolves as 'a' < 'b' < 'h' < 's'; within `rwbag*` at index 5 'b' (build) < 'c' (cat) < 't' (tool); within `rwset*` at index 5 'b' (build) < 'c' (cat) < 'i' (intersect) < 'm' (member) < 't' (tool) < 'u' (union); at index 3 `rwset*`'s 'e' (101) < `rwsnoop`'s 'n' (110). LC_ALL=C sort verified.
- **SiLK rw* family — rwfilter + rwstats + rwsort + rwuniq + rwcat + rwcount + rwfileinfo + rwgroup (8 binary stems via single multi-stem file)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Single multi-stem file `_rwfilter` is `#compdef rwfilter rwstats rwsort rwuniq rwcat rwcount rwfileinfo rwgroup`, dispatching on `$service` — covers CERT NetSA's flow-record analysis suite for IPFIX/NetFlow traffic. The 8 tools share an output framework but each has its own selection/aggregation surface. **Shared `_io` array** (14 flags re-applied per stem): `--output-path` (default stdout), repeatable `*--xargs FILE` (read filenames from file/stdin), `--print-filenames`, `--compression-method none|zlib|lzo1x|snappy|best`, `--note-add`/`--note-file-add` (annotate output header), `--site-config-file`, repeatable `*--plugin` (load C plugin), repeatable `*--pmap-file MAPNAME:PATH` (prefix maps for IP/port labels), repeatable `*--python-file *.py` (custom field code), `--temp-directory`, `--help`/`--version`/`--help-fields`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`rwfilter`** (~45 selection flags) — the workhorse query tool: time (`--start-date`/`--end-date YYYY/MM/DD[:HH]`, `--stime`/`--etime`/`--active-time`/`--duration`), repo (`--data-rootdir`, `--class`/`--type`/`--flowtypes`/`--sensors`), addresses (repeatable `*--scidr`/`*--dcidr`/`*--any-cidr` + `*--not-` negations, `*--saddress`/`*--daddress`/`*--any-address`, `*--sipset`/`*--dipset`/`*--anyset` for IPset-file lookups), ports/protos (`--sport`/`--dport`/`--aport`, `--protocol`, `--icmp-type`/`--icmp-code`), TCP flags (3-flag set `--flags-all`/`--flags-initial`/`--flags-session`), volume (`--bytes`/`--packets`/`--bytes-per-packet`), output partitioning (`--pass-destination`/`--fail-destination`/`--all-destination`), statistics (`--print-statistics`/`--print-volume-statistics`/`--max-pass-records`/`--max-fail-records`), advanced (`--tuple-file`/`--python-expr`/`--threads`/`--dry-run`). **`rwstats`** (Top-N/Bottom-N aggregation): `--fields`/`--values`, output limiting trio (`--count N`/`--threshold value`/`--percentage N`), **sort-direction mutex** `--top` ↔ `--bottom`, `--no-titles`/`--column-separator`. **`rwsort`**: `--fields` (sort keys), `--presorted-input` (merge-sort), `--reverse`, `--sort-buffer-size` (default ~2GB). **`rwuniq`** (binning + aggregation): `--fields`/`--values`/`--threshold FIELD=MIN[-MAX]`, time control (`--bin-time SEC`/`--nano-value-times`/`--timestamp-format`/`--epoch-time`), IP formatting (`--ip-format` 5-value enum `canonical`/`decimal`/`hex`/`any-cidr`/`force-ipv6`, `--integer-ips`/`--zero-pad-ips`), output format (`--no-titles`/`--no-columns`/`--column-separator`/`--delimited`). **`rwcat`** (concat + byte-order conversion): `--byte-order native|big|little`, `--ipv4-output`. **`rwcount`** (time-bin aggregation): `--bin-size SEC` (default 30), `--load-scheme` with 7-value enum (`start-time`/`end-time`/`middle`/`duration`/`time-proportional`/`minimum-volume`/`maximum-volume` — how to distribute multi-bin flows), `--start-time`/`--end-time`, `--skip-zeroes`. **`rwfileinfo`** (file-header introspection): `--fields`, `--summary`, `--no-titles`. **`rwgroup`** (flow grouping by key + delta): `--id-fields` (group keys), `--delta-field`/`--delta-value` (time-gap clustering), `--rec-threshold N`, `--objective`/`--summarize`. **Blacklist additions (8)**: all 8 rw* stems inserted into the `rw*` block — 5 between `rwbytype.d` and `rwho` (rwcat/rwcount/rwfileinfo/rwfilter/rwgroup) and 3 between `rwsnoop` and `rx` (rwsort/rwstats/rwuniq). Sort verified position-by-position: at index 2 the rw* block resolves as `b`<`c`<`f`<`g`<`h`<`s`<`u`; within the c-tied pair `rwcat`<`rwcount` (index 3 `a`<`o`); within the f-tied pair `rwfileinfo`<`rwfilter` (index 5 `e`<`t`); within the s-tied pair `rwsort`<`rwstats` (index 3 `o`<`t`). LC_ALL=C sort verified.
- **wodim (Debian's renamed cdrecord fork — CD/DVD-Recorder driver)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + an **upgraded round-116 grep using `^#compdef( |.* )${c}( |$)`** that tightens the word-boundary check per the round-133 false-positive lesson — `\<` was matching hyphenated containment like `pstops` inside `foo2zjs-pstops`; this round's pattern requires `pstops` to be either the first space-separated token after `#compdef ` or surrounded by spaces / end-of-line, eliminating the substring-in-hyphen-cluster failure mode). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/wodim/wodim.1](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/wodim/wodim.1.en.html). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (substantial — 11 already-covered + 5 stock-zsh dups)**: `cdrecord` at `src/_cdrecord` + stock zsh (Joerg Schilling's original upstream — `wodim` is Debian's renamed fork following the 2006 licensing dispute), `mkisofs`/`cdda2wav` at `src/`, `flac`/`metaflac` at `more_src/` (plus stock `_flac`), `mosh`/`mosh-server` at `more_src/` (plus stock `_mosh`), `eternal-terminal`/`et` (the latter caught via multi-stem `more_src/_eternal-terminal` `#compdef` line — a clean example of the round-116 grep working as intended); stock-zsh dups `growisofs`/`cdrdao`/`abcde`/`abcde`. Single-file completion `_wodim` covers Debian's renamed `cdrecord` fork — the actual CD/DVD-burner workhorse on Debian/Ubuntu systems. ~70 flags across 8 functional groups: meta `-version`/`-checkdrive`/`-inq`/`-scanbus`/`--devices`/`-prcap`/`-atip`/`-toc`/`-msinfo` (all `(- *)` mutex — quit-after-print); verbosity stackable `*-v` (write progress) + `*-V` (SCSI transport; `-VV` shows buffer content); **device + tuning `key=value` syntax** (uncommon `value` completion via `+-`): `dev=` (via `_wodim_devs` helper running `wodim --devices` + awk-extraction of `dev=` lines for live device discovery), `speed=N`, `blank=` (5-mode enum `all`/`fast`/`track`/`session`/`unclose`), `fs=BYTES`, `minbuf=PCT` (25..95% ATAPI wait), `gracetime`/`timeout SEC`, `padsize`, `driver=NAME` (advanced manual selection), `driveropts=` (comma-separated with 6-value seed `burnfree`/`noburnfree`/`varirec`/`gigarec`/`audiomaster`/`forcespeed`), `cuefile=*.cue`/`msifile=`/`textfile=`. **Track-format 5-flag mutex** `-audio`/`-data`/`-mode2`/`-xa`/`-xa1` (CD-DA 44.1kHz vs CD-ROM mode 1 2048-byte sector vs mode 2 2336-byte vs XA mode 2 form 1 with drive-headers vs XA with app-headers). **Write-mode 7-flag mutex** `-tao`/`-sao`/`-dao`/`-raw`/`-raw96r`/`-raw96p`/`-raw16` (track-at-once default + session-at-once + DAO alias + the 4 raw subchannel variants). **Fixation mutex** `-fix` ↔ `-nofix`. Behavior `-multi` (multi-session), `-dummy` (laser-off dry-run — saves a coaster), `-eject`, `-load`/`-lock`, `-noclose`, `-force` (disable safety checks), `-immed` (non-blocking SCSI). **Padding mutex** `-pad` ↔ `-nopad`. `-isosize`, `-swab` (byte-swap little-endian audio for the drive), `-useinfo`, `-text` (write CD-Text from `.inf`/CUE). **Copy-protection 3-flag mutex** `-copy` (unrestricted) ↔ `-nocopy` (single-personal-copy default) ↔ `-scms` (no copying). Misc `-clone` (readom raw image), `-format` (CD-RW/DVD-RW/DVD+RW format). Trailing repeatable positional `*:track file:_files -g "*.(wav|cdr|raw|iso|cue|mp3|flac)"` covers the 7 common burn-source formats. `wodim` already in `blacklist.txt`; no add needed.
- **psutils Round 2 — pstops + psselect + epsffit + extractres + includeres (5 binary stems via single multi-stem file, completes psutils coverage to 9)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/psutils/](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/psutils/) per-tool man pages (`pstops.1` + `psselect.1` + `epsffit.1` + `extractres.1` + `includeres.1`). **Tooling-bug callout discovered this round**: the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep returned a **false positive** on `pstops` because the existing `src/_foo2zjs-pstops` file declares `#compdef foo2zjs-pstops` and the regex `^#compdef.*\<pstops\>` matches `pstops` as a word inside that hyphenated identifier (zsh-style `\<` word-boundary treats `-` as non-word). Verified by inspecting the actual `#compdef` line; `_foo2zjs-pstops` does NOT cover the bare `pstops` binary, so it remains truly fresh and is included in this round. Lesson for future grep upgrades: the word-boundary regex needs tightening (e.g. `^#compdef([^a-zA-Z0-9_-]|.* )pstops([^a-zA-Z0-9_-]|$)`) to reject hyphenated containment. **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (5 already-covered)**: `psjoin` at `man_src/_psjoin`, `rootlesskit`/`slirp4netns`/`dvdauthor` all at `src/`, `enscript`/`genisoimage` ship in stock zsh at `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh/functions/`. Single multi-stem file `_pstops` is `#compdef pstops psselect epsffit extractres includeres`, dispatching on `$service` — companion to the round-132 `_psnup` multi-stem; **the two files together provide complete coverage of the 9 active psutils binaries** (psnup/psresize/psbook from round 132 + pstops/psselect/epsffit/extractres/includeres from this round + ps2pdf from round 132 as a Ghostscript wrapper). **`pstops`** (general page-by-page transform — the engine behind `psnup`'s n-up imposition): 6 flags + 3 positionals: `-q` (suppress page-number output), `-b` (prevent `bind` ops in PS prolog), `-w width`/`-h height`/`-p paper-name` (15-value enum from shared `_papers`), `-d lwidth` (draw border line, default 1pt); positionals 1 `page-spec` (e.g. `2:0(0,0)+1(0,0)` for the famous 2-up imposition spec), 2 `infile`, 3 `outfile`. **`psselect`** (page selector): 5 flags + 2 positionals: `-q`, **even/odd mutex** `-e` ↔ `-o`, `-r` (reverse output order), `-p pages` (e.g. `1,3-5,7` range expression). **`epsffit`** (EPS bounding-box fitter): 5 flags + 6 positionals: `-c` (centre image), `-r` (rotate 90° CCW), **aspect-vs-rotate mutex** `-a` (adjust aspect to fit, default preserve) ↔ `-m` (rotate-for-best-fit), `-s` (append `showpage` to force print); positionals 1..4 are the bounding-box coordinates `llx`/`lly`/`urx`/`ury` and 5..6 are `infile`/`outfile`. **`extractres`** (extract resources from a PostScript document): 1 flag `-m` (combine same-named resources into one file — needed for some font downloaders that emit fonts piece-by-piece). **`includeres`** (splice extracted resources back in): pure stdin → stdout filter with no documented flags — the completion returns `0` early so zsh just falls through to its default `_files` handling. All 5 stems already in `blacklist.txt`; no add needed.
- **PostScript transformation family — psnup + psresize + psbook + ps2pdf (4 binary stems via single multi-stem file)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/psutils/](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/psutils/) (`psnup.1` + `psresize.1` + `psbook.1`) plus [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/ghostscript/ps2pdf.1](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/ghostscript/ps2pdf.1.en.html). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (7 already-covered)**: `ps2eps` at `src/_ps2eps`, `multipath`/`iscsiadm`/`iscsid`/`tgt-admin`/`tgtadm` all at `src/`/`man_src/`/`more_src/`. Single multi-stem file `_psnup` is `#compdef psnup psresize psbook ps2pdf`, dispatching on `$service` — covers Angus Duggan's 3 most-used PostScript-transformation tools from psutils plus the Ghostscript `ps2pdf` wrapper. **Shared paper-size enum** across `psnup`/`psresize` via `_papers` array (15 values: `a0`/`a1`/`a2`/`a3`/`a4`/`a5`/`b5`/`letter`/`legal`/`tabloid`/`statement`/`executive`/`folio`/`quarto`/`10x14` — the canonical psutils paper menu interpolated into `-p`/`-P` enum lists). **`psnup`** (n-up imposition, 16 flags + repeatable input) — output paper `-w width`/`-h height`/`-p paper-name`, input paper `-W width`/`-H height`/`-P paper-name`, **rotation 3-flag mutex** `-l` (landscape, 90° CCW) ↔ `-r` (seascape, 90° CW) ↔ `-f` (swap w/h without rotation), `-c` (column-major layout, default row-major), margins `-m margin` (around entire output) vs `-b border` (around each input page), `-d lwidth` (draw border line, default 1pt), `-s scale` (manual scale override), `-i nup` (pages per sheet — same as the unusual `-N` bare-number form per upstream), `-q` (suppress page-number output); positional `*:postscript file:_files -g "*.(ps|eps)"`. **`psresize`** (rescale + paper-format change, 7 flags + 2 positionals) — output `-w`/`-h`/`-p paper-name`, input `-W`/`-H`/`-P paper-name`, `-q`; positionals 1 `infile` and 2 `outfile`. **`psbook`** (signature reordering for bookbinding, 2 flags + 2 positionals) — `-q` (suppress page-number output), `-s N` (signature size — must be a multiple of 4; enum seeded with `4 8 12 16 20 24 28 32` covering the practical book-binding range). **`ps2pdf`** (GhostScript wrapper) — upstream man page explicitly defers to `gs(1)` for the full option set; this completion models the 9 most-practitioner-useful Ghostscript flags: `-dPDFSETTINGS=` with 5-preset enum (`/screen`/`/ebook`/`/printer`/`/prepress`/`/default` — the standard quality-vs-size trade-off menu used in 99% of ps2pdf invocations), `-dCompatibilityLevel=` with 7-version PDF enum (`1.2`/`1.3`/`1.4`/`1.5`/`1.6`/`1.7`/`2.0`), font controls `-dEmbedAllFonts=true|false`/`-dSubsetFonts=true|false`/`-dCompressFonts=true|false`, page handling `-dAutoRotatePages=/None|/All|/PageByPage`, image-resolution trio `-dColorImageResolution=dpi`/`-dGrayImageResolution=dpi`/`-dMonoImageResolution=dpi`; positionals 1 input `.ps`/`.eps` and 2 optional output `.pdf` (stdout if omitted). All 4 stems already in `blacklist.txt`; no add needed.
- **CUPS print-management family — lpstat + lpq + lprm + lpoptions + lpadmin (5 binary stems via single multi-stem file)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream Apple/OpenPrinting CUPS man pages at [www.cups.org/doc/man-lpstat.html](https://www.cups.org/doc/man-lpstat.html) + `man-lpq.html`/`man-lprm.html`/`man-lpoptions.html`/`man-lpadmin.html`. **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (7 already-covered + 1 stock-zsh dup)**: `lp` ships in stock zsh at `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh/functions/_lp`, `lpc` already at `src/_lpc` (and multi-stem `src/_lpc.cups` `#compdef` line for the platform variant), `lpr` covered via multi-stem `src/_lpr-cups` `#compdef`; LaTeX-lint family `chktex`/`lacheck` at `src/`/`more_src/`; flow-analysis `cflow` at `more_src/`, `cscope` shipping stock zsh at `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh/functions/_cscope` (and `more_src/_cscope-indexer` multi-stem catches the wrapper variant). Single multi-stem file `_lpstat` is `#compdef lpstat lpq lprm lpoptions lpadmin`, dispatching on `$service` — covers the 5 user-facing CUPS print-management binaries. The family shares a common server-connection sub-set across all members: `-E` (force encryption to the CUPS server), `-h server[:port]` (alternate server via `_hosts`), `-U username` (alternate CUPS user via `_users`); beyond that each binary's flag set is distinct. **Live printer helper `_lp_printers`** runs `lpstat -p` and pipes through `awk '/^printer/ {print $2}'` to extract installed printer names for the `-d`/`-p`/`-P`/`-o`/`-v`/`-x` printer-target positionals — works against the local CUPS instance by default but follows `-h`/`-U` overrides via env propagation. **Per-stem coverage**: **`lpstat`** (18 flags) — print-system introspection covering jobs (`-o destination`, `-u user`, `-W completed|not-completed`, `-R` ranking), printers (`-p`/`-a`/`-v`/`-c`/`-l` long-listing), defaults (`-d`/`-e`/`-r` server-running/`-s` summary/`-t` everything), connection (`-E`/`-H`/`-h`/`-U`); **`lpq`** (8 flags) — queue status with `-P printer`, `-a` (all printers), `-l` (long format), trailing `+interval` continuous-polling syntax (e.g. `lpq +5` to refresh every 5 seconds), positional `*:job-id:`; **`lprm`** (6 flags) — job cancellation with `-P printer`, bare `-` (cancel all queued jobs), positional `*:job-id:` for selective removal; **`lpoptions`** (8 flags) — per-user option editing with `-d destination[/instance]` (set user default), `-p destination[/instance]` (set instance context), `-l` (list current options), repeatable `*-o name[=value]` (set option), `-r option` (remove option), `-x destination[/instance]` (clear all instance options); **`lpadmin`** (17 flags) — administrator-only printer setup with `-p destination` (configure named printer), `-x destination` (delete), `-c class`/`-r class` (class membership add/remove), `-d destination` (system default), `-v device-uri` (queue backend), `-m model` (PPD model), `-D info`/`-L location` (textual metadata), `-u expr` (user-level access policy), repeatable `*-o name=value` (PPD/job options) + repeatable `*-R name-default` (delete defaults), deprecated `-i FILE` (interface script) / `-P FILE` (`.ppd` glob). All 5 stems already in `blacklist.txt`; no add needed.
- **eksctl-anywhere (AWS EKS Anywhere CLI — on-premises Kubernetes)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Single-file completion `_eksctl-anywhere` covers the AWS EKS Anywhere CLI — manages on-premises Kubernetes clusters using the same APIs as Amazon EKS; supports vSphere/bare-metal-Tinkerbell/CloudStack/Snowball/Nutanix/Docker (dev-only) provider backends. The umbrella `eksctl` binary also exposes these via `eksctl anywhere <sub>`; this completion targets the standalone `eksctl-anywhere` form (already-covered `eksctl` at `man_src/_eksctl` handles the integrated case). 17 top-level subcommands via `_subcmds` describe: `apply`, `check-images`, `copy`, `create`, `delete`, `describe`, `download`, `exp`, `generate`, `get`, `help`, `import`, `install`, `list`, `renew`, `upgrade`, `version`. 2 shared persistent flags via `_global`: `-h/--help`, `-v/--verbosity 0..9` (numeric log-level enum). **`create`/`delete`/`upgrade` state machine**: target enum (`cluster`/`packages`/`hardware`/`support-bundle`). The `create cluster` leaf covers 14 flags including `-f/--filename FILE` (cluster YAML, `_files -g "*.(yaml|yml)"`), `-z/--hardware-csv FILE` (Tinkerbell hardware CSV), `--bundles-override FILE` (custom EKS-A release bundle manifest), `--kubeconfig FILE` (management cluster kubeconfig), `--install-packages FILE` (curated-packages config), `--tinkerbell-bootstrap-ip IP` (bootstrap-cluster Tinkerbell stack IP), 3 timeout overrides `--control-plane-wait-timeout DURATION` (default `1h0m0s`)/`--external-etcd-wait-timeout` (default `1h0m0s`)/`--per-machine-wait-timeout DURATION` (default `10m0s`), 2 deprecated timeouts `--node-startup-timeout`/`--unhealthy-machine-timeout`, `--no-timeouts` (disable all wait timeouts), `--skip-ip-check` (skip control-plane IP availability check), repeatable `*--skip-validations name` (bypass named create validation — useful for development clusters). **`generate` state machine**: 4-target enum (`clusterconfig`/`hardware`/`packages`/`support-bundle`). The `generate clusterconfig` leaf covers `-p/--provider` with the full 6-provider enum (`vsphere`/`tinkerbell`/`docker`/`snow`/`cloudstack`/`nutanix`) + cluster-name positional. **`exp` state machine** (experimental subcommands): 2-target enum (`validate`/`vsphere`). Remaining subcommands (`get`/`describe`/`list`/`install`/`import`/`apply`/`renew`/`check-images`/`copy`/`download`) fall through to generic positional handling — they have their own per-target sub-trees that need more docs to source-verify; deferred for a future round. `eksctl-anywhere` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 7151 between `eksctl` (7150) and `elan` (7151 → 7152) — sort verified shared `eksctl` prefix means `eksctl` (length 6) < `eksctl-anywhere` (length 15) by shorter-string-wins; at index 1 `eksctl-anywhere`'s 'k' (107) < `elan`'s 'l' (108). Single multi-stem file `_otfccdump` is `#compdef otfccdump otfccbuild`, dispatching on `$service` — covers Caryll's bidirectional OpenType font compiler used heavily in font-engineering workflows where you decompile binary OTF/TTF → JSON, patch font tables, then recompile JSON → OTF/TTF. **`otfccdump`** (decompile → JSON, 14 flags): meta `-h/--help`, `-v/--version`; output `-o FILE` (defaults to stdout, JSON glob); TTC sub-font selection `-n/--ttc-index N`; **JSON formatting mutex** `--pretty` ↔ `--ugly`; `--verbose`; content filters `--ignore-glyph-order`, `--glyph-name-prefix pfx`, `--ignore-hints`, `--decimal-cmap` (`cmap` keys as decimal numbers vs default hex), `--name-by-hash`; **BOM mutex** `--add-bom` ↔ `--no-bom`; input via `_files -g "*.(otf|ttf|ttc|otc)"` covering all 4 OpenType container forms. **`otfccbuild`** (compile JSON → OTF/TTF, 24 flags + 4-level optimization enum): meta `-h/--help`, `-v/--version`; output `-o FILE`; **4-level optimization mutex** `-O0` (off) ↔ `-O1` (default) ↔ `-O2` (aggressive web-font) ↔ `-O3` (most aggressive); `-s/--dummy-dsig` (empty DSIG table — needed for self-signing some Windows scenarios), `--verbose`, `--ignore-hints`; **preservation flags** `--keep-average-char-width` (preserve `OS/2.xAvgCharWidth`), `--keep-unicode-ranges` (preserve `OS/2.ulUnicodeRange`), `--keep-modified-time` (keep `head.modified` from JSON), `--short-post` (no glyph names in output); **glyph-order 3-flag mutex** `-i/--ignore-glyph-order` ↔ `-k/--keep-glyph-order` ↔ `--dont-ignore-glyph-order` (the last is an explicit alias for `--keep-glyph-order` — encoded so users get tab discovery of both spellings); **feature dedup mutex** `--merge-features` ↔ `--dont-merge-features`; **lookup dedup mutex** `--merge-lookups` ↔ `--dont-merge-lookups`; CFF-table tweaks `--force-cid` (name-keyed → CID-keyed conversion), `--subroutinize` (CFF table subroutinization for size); cmap `--stub-cmap4` (stub `cmap` format 4 subtable when format 12 is present, for legacy-tool compat); input via `_files -g "*.json"`. **Blacklist additions (2)**: `otfccbuild` and `otfccdump` inserted between `oterm` (18537) and `otfinfo` (18538) — sort verified at index 3 `otfcc*`'s 'c' (99) < `otfinfo`'s 'i' (105); at index 5 within the `otfcc*` block, `otfccbuild`'s 'b' (98) < `otfccdump`'s 'd' (100). Single-file completion `_dolphin-tool` covers the Wii/GameCube disc image toolkit shipped alongside the Dolphin emulator for headless format conversion + verification + extraction workflows (common in archival ROM-hacking pipelines). 4 subcommands via `_subcmds` describe: `convert` (transform between ISO/GCZ/WIA/RVZ + optional scrub + compress), `verify` (validate integrity + compute CRC32/MD5/SHA1/rchash digests), `header` (dump metadata: block size, compression details), `extract` (unpack files/partitions). **`convert`** (9 flags): `-u/--user DIR` (Dolphin user folder, auto-created), `-i/--input FILE`, `-o/--output FILE`, `-f/--format` (4-value enum `iso\|gcz\|wia\|rvz`, default `rvz`), `-s/--scrub` (junk-data scrubbing), `-b/--block_size N` (RVZ default `131072` = 128 KiB), `-c/--compression` (5-value enum `none\|zstd\|bzip2\|lzma\|lzma2`, RVZ default `zstd`), `-l/--compression_level N` (RVZ zstd default 5). **`verify`** (4 flags): `-u/--user`, `-i/--input`, `-a/--algorithm` (4-value enum `crc32\|md5\|sha1\|rchash`). **`header`** (6 flags): `-i/--input`, `-j/--json` (machine-readable; overrides individual print flags), `-b/--block_size`, `-c/--compression`, `-l/--compression_level` (each as a boolean toggle for selective display). **`extract`** (8 flags): `-i/--input`, `-o/--output DIR`, `-p/--partition PARTITION`, `-s/--single PATH` (single-file/directory mode), `-l/--list` (list contents, honours `--single`), `-q/--quiet`, `-g/--gameonly` (DATA partition only). Input file completion across all subcommands uses `_files -g "*.(iso|gcz|wia|rvz|wbfs|ciso)"` covering the 6 common Wii/GameCube container formats (ISO baseline, GCZ Dolphin-native, WIA WiiTime archive, RVZ Dolphin-next-gen, WBFS USB-loader, CISO Compressed-ISO). `dolphin-tool` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 6542 between `dolphin-emu` and `dolphin5` (sort verified position-by-position: at index 8 `dolphin-emu`'s 'e' (101) < `dolphin-tool`'s 't' (116); at index 7 `dolphin-tool`'s '-' (45) < `dolphin5`'s '5' (53)). Single-file completion `_pacseek` covers the interactive TUI for searching and installing Arch Linux packages — most navigation is keyboard-driven inside the TUI (ENTER/TAB/CTRL+S settings/CTRL+Q quit), config persisted at `~/.config/pacseek/config.json`, so the CLI surface is intentionally thin. 7 flags: meta `-h/--help`; repo filtering `-r REPOS` (comma-separated list, completes via `_values -s ,` with a static seed of 10 common Arch repos — `core`/`extra`/`multilib` + their `-testing` variants, plus `aur`/`chaotic-aur`/`eos`/`endeavouros-aur` for derivative-distro users); initial state `-s TERM` (initial search term), `-u` (show upgrades after startup), `-i` (show installed packages after startup); rendering `-a` (ASCII mode — no Unicode box-drawing, useful for serial consoles + Windows Terminal pre-fluent builds), `-m` (monochrome mode — no colours, useful for tmux-pipes / `script` recordings). The `-r REPOS` `_values -s ,` invocation is the canonical zsh pattern for comma-separated repeatable enums — lets users type `-r core,extra` and tab-complete each comma-segment independently from the same `_repos` array. `pacseek` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 18664 between `pacsearch` and `pacsift` (sort verified position-by-position: index 4 both share 'e' (101), so resolves at index 5 — `pacsearch`'s 'a' (97) < `pacseek`'s 'e' (101); and at index 4 `pacseek`'s 'e' (101) < `pacsift`'s 'i' (105)). - **FRR daemon family expansion — pbrd + ripngd (2 binary stems via single multi-stem file, fills out the FRR routing-daemon coverage to 11)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Common-flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream [docs.frrouting.org/en/latest/basic.html](https://docs.frrouting.org/en/latest/basic.html) plus per-daemon pages: [pbr.html](https://docs.frrouting.org/en/latest/pbr.html) and [ripngd.html](https://docs.frrouting.org/en/latest/ripngd.html) (both daemons explicitly defer to the common-options page — they ship no daemon-specific invocation flags). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (9 FRR daemons already-covered)**: `babeld`, `bgpd`, `eigrpd`, `isisd`, `ldpd`, `nhrpd`, `ospf6d`, `ospfd`, `pimd`, `ripd`, `staticd` — all already at `more_src/_*` (a remarkably-comprehensive FRR coverage already in the repo; this round just fills in the last 2 missing daemons). Single multi-stem file `_pbrd` is `#compdef pbrd ripngd`, dispatching on `$service` — both daemons share the FRR-common command-line flag set verbatim (per upstream both pages explicitly say "There are no $daemon-specific invocation options. Common options can be specified"). `pbrd` is FRR's Policy-Based Routing daemon (per-source/per-application routing decisions beyond destination-only matching); `ripngd` is FRR's RIPng (RIP for IPv6) routing daemon, the IPv6 sibling of `ripd`. **18 shared flags** (the FRR common-invocation set): meta `-h/--help`, `-v/--version`; daemonize `-d/--daemon`; config `-f/--config_file FILE`, `-i/--pid_file FILE`, `-z/--socket FILE` (zebra control socket); VTY `-A/--vty_addr ADDR`, `-P/--vty_port PORT`; identity `-u/--user USER` (via `_users`), `-g/--group GROUP` (via `_groups`); namespacing `-N/--pathspace NS` (per-instance config namespace), `-w/--vrfwnetns` (discover VRFs via Linux network namespaces — Linux-only feature), `-o/--vrfdefaultname NAME` (override "Default VRF" CLI display name); module loading `-M/--module module[:opts]` (FRR's pluggable module system — used for SNMP, etc); logging `--command-log-always` (permanent command logging), `--log dest` (initial destination — special `(stdout syslog)` enum plus `file:/path` form via `_alternative`), `--log-level` with 8-value enum (`emergencies`/`alerts`/`critical`/`errors`/`warnings`/`notifications`/`informational`/`debugging`); CLI features `--tcli` (transactional CLI mode); resource limits `--limit-fds N`. The `--log` flag uses `_alternative` to multiplex two surfaces — the bare special values `stdout`/`syslog` and the `file:/path` form via `_files` — matching upstream's `--log <stdout|syslog|file:/path/to/log/file>` syntax. **Blacklist additions (2)**: `pbrd` inserted between `pbr` (19043) and `pbs_iff` (19044) — sort verified shared `pbr` prefix means `pbr` (length 3) < `pbrd` (length 4) by shorter-string-wins, and `pbrd`'s `r` (114) < `pbs_iff`'s `s` (115) at index 2; `ripngd` inserted between `ripmime` (22257) and `rippkgs` (22258) — sort verified at index 3 `ripmime`'s 'm' (109) < `ripngd`'s 'n' (110) < `rippkgs`'s 'p' (112). - **rmlint (Christopher Pahl & Daniel Thomas's duplicate-and-lint finder)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/rmlint/rmlint.1](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/rmlint/rmlint.1.en.html). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (8 already-covered)**: round-124's deferred mkvtoolnix CLI family — `mkvmerge`/`mkvinfo`/`mkvextract`/`mkvpropedit` — all turned out to **already be covered** at individual `more_src/_mkv*` files (the earlier deferral was based on an incorrect "deferred for multi-stem fanout" call; the per-tool completions were already shipped). Round-124's `daemontools` deferral also resolved: `svc`/`svstat`/`svscan`/`supervise` all at `more_src/` (some catching via `_s6-svstat`/`_s6-svscan` multi-stem `#compdef` lines), plus `jdupes` at `more_src/_jdupes` and `exiv2` at `src/_exiv2`. Single-file completion `_rmlint` covers the duplicate-and-lint finder — locates duplicate files, empty files/dirs, broken symlinks, broken sUid/sGid bits, non-stripped binaries, and bad encodings; outputs a shell script that can be reviewed before running to actually delete the cruft (the "review-before-delete" workflow is rmlint's killer feature for safe dedup). ~58 flags grouped with 14 mutex sets: meta `-h/--help`, `-H/--show-man` (open full manpage), `--version` (shows compiled-feature list). **Output**: repeatable `*-T/--types` (CSV `+/-name` filter — e.g. `+duplicates,-emptyfiles`), repeatable `*-o/--output fmt:file` (custom format-to-file pairs), repeatable `*-O/--add-output fmt:file` (add without overwriting defaults), repeatable `*-c/--config key=value` (formatter knob). **Filters**: `-z/--perms RWX` (permission filter), `-s/--size RANGE` (e.g. `1K-100M`), `-d/--max-depth N`. **Hash algorithm enum (`-a/--algorithm`)** with 24 values covering the full upstream menu: blake2b/blake2bp/blake2s/blake2sp, sha3 family, sha256/sha512/sha1/md5, highway64/128/256, metro/metro256/metrocrc/metrocrc256, xxhash, murmur/murmur256, city/city256, cumulative, ext, paranoid. **Paranoia mutex** `-p/--paranoid` ↔ `-P/--less-paranoid`. **Verbosity mutex** stackable `-v/--loud` ↔ `-V/--quiet`. **Progress mutex** `-g/--progress` ↔ `-G/--no-progress`. **Color mutex** `-w/--with-color` ↔ `-W/--no-with-color`. **Hardlink mutex (3-flag)** `-l/--hardlinked` ↔ `-L/--no-hardlinked` + `--keep-hardlinked`. **Symlink mutex (3-flag exclusion)** `-f/--followlinks` ↔ `-F/--no-followlinks` ↔ `-@/--see-symlinks` (the last is rmlint's `@` trick: a single character flag, encoded literally so zsh doesn't choke on the `@`). **Crossdev mutex** `-x/--no-crossdev` ↔ `-X/--crossdev`. **Hidden mutex** `-r/--hidden` ↔ `-R/--no-hidden` + `--partial-hidden`. **Basename matching mutex** `-b/--match-basename` ↔ `-B/--unmatched-basename`. **Extension matching pair-mutex** `-e/--match-with-extension` ↔ `-E/--no-match-with-extension`, plus `-i/--match-without-extension` ↔ `-I/--no-match-without-extension`. **Time filtering**: `-n/--newer-than-stamp FILE` vs `-N/--newer-than TIME`. **Tagged-path semantics**: `-k/--keep-all-tagged` (preserve tagged), `-K/--keep-all-untagged` (preserve untagged), `-m/--must-match-tagged` (only dups in tagged), `-M/--must-match-untagged` (only dups in untagged), `-S/--rank-by` with 20-value enum (`m`/`a`/`c`/`M`/`A`/`C`/`l`/`L`/`p`/`P`/`x`/`X`/`h`/`H`/`o`/`O`/`d`/`D`/`r`/`R`). **Replay mode** `--replay FILE` (reprocess previous JSON output with new filters — the rmlint workflow lets you tweak filtering without re-hashing). **xattr caching** `-C/--xattr` (cache to xattrs) + sub-flags `--xattr-read`/`--xattr-write`/`--xattr-clear`. **Misc**: `-U/--write-unfinished`, `-t/--threads N`, `-u/--limit-mem SIZE`, `-q/--clamp-low N` and `-Q/--clamp-top N` (examine only a portion of each file from start/end — useful for fast video-prefix matching), `-Z/--mtime-window SECONDS`, `--with-fiemap`/`--without-fiemap`. Repeatable trailing positional `*:path:_files -/`. `rmlint` already in `blacklist.txt` at line 22312; no add needed.
- **sleepenh (Edrusb's high-precision drift-correcting sleep)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flags + positional shape transcribed directly from upstream [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/sleepenh/sleepenh.1](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/sleepenh/sleepenh.1.en.html). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (substantial — 17 already-covered + 2 deferred)**: Lua family hit `lua-language-server`/`fennel`/`hy`/`moonc`/`starlark`/`sky` (the last caught via `more_src/_endless-sky` multi-stem `#compdef` line, another nice round-116 grep win), `tectonic` at `more_src/_tectonic`, `arara`/`mtxrun` at `man_src/`, `tlmgr`/`texdoc` at `src/`; video family hit `HandBrakeCLI` at `more_src/_HandBrakeCLI`, `nq` at `more_src/_nq`; supervisor family hit `s6-svc`/`s6-svscan` at `more_src/`. Deferred: `mkvtoolnix` truly fresh but it's the GUI binary while the actual CLI tools are `mkvmerge`/`mkvinfo`/`mkvextract`/`mkvpropedit` which would need separate per-tool completion writes — left for a future multi-stem round; `daemontools` truly fresh but the actual binaries are `svc`/`svstat`/`svok`/`svscan`/`supervise` — same per-tool fan-out concern. Single-file completion `_sleepenh` covers the high-precision drift-correcting sleep utility — unlike `sleep(1)` which sleeps for a fixed duration, `sleepenh` aligns its wakeup to an absolute timestamp so chained invocations don't accumulate drift, ideal for periodic-task loops where you want exactly N seconds between wakes regardless of how long the work in between took. 3 flags + 2 positionals: meta `-h/--help`, `-V/--version`; `-w/--warp` (adjust returned timestamp so the next sleepenh call is guaranteed to actually sleep — useful when the previous iteration's work overran the budget); positional 1 `INITIALTIME` (defaults to now if omitted), positional 2 `TIMETOSLEEP` (seconds — the canonical use is `T=$(sleepenh $T 1.5)` in a Bash loop to maintain a 1.5-second period). `sleepenh` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 23780 between `sleep` and `slic3r` (sort verified position-by-position: shared `sleep` prefix means `sleep` (length 5) < `sleepenh` (length 8) by shorter-string-wins; at index 2 `sleepenh`'s 'e' (101) < `slic3r`'s 'i' (105)). LC_ALL=C sort verified.
- **gmsh (Christophe Geuzaine & Jean-François Remacle's 3D FEM mesh generator)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/gmsh/gmsh.1](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/gmsh/gmsh.1.en.html). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (8 already-covered)**: `ngspice` at `more_src/_ngspice`, `openscad`/`freecad` at `more_src/`, `maxima`/`sage`/`scilab` all at `more_src/` (with `maxima-jupyter` multi-stem catching `maxima` via `#compdef`), `dbus-send`/`dbus-monitor` already in blacklist but with no completion file — fresh write candidates but their CLI is mostly D-Bus IPL syntax (interface/method/signature mapping) which doesn't tab-complete cleanly against a static flag set, deferred. Single-file completion `_gmsh` covers the 3D finite-element mesh generator with built-in CAD engine and post-processor — drives both interactive GUI and headless batch meshing, used heavily in academic and industrial FEA workflows. ~40 flags grouped with 2 mutex sets: meta `-help`, `-version`, `-info`; control `-` (parse + exit), `-0` (output model + exit). **Mesh-dimension mutex** `-1` ↔ `-2` ↔ `-3` (1D/2D/3D mesh generation — only one active per invocation). Output: `-o FILE`, `-format` with 22-format enum (`msh`/`msh1`/`msh2`/`msh4`/`stl`/`vrml`/`unv`/`vtk`/`wrl`/`mesh`/`ply`/`ply2`/`bdf`/`cgns`/`med`/`inp`/`diff`/`key`/`x3d`/`ir3`/`mail`/`neu`/`su2`/`p3d`), `-bin` (binary when available), `-saveall` (discard physical groups). Algorithm tuning: `-algo` with 11-value enum (`meshadapt`/`del2d`/`front2d`/`delquad`/`pack`/`initial2d`/`auto`/`del3d`/`front3d`/`mmg3d`/`hxt`/`initial3d`), `-parametric`, `-part N` (partition mesh post-batch), `-smooth N`, `-order 1..5`, `-clscale FLOAT` (global element-size scale), `-clmin`/`-clmax` (size bounds), `-rand FLOAT` (random perturbation), `-bgm FILE` (background-mesh view), `-tol FLOAT` (geometrical tolerance), `-check` (consistency). **Mode-mutex** `-a` ↔ `-g` ↔ `-m` ↔ `-s` ↔ `-p` (automatic/geometry/mesh/solver/post-processing startup mode — 5-flag exclusion group). Display: `-n` (hide meshes/views on startup), `-fontsize`, `-display`. File ops: `-new` (new model before merge), `-merge`/`-open` (next files), `-pid` (PID to stdout), `-listen SOCKET`. Verbosity `-v 0..5,99` (99 = full debug). Scripting: `-nopopup`, repeatable `*-setnumber name value`, `*-setstring name value`, `*-string option`, `*-option FILE` (parse option file). Post-processing: `-combine` (merge views into multi-time-step). Batch convert: `-convert files` (latest formats + exit). Repeatable positional `*:geo/msh/stp/igs/iges/brep/stl file:_files -g "*.(geo|msh|stp|igs|iges|brep|stl|step|opt|pos)"` covers the 10 standard input extensions (geometry, mesh, STEP/IGES/BREP CAD, options, post). `gmsh` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 9545 between `gmplayer` and `gmt` (sort verified position-by-position: at index 2 `gmplayer`'s 'p' (112) < `gmsh`'s 's' (115) < `gmt`'s 't' (116)). - **clpeak (Krishnaraj Bhat's accelerator peak-throughput micro-benchmark)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Single-file completion `_clpeak` covers the single-binary accelerator peak-throughput micro-benchmark — probes OpenCL/Vulkan/CUDA/Metal back-ends and reports compute/memory/transfer peaks; widely used on Linux + macOS for tuning ML and crypto workloads. 25 flags grouped with 4 backend mutex pairs: meta `--help`, `--list-devices` (enumerate devices + exit). **Backend dispatch (4 mutex pairs)**: `--opencl` ↔ `--no-opencl`, `--vulkan` ↔ `--no-vulkan`, `--cuda` ↔ `--no-cuda`, `--metal` ↔ `--no-metal` — each encoded as a `(--flagA --flagB)` exclusion list so zsh suppresses the dominated half once the user picks one. **Test selection** (6 flags, no mutex — multiple kernels can run in one invocation): `--single-precision-compute` (SP-only compute), `--wmma` (CUDA tensor-core via hand-rolled WMMA), `--cublas` (CUDA vendor-SDK GEMM peak via cuBLASLt), `--simdgroup-matrix` (Apple matrix-engine), `--mps-gemm` (Apple vendor-SDK GEMM via MPS), `--coopmat` (Vulkan tensor-core via VK_KHR_cooperative_matrix). **Device selection** (5 flags — per-backend device index): `--cl-platform N` (OpenCL platform), `--cl-device N`, `--vk-device N` (Vulkan physical device), `--cuda-device N`, `--mtl-device N`. **Output routing** (4 flags): `--xml-file PATH`, `--json-file PATH`, `--csv-file PATH` (three machine-readable formats — can stack since each writes to its own file), `--compare FILE` (compare against baseline JSON via `_files -g "*.json"`). `clpeak` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 4033 between `clpbar` and `clush` (sort verified position-by-position: at index 3 `clpbar`'s 'b' (98) < `clpeak`'s 'e' (101); at index 2 `clpeak`'s 'p' (112) < `clush`'s 'u' (117)).
